RECIPE 1: Aam Papad Challi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Aam-Papad-Challi-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A zesty fusion of tangy aam papad and crunchy nuts, delivering a burst of sweet and sour flavors in every delightful bite. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Regular aam papad, Kala aam papad | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 0-5 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet &amp; Sour | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 corn on cob Oil for drizzling Butter for brushing
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder Black salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala + for sprinkling
  - 2 tablespoons lemon juice

METHOD:
  1. Peel corn on cob and roast directly on high flame.
  2. Heat a non-stick grill pan.
  3. Cut roasted corn on cob into 3 portions, halve and place on the hot pan.
  4. Drizzle some oil and toss well.
  5. Brush the corn pieces with some butter, add red chilli powder, black salt, chaat masala and lemon juice.
  6. Top with regular and kala aam papad pieces and cook till soft.
  7. Transfer into a serving bowl, sprinkle chaat masala and serve immediately.

RECIPE 2: Almond Milk Smoothie
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Almond-Milk-Smoothie-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Enriched with almonds and garnished with sabza and blueberries, this smoothie is a power house of essential nutrients.

Main Ingredients: Almonds, Ripe bananas | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Beverages | Prep Time: 6-7 hour | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup almonds, soaked overnight and drained
  - 2 medium ripe banana
  - 1 cup fresh blueberries + for garnish
  - 1 teaspoon vanilla essence
  - 3 tablespoons honey Fresh mint sprigs for garnish
  - 2 tbsps basil seeds (sabza), soaked

METHOD:
  1. Put soaked almonds in a grinder jar, add 2 cups warm water and grind till mixture is smooth.
  2. Line a strainer kept on a bowl with muslin cloth, pour the ground almond mixture into it and strain the almond milk into the bowl.
  3. Grind the residue again with 1 cup warm water to get more almond milk and strain this into the same bowl.
  4. Peel the bananas, break into half and put in the grinder jar.
  5. Add blueberries, vanilla essence, honey, almond milk and grind to a smooth mixture.
  6. Skew blueberries and a mint sprig on each skewer.
  7. Put some basil seeds in each serving glass and pour the smoothie over them.
  8. Place one skewer on each glass and serve immediately.

RECIPE 3: Almond Phirni
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Almond-Phirni-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

This recipe is specially for those who are intolerant to lactose, so almond milk is used instead of milk This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Almond milk, Rice | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 1-1.30 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 cups Almond milk
  - 30 minutes and drained a large pi to garnish Saffron
  - 1/2 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 3/4 cup Jaggery , chopped
  - 1/2 tablespoon Rose water to garnish Blanched pistachios , slivered

METHOD:
  1. Heat almond milk in a deep non-stick pan and let it come to a boil.
  2. Reduce heat and let it simmer for 8-10 minutes.
  3. Put rice in a blender jar, add ¼ cup water and blend to a coarse paste.
  4. Add this paste to almond milk and mix well.
  5. Add a large pinch of saffron and mix well and cook till the rice is cooked and the mixture thickens.
  6. Add green cardamom powder and mix well.
  7. Cook on low heat for 3-4 minutes, stirring constantly.
  8. Add jaggery and mix well.
  9. Cook till the jaggery is completely dissolved.
  10. Add rose water and mix well.
  11. Take the pan off the heat.
  12. Pour phirni into individual earthen bowls, sprinkle pistachio slivers on top and garnish with a few strands of saffron and serve chilled.

RECIPE 4: Aloo Masala Cheese Toast
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/aloo-masala-cheese-toast-7368492

Here, we’re giving a delicious makeover to leftover aloo sabzi with our easy recipe for 'Aloo Masala Cheese Toast.' So, follow our step-by-step guide to easily recreate it and enjoy a delightful toast at home!

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 5-6 minutes | Cook Time: 6-8 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 white bread slices
  - 1½ tablespoons tomato ketchup
  - 2 teaspoons chopped fresh parsley + to sprinkle Black sesame seeds to sprinkle

METHOD:
  1. Take leftover aloo sabzi in a bowl.
  2. Add mayonnaise, tomato ketchup and parsley and mix well.
  3. Preheat the oven at 180°C.
  4. Arrange the bread slices on baking tray and spread the potato mixture evenly.
  5. Sprinkle mixed cheese and bake in preheated oven for 6-8 minutes.
  6. Sprinkle black sesame seeds and parsley.
  7. Cut into halves and serve.

RECIPE 5: Aloo Muri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/aloo-muri-8699704

Satisfy your snack cravings with 'Aloo Muri', a beloved street-side delight from Meghalaya. This irresistible recipe features crispy puffed rice, spiced mashed potatoes, a special homemade masala, and a drizzle of tangy mustard oil.

Cuisine: Meghalaya | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 25-30 minutes | Cook Time: 6-8 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 medium potatoes (aloo), boiled and peeled
  - 4 cups puffed rice (muri)
  - 2 tablespoons coriander seeds
  - 1 tablespoon cumin seeds
  - 1 medium onion, chopped
  - 2 green chillies, chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder Black salt to taste Salt to taste ¼ cup tamarind water
  - 2-3 tablespoons mustard oil
  - 2-3 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves + to sprinkle ¼ cup aloo bhujiya + to sprinkle ½ lemon

METHOD:
  1. Heat a nonstick pan.
  2. Add coriander seeds, cumin seeds and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  3. Transfer in a mortar and crush to fine powder with a mortar.
  4. Take a bowl, cut the potatoes into medium sized pieces and add to the bowl.
  5. Add onion, green chillies, puffed rice, 2-3 tbsps ground spice mix, tamarind water, mustard oil and mix well.
  6. Add coriander and aloo bhujiya and mix well.
  7. Squeeze lemon and mix.
  8. Transfer in serving bowls, sprinkle coriander, aloo bhujiya and serve immediately.

RECIPE 6: Anjeer and Boondi Pancakes
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Anjeer-and-Boondi-Pancakes--Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A delectable fusion of traditional Indian flavors, featuring sweet figs and crunchy boondi, wrapped in a fluffy pancake for a delightful breakfast treat. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Dried figs, Sweet boondi | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 51-60 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8-10 dried figs, soaked and chopped ¼ cup sweet boondi
  - 1¾ cups milk
  - 15-20 walnuts Butter for shallow frying
  - 8 whole dried figs, soaked Rabri for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Take refined flour in a bowl, add baking soda and vanilla essence.
  2. Heat 1½ cups milk in a deep non-stick pan stirring continuously till the milk comes to a boil.
  3. Add jaggery, switch off heat and mix well till jaggery melts.
  4. Pour the milk mixture into the refined flour mixture.
  5. Add chopped figs, boondi and remaining milk.
  6. Add little water and mix well to make a medium thick and smooth batter.
  7. Chop and add walnuts and mix well.
  8. Set aside to rest for 10 minutes.
  9. Heat butter in a non-stick tawa, pour a ladle of batter and spread into a medium sized pancake.
  10. Place a whole fig in centre of and cook on medium heat for 2-3 minutes, turnover and cook on other side till golden brown on both sides.
  11. Transfer onto a serving plate and garnish with rabri.
  12. Serve immediately.

RECIPE 7: Anjeer aur Khajur Milkshake
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/anjeer-aur-khajur-milkshake-7094878

Healthy and delicious Milkshake made using #ProVfoods Anjeer aur Khajur is absolutely easy to make. Especially during hot summer, a glass full of this milkshake gives an instant boost of energy.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Beverages Prep time 6-8 hours | Cook Time: 0 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 10-15 Pro V Zahidi Whole Natural Dates (khajur)
  - 2 cups milk
  - 2-3 tablespoons honey Pro V Fusion Omega Boost Trail Mix to sprinkle

METHOD:
  1. Take Pro V Zahidi Whole Natural Dates in a bowl and deseed.
  2. Add sufficient water and soak for 6-8 hours.
  3. Take Pro V Select Figs in a bowl and deseed.
  4. Add sufficient water and soak for 6-8 hours.
  5. Drain the water from dates and figs and transfer in a blender jar.
  6. Add milk, honey and blend to fine mixture.
  7. Transfer in individual glasses and sprinkle Pro V Fusion Omega Boost Trail Mix on top.
  8. Serve.

RECIPE 8: Anjeer Toffee
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Anjeer-Toffee-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A healthy sweet made without the addition of sugar – ideal for growing children This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Dried figs (anjeer), Ghee | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 3.30-4 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2-3 hours and drained
  - 1 tbsp + for greasing Ghee
  - 4-5 Walnuts
  - 2 tablespoons Cashewnuts , chopped
  - 2 tablespoons Pistachios , chopped
  - 2 tablespoons Almonds , chopped
  - 1/2 cup Gum resin (gond) , fried

METHOD:
  1. Put the figs in a grinder jar, add a little water and grind to fine paste.
  2. Heat ghee in a deep non-stick pan and add fig paste and sauté on medium heat for 3-4 minutes.
  3. Add dates, mix well and cook for 10-15 minutes or till excess moisture dries up.
  4. Chop walnuts and add to the pan along with cashewnuts, pistachios and almonds.
  5. Mix well and cook till mixture begins to leave the sides of the pan.
  6. Add gond and mix well.
  7. Cook for 3-4 minutes on medium heat.
  8. Set aside in a bowl and allow to cool.
  9. Refrigerate for 30 minutes.
  10. Grease your palms with ghee and shape the mixture into oblong or any other desired shape.
  11. Take strips of parchment paper and place a toffee on each paper and roll them.
  12. Take coloured toffee sheets and roll the toffees again.
  13. Store the toffees in a glass jar or serve.

RECIPE 9: Arugula and Apple Salad
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/arugula-and-apple-salad-6595146

A peppery, distinctive-tasting green combined with apple slices and dressed with some sauces for a vibrant blend of flavors and textures makes up #ProVFoods special Arugula and Apple Salad! Give it a try to refresh your palate in a healthy style.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Salads Prep time 8-10 minutes | Cook Time: 0 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 red apple
  - 1 ½ tablespoons honey
  - 4 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil Crushed black peppercorns to taste Salt to taste Pro V Regal Jumbo Cranberries as required Pro V Lite Activated Pecan Nuts as required

METHOD:
  1. Cut red and green apple into quarters.
  2. Deseed and slice.
  3. Halve and slice English cucumber.
  4. Take ice cold water in a bowl.
  5. Add arugula leaves and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  6. Transfer in a salad rinser and drain excess water.
  7. Take mustard paste in a glass jar.
  8. Squeeze lemon, add honey, extra virgin olive oil, crushed black peppercorns and salt.
  9. Close the lid and shake well.
  10. Take cucumber in a bowl.
  11. Add green apple and red apple.
  12. Reserve some dressing and drizzle prepared dressing and mix well.
  13. Arrange some arugula leaves on a serving plate.
  14. Add some apple mixture on top.
  15. Sprinkle Pro V Lite Activated Pecan Nuts and Pro V Regal Jumbo Cranberries on top.
  16. Arrange remaining arugula leaves and apple mixture on top.
  17. Sprinkle some more Pro V Lite Activated Pecan Nuts and Pro V Regal Jumbo Cranberries on top.
  18. Drizzle remaining dressing and serve.

RECIPE 10: Avocado Toast
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/avocado-toast-6595184

Avocado toast gets a vibrant makeover with the addition of ProV’s Omega Boost Trail Mix. These nutrient-packed mixes are more than just toppings; they're a burst of flavor and nutrition.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 5-10 minutes | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 avocados ½ sourdough bread loaf
  - 4 tablespoons butter Cream cheese for applying Crushed black peppercorns to taste Salt to taste Pickled onion rings for garnish
  - 4 tablespoons ProV Healthy Seed Mix Micro greens for garnish Extra virgin olive oil for drizzling

METHOD:
  1. Cut the sourdough bread loaf into thick slices.
  2. Heat a cast iron pan.
  3. Add butter and let it melt.
  4. Place the sourdough slices on the pan and toast on both sides on low heat till golden and crisp.
  5. Take slices off the heat and arrange on a worktop.
  6. Cut the avocados in half, remove the seed, peel, and cut each half of the avocados into thin slices.
  7. Apply some cream cheese over one side of the toasted bread slices.
  8. Arrange the avocado slices over them and sprinkle crushed black peppercorns and salt.
  9. Garnish with pickled onion rings.
  10. Sprinkle ProV Healthy Seed Mix, garnish with micro greens, and drizzle extra virgin olive oil.
  11. Serve immediately.

RECIPE 11: Babycorn Paneer Drumsticks
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Babycorn-Paneer-Drumsticks--Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A savory symphony of textures and flavors, marrying the tender crunch of babycorn wrapped with creamy paneer and potato mixture, all rolled into one delicious bite. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Babycorn, Cottge cheese (paeer) | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8-10 baby corns
  - 1 cup grated cottage cheese (paneer)
  - 2 medium potatoes, boiled, peeled and grated
  - 1 small carrot, finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon chopped ginger
  - 1 teaspoon chopped garlic
  - 2-3 green chillies, chopped
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 1½ teaspoons soy sauce
  - 1 tablespoon refined flour (maida)
  - 1 tablespoon +
  - 2 red cherry tomatoes for garnish Spring onion flower for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Take paneer in a bowl, add potatoes, carrot, ginger, garlic, green chillies, onion, red chilli powder, garam masala powder, red chilli sauce and soy sauce and mix well.
  2. Add refined flour, 1 tablespoon cornflour and salt and mix well.
  3. Cover ¾ of each baby corn with the mixture to form drumsticks.
  4. Transfer in plate and add ½ cup cornflour and coat well.
  5. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai, slide in the baby corn drumsticks and deep fry on low heat till golden and crisp.
  6. Drain on absorbent paper.
  7. Sprinkle chaat masala.
  8. Arrange them on a serving platter, sprinkle some more chaat masala, garnish with red cherry tomatoes and spring onion flower.
  9. Serve hot with red chilli sauce.

RECIPE 12: Bajra Risotto
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Bajra-Risotto-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Healthy version of risotto – bajra is a good replacement for Arborio rice since it has a similar bite This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Pearl millet (bajra), Olive oil | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Main | Prep Time: 10-15 hours | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 12 hours, drained and cooked with v
  - 1/2 tablespoons butter
  - 1/2 medium onion , peeled
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 3-4 sprigs of fresh thyme Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1/2 tablespoons fresh cream Red chilli flakes to sprinkle Fresh parsley leaves to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat olive oil in a non-stick pan, add butter and let it melt.
  2. Finely chop onion and add to the pan, sauté till translucent.
  3. Add garlic and sauté well for 2 minutes.
  4. Add white wine, mix well and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  5. Add cooked bajra and mix well.
  6. Cook for 2-3 minutes.
  7. Add thyme sprigs and crushed black peppercorns and mix well.
  8. Grate parmesan cheese into the risotto and add fresh cream and mix well.
  9. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  10. Transfer into a serving bowl, sprinkle chilli flakes and crushed black peppercorns.
  11. Garnish with parsley and serve hot.

RECIPE 13: Baked Chocolate Apple
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Baked-Chocolate-Apple--Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Apples hollowed out, stuffed with fresh coconut and jaggery mixture, baked and served sprinkled with chocolate chips This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Red apples, Chocolate chips | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 medium Red apples to garnish Chocolate chips to sprinkle Sea salt

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 160º C.
  2. Slice the top and bottom of the apples and scoop out the flesh.
  3. Sprinkle sea salt and rub it uniformly inside the hollowed apples and place them on a baking tray.
  4. Chop the flesh.
  5. Heat a non-stick pan, add the chopped apple flesh and sauté till lightly cooked.
  6. Add coconut, mixed nuts and jaggery and mix well.
  7. Cook on low heat till jaggery melts.
  8. Switch off heat.
  9. Add green cardamom powder and cinnamon powder and mix well.
  10. Wipe the apples from inside with a tissue if they are moist from inside.
  11. Fill the nut mixture into each cored apple.
  12. Break half the caramel bars into small pieces and place on top, drizzle some rabdi.
  13. Repeat the process once more.
  14. Place the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 12-15 minutes.
  15. Spread remaining stuffing in deep serving plate and place the baked apples over it.
  16. Garnish with rabdi, chocolate chips and mixed nuts and serve immediately.

RECIPE 14: Banana Bread
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Banana-Bread.html

Savor the warmth of home baking in every slice of our Banana Bread – a comforting embrace of ripe bananas and nostalgia. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Ripe bananas, Almonds, Eggs | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 51-60 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Non Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium ripe bananas
  - 110 grams almonds, soaked overnight and peeled ¼ cup butter, cut into cubes ½ teaspoon cinnamon powder ½ teaspoon vanilla essence ½ tablespoon lemon juice
  - 2 eggs
  - 1 tablespoon flax seeds (alsi)
  - 1 tablespoon chocolate chips

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 110º C.
  2. Spread the almonds on one baking tray and bananas on another baking tray and place both the trays in the preheated oven and bake for 30 minutes.
  3. Remove them from the oven, increase the temperature to 200º C.
  4. Peel the bananas, put into a bowl and mash with a fork.
  5. Add butter and mix well, add cinnamon powder, vanilla essence, lemon juice, maple syrup, baking soda and salt.
  6. Add eggs and mix well until well combined.
  7. Put toasted almonds in a mixer jar, add flax seeds and grind into a fine powder.
  8. Add this powder to the banana and egg mixture and fold in gently.
  9. Pour the mixture into a silicon loaf mould, level the surface and sprinkle chocolate chips on top.
  10. Place the mould in the preheated oven and bake for 20-25 minutes.
  11. Check the bread by inserting a toothpick in the centre and if it comes out clean the bread is done.
  12. Remove the mould from the oven and let it cool.
  13. Slice the bread.
  14. Wrap the slices in Freshwrapp and pack it in the tiffin box.

RECIPE 15: Banana Walnut Chocolate Ice Cream
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Banana-Walnut-Chocolate-Ice-Cream-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

The combination of ripe bananas, walnuts and chocolate make for a super delicious ice cream that will win many a heart This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Ripe bananas, Walnuts | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 10-15 hour | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 medium Ripe bananas , peeled and frozen
  - 3/4 cup Walnuts
  - 4 tablespoons Unsweetened cocoa powder
  - 1/2 cup Fresh cream
  - 3 tablespoons Honey
  - 1 teaspoon Vanilla essence to garnish Ripe banana , peeled and coated with melted dark chocolate clove Sugar fondant to garnish Walnuts , crushed

METHOD:
  1. Cut each banana into 3 pieces and put in a grinder jar.
  2. Add cocoa powder, cream, honey, walnuts and vanilla essence and grind into a smooth mixture.
  3. Pour this mixture into an air tight container and put the lid on.
  4. Keep it in the freezer for 6-8 hours or overnight.
  5. Once set take the ice cream out of the freezer.
  6. Dip ice cream scooper in warm water and then scoop out 5 scoops of ice cream into a serving bowl.
  7. Skew the banana coated with melted dark chocolate onto a skewer and place it on the rim of the bowl.
  8. Use sugar fondant to create eyes and nose of a penguin.
  9. Garnish with crushed walnuts and serve immediately.

RECIPE 16: Barley Risotto
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Barley-Risotto-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Barley replaces Arborio rice in this risotto and the result is very tasty. Barley cooked with garlic , assorted mushrooms and served. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Barley (jau), Olive oil | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Main | Prep Time: 8-10 hours | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8 hours and cooked
  - 1 tablespoon olive oil
  - 1 tablespoon butter
  - 6-8 garlic cloves , chopped
  - 4-5 button mushrooms
  - 7-8 dried shiitake mushrooms , soaked, squeezed and sliced Salt to taste
  - 50 grams processed cheese Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1/2 cup fresh cream

METHOD:
  1. Heat olive oil and butter in a deep non-stick till butter melts.
  2. Add garlic and sauté well.
  3. Add onion, mix well and saute till translucent.
  4. Quarter button mushrooms and add to the onion mixture.
  5. Add white wine, mix well and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  6. Add shitake mushrooms and mix well.
  7. Cover and cook for 4-6 minutes.
  8. Add cooked barley and mix well.
  9. Add salt.
  10. Grate processed cheese directly into the barley mixture and mix well.
  11. Add crushed black peppercorns, mix well and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  12. Add fresh cream and mix well.
  13. Cook for 1 minute and take the pan off the heat.
  14. Transfer into a serving bowl, sprinkle crushed black peppercorns and serve hot.


========================================================================
RECIPE 17: Batata Puri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Batata-Puri-.html

Call them batata puri or sabudana vada, they are just as delicious This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Medium potatoes, Sago (sabudana) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 Medium potatoes medium, boiled and peeled
  - 1 cup Sago (sabudana) soaked
  - 1/2 cup Roasted peanuts crushed
  - 2 tablespoons Fresh coriander leaves chopped
  - 1 pinch Sugar to taste Rock salt (sendha namak)
  - 1 tablespoon Ginger-green chilli paste
  - 2 Banana leaves cut into medium squares to deep-fry Oil to serve Coconut chutney

METHOD:
  1. Take sago in a bowl add sago, add peanuts, coriander leaves, sugar, rock salt, ginger green chilli paste and lemon juice.
  2. Mash and add potatoes and mix well.
  3. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  4. Divide the mixture into equal portions.
  5. Place a banana leaf square on the worktop, apply little oil on it, place a portion of potato mixture, gently press and flatten slightly.
  6. Slide into hot oil and deep-fry, turning sides, till golden brown on both sides.
  7. Drain on absorbent paper.
  8. Arrange the puris on a serving plate and serve hot with coconut chutney.

RECIPE 18: Bathue ka Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Bathue-ka-Parantha-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Bathua leaves kneaded with whole wheat flour, rolled into paranthas and cooked This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Bathua leaves , Whole wheat flour | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups for dusting Whole wheat flour
  - 2-3 Green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Ginger , finely chopped
  - 1/2 tsp + to sprinkle Red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1 medium Onion , chopped as required Ghee to sprinkle Chaat masala to serve White butter to serve Yogurt to serve Pickle

METHOD:
  1. Roughly chop bathua leaves and transfer into a bowl.
  2. Add carom seeds, green chillies, ginger, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, wheat flour and onion and mix well.
  3. Add water as required and knead to a soft dough.
  4. Divide the dough into equal portions and roll out into large rotis on a dusted worktop.
  5. Apply some ghee on the rotis, dust some flour and sprinkle chilli powder and chaat masala on top.
  6. Fold into a square and roll out into paranthas.
  7. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  8. Place the parathas on it, one at a time, and cook, basting with ghee, till evenly golden brown on both the sides.
  9. Place them on individual serving plates and serve hot with white butter, yogurt and pickle of your choice.

RECIPE 19: Beetroot Browines
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Beetroot-Browines.html

These extremely healthy and dark pink brownies are simply irresistible This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Boiled beetroot puree, Butter | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Boiled beetroot puree for greasing Butter
  - 1 Ripe banana , roasted
  - 3/4 cup Honey
  - 3/4 cup Coconut oil
  - 1 cup Rice flour
  - 3/4 cup Cocoa powder
  - 1 pinch Salt
  - 1 teaspoon Baking powder
  - 1/2 cup Walnuts , chopped

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 200º C.
  2. Grease a square baking tin with butter and line it with butter paper.
  3. Take flax seed powder in a large bowl, add 9 tablespoons water and mix well, set aside for 5 minutes.
  4. Peel the roasted banana and mash it with a fork.
  5. Add the banana to the flax seed mixture.
  6. Add beetroot puree and mix well.
  7. Add honey and coconut oil and whisk till well combined.
  8. Sift rice flour into the beetroot mixture and fold in gently.
  9. Sift cocoa powder into the beetroot mixture and fold in again.
  10. Add salt, baking powder and walnuts and mix well.
  11. Pour the batter into the prepared cake tin, keep it in the preheated oven and bake for 20-25 minutes.
  12. Remove the tin from the oven and let it cool.
  13. Cut it into squares and pack it in the tiffin.

RECIPE 20: Beetroot Coconut Barfi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Beetroot-Coconut-Barfi-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

These beautiful ruby red barfis are so tasty that they will get consumed in a jiffy This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Beetroot, Fresh coconut | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium Beetroot , peeled and grated
  - 2 cups Fresh coconut , scraped
  - 1 tbsp _ for greasing Ghee
  - 1 cup Sugar
  - 1/2 cup Fresh cream to garnish Walnuts
  - 3 tablespoons Powdered sugar
  - 1/2 teaspoon Green cardamom powder

METHOD:
  1. Grease a barfi tray with some ghee.
  2. Heat ghee in a deep non-stick pan, add sugar, coconut and cream and mix well.
  3. Cook on medium heat, stirring continuously, for 15-20 minutes.
  4. Meanwhile roughly chop walnuts.
  5. When mixture begins to leave the pan, add the beetroot and mix well.
  6. Add powdered sugar and green cardamom powder, mix well and cook on medium heat for 2-3 minutes.
  7. Transfer the barfi mixture in the greased tray and spread it evenly.
  8. Sprinkle walnuts on top.
  9. Set aside till set and cooled down to room temperature.
  10. Cut into rectangular barfis.
  11. Insert a coloured ice cream stick in each barfi, arrange them on a serving platter and serve immediately.

RECIPE 21: Beetroot Quinoa Pachadi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/beetroot-quinoa-pachadi-7076695

Popular South Indian accompaniment made with all super foods. Watch this video to find out how to make this recipe. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: South Indian | Course: Accompaniments Prep time 20-25 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3-4 tablespoons beetroot puree ¼ cup quinoa
  - 1 cup yogurt Salt to taste ½ tablespoon +
  - 1 teaspoons oil ¼ cup scraped fresh coconut
  - 4-5 curry leaves

METHOD:
  1. Heat a small deep non-stick pan.
  2. Add quinoa, 1 cup water and salt and mix.
  3. Add 1 teaspoon oil, mix and bring the mixture to boil.
  4. Cover and cook till quinoa is done.
  5. Transfer in a bowl and refrigerate it.
  6. Coarsely grind together coconut, green chillies and ginger.
  7. Take yogurt in another bowl and whisk.
  8. Add ground coconut mixture and whisk.
  9. Add beetroot puree and whisk well.
  10. Add salt to yogurt mixture and whisk.
  11. Add cooked quinoa and whisk well.
  12. Transfer on a shallow serving plate.
  13. To prepare tempering, heat remaining oil in a tempering pan.
  14. Roughly cut dried red chillies using a pair of scissors.
  15. Add mustard seeds to hot oil and let it sputter.
  16. Add curry leaves and let it crackle.
  17. Add dried red chillies and swirl the pan for few seconds.
  18. Pour the tempering over the beetroot yogurt mixture and serve.

RECIPE 22: Bhakri Pizza
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Bhakri-Pizza-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A creative fusion dish that combines the rustic charm of traditional Indian bhakri with the flavorful toppings of a classic pizza, offering a unique culinary experience. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Readymade pearl millet (bajra) dough, Pearl millet (bajra) flour | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 teaspoon oil ½ teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 teaspoon chopped garlic
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped
  - 2 medium tomatoes, blanched, peeled and pureed ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder Salt to taste Grated mozzarella cheese as required
  - 1 medium red capsicum, cut into triangles
  - 1 medium green capsicum, cut into triangles ½ cup boiled corn kernels Cheese sauce as required Halved black olives for garnish Black olive slices for garnish

METHOD:
  1. To prepare pizza sauce, heat oil in a non-stick pan, add cumin seeds and garlic and mix well.
  2. Add onion, mix and sauté till translucent.
  3. Add tomato puree, turmeric powder, red chilli powder and salt and mix well.
  4. Sauté till oil separates.
  5. Sprinkle bajra flour on worktop, keep the dough on it and roll into a thick disc.
  6. Heat a non-stick tawa and place the disc on it and cook for 3-4 minutes.
  7. Flip and cook on other side till golden brown specs appear.
  8. While the bhakri is still on the pan, spread a spoonful of pizza sauce on it, sprinkle mozzarella cheese in the centre, sprinkle red and green capsicum triangles, boiled corn kernels on top.
  9. Cover and cook on low heat till cheese melts completely.
  10. Transfer the pizza on a serving plate.
  11. Put cheese sauce in a piping bag and pipe out cheese sauce on top of pizza in the shape of spider web.
  12. Place a halved black olive in centre.
  13. Place 6 halved olives around.
  14. Now place black olive slices as legs of the spider.
  15. Serve hot.

RECIPE 23: Bhakri with Thecha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Bhakri-with-Thecha-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Typical rural meal of Maharashtra – it is so very tasty that you will want to eat it again and again This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Bhakri, Finger millet (nachni/ragi) flour | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup + for dusting Finger millet (nachni/ragi) flour to taste Salt Thecha
  - 3 tablespoons Oil
  - 10-
  - 10-12 Light green chilliess to taste Sea salt
  - 1/4 cup Roasted peanuts

METHOD:
  1. To make bhakri, heat sufficient water in an earthen pot, and let it come to a boil.
  2. Take ragi flour in a large bowl, add salt and mix well.
  3. Pour the hot water little at a time, mix well till it forms soft dough.
  4. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape each into a ball.
  5. Dust each ball with ragi flour, flatten it and roll into a thin disc.
  6. Heat an earthen tawa, place the discs on it, one at a time, and cook, turning sides, till small brown specks appear on both sides.
  7. Take it off the heat and keep under a muslin cloth.
  8. To make thecha, heat oil in another earthen pot, add garlic, dark green chillies, light green chillies and sea salt and sauté well.
  9. Cover and cook for 12-15 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  10. Remove the lid and add roasted peanuts, adjust salt and sauté well.
  11. Cook for 2-3 minutes and take it off the heat.
  12. Cool the mixture, transfer into a mortar pestle and pound it coarsely.
  13. Arrange the bhakris on a serving platter and transfer thecha into a bowl and serve the two together.

RECIPE 24: Bhindi Hara Masala
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Bhindi-Hara-Masala-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Bursting with flavour this bhindi dish is so very irresistible. Ladyfingers cooked with a green masala and Indian spices. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Ladyfingers (bhindi), Oil | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 inch pieces
  - 1 inch ginger , cut into strips + to garnish
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 2-3 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 2 small onions , finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1/2 teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur) Salt to taste
  - 2 medium tomatoes
  - 1 green chilli , slit Yellow capsicum strips to garnish Red capsicum strips to garnish Hara masala
  - 1 cup fresh coriander leaves
  - 1/2 cup fresh mint leaves
  - 1/4 cup scraped fresh coconut
  - 1 inch ginger

METHOD:
  1. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai and deep-fry the ladyfinger pieces till crisp.
  2. Drain on absorbent paper.
  3. To make hara masala, put coriander leaves, mint leaves, coconut, green chillies and ginger in a grinder jar and grind to a coarse paste.
  4. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a non-stick pan, add ginger, cumin seeds and green chillies and sauté till fragrant.
  5. Add garlic, mix and sauté till it turns brown.
  6. Add onions, mix and sauté till translucent.
  7. Add the fried ladyfingers, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, dried mango powder and salt, mix and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  8. Add hara masala and mix well.
  9. Roughly chop tomatoes, add to the pan and cook till they turn soft and pulpy.
  10. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with ginger strips, slit green chilli, yellow and red capsicum strips and serve hot.

RECIPE 25: Bhindi Methi Bhurjee
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Bhindi-Methi-Bhurjee-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Bhindi and methi make odd couple but in this dish they are simply very compatible. Ladyfingers and fenugreek leaves cooked with Indian spices. Best served with hot phulkas. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Ladyfinges (bhindi), Fresh fenugreek leaves (methi) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 250 grams ladyfinges (bhindi) , finely chopped
  - 1 large bunch fresh fenugreek leaves (methi) , chopped
  - 3 tablespoons oil
  - 2-3 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon ginger , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon garlic , finely chopped
  - 2 medium onions , finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 tablespoon coriander powder
  - 1/2 teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur) Salt to taste
  - 1 medium tomato , finely chopped Fresh coriander sprigs to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat rice bran oil in a non-stick pan, add green chillies, ginger and garlic and sauté till fragrant.
  2. Add onions, mix and sauté till translucent.
  3. Add ladyfingers, mix and cook for 8-10 minutes.
  4. Add red chilli powder, turmeric powder, coriander powder, garam masala powder, dried mango powder and salt.
  5. Mix well and cook for 4-5 minutes.
  6. Add fenugreek leaves and tomato, mix and cook till the tomatoes turn soft and pulpy.
  7. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with coriander sprigs and serve hot.

RECIPE 26: Biscuit Ice Cream Chocolate Bars
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Biscuit-Ice-Cream-Chocolate-Bars-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Icecream bar covered with glucose biscuits, frozen and served drizzled with melted chocolate and nuts Icecream bar covered with glucose biscuits, frozen and served drizzled with melted chocolate and nuts This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Glucose biscuits, Vanilla ice cream bar | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 litres Vanilla ice cream bar
  - 1 cup Dark chocolate , melted to garnish Pistachios , finely chopped to garnish Vermicelli sprinklers to garnish Almonds , chopped

METHOD:
  1. Stick half the glucose biscuits on the edge of one aide of the ice cream bar.
  2. Trim the exposed portion of the bar and turn it sideways so that biscuit portion is on one side.
  3. Now halve the bar from middle lengthwise and stick the remaining biscuits on the cut side.
  4. Transfer the bar on an aluminium sheet and cover it completely.
  5. Freeze for 1-2 hours.
  6. Further cut into smaller bars.
  7. Insert an ice cream stick in centre of each bar.
  8. Take melted dark chocolate in a bowl.
  9. Pour melted dark chocolate on each bar with a spoon.
  10. Drip off extra chocolate.
  11. Sprinkle pistachio, vermicelli sprinkles and almonds on each bar.
  12. Place them on a silicon mat and refrigerate for 5 minutes.
  13. Remove from refrigerator and transfer onto a serving platter and serve immediately.

RECIPE 27: Black Grapes Shikanji
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/black-grapes-shikanji-7579908

A refreshing and tangy black grape shikanji with a burst of spices, perfect for a chilled, revitalizing drink! This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Beverages Prep time 35-40 minutes | Cook Time: 6-8 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 25-30 black grapes + for garnish ¼ cup sugar ¼ teaspoon salt A pinch of red chilli powder ¼ teaspoon roasted cumin powder A pinch of chaat masala Lemon wedges as required Pink salt as required Ice cubes as required Lemon slices as required Grape slices as required Mint sprigs as required Drinking soda as required

METHOD:
  1. Transfer black grapes in a blender jar.

  3. Heat a nonstick pan and strain the puree through a fine sieve.
  4. Cook till the mixture thickens.

  7. Allow to cool.
  8. Apply lemon on rim the glass and press pink salt on it.

  10. Add mint sprigs and pour a portion of prepared syrup.

RECIPE 28: Broccoli & Cheese Soup
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Broccoli-Cheese-Soup-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood

This velvety concoction combines the wholesome goodness of tender broccoli florets with the rich, creamy allure of melted cheese, creating a symphony of flavors. This soup gets done easily and quickly with no compromise in its taste.

Main Ingredients: Broccoli, Bocconcini, | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Soups | Prep Time: 5-10 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium broccoli
  - 8-12 small pieces of bocconcini
  - 3 tablespoons butter
  - 1 medium onion
  - 8-10 garlic cloves
  - 6 cups vegetable stock Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1 cup milk
  - 2 teaspoons olive oil Slices of bread to serve Parsley sprig for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Separate small florets from broccoli and discard their stems.
  2. Put butter in a soup maker.
  3. Roughly chop onion and add.
  4. Add garlic cloves, broccoli florets, vegetable stock, salt and crushed black peppercorns and cover with the lid.
  5. Select the desired option and let it cook for 4-6 minutes.
  6. Remove the lid and add milk, cover with lid, select the option and cook till the soup is done.
  7. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, keep the bread slices in it and cook, turning sides, till crisp on both sides.
  8. Keep them on a plate.
  9. Place 2-3 bocconcini pieces at the bottom of each serving bowl and pour the soup over.

RECIPE 29: Broccoli Mac and Cheese
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Broccoli-Mac-and-Cheese-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Main Ingredients: Broccoli, Cheese | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Main | Prep Time: 8-10 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium broccoli Salt to taste
  - 4 tablespoons butter
  - 1 tablespoon whole wheat flour
  - 2 cups milk
  - 50 grams processed cheese Crushed black peppercorns to taste A pinch of dried mixed herbs Red chilli flakes to sprinkle

METHOD:

  2. Cut small florets of broccoli.

RECIPE 30: Burnt Garlic Vegetable Fried Rice
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/-Burnt-Garlic-Vegetable-Fried-Rice.html

Rice tossed with fresh cut vegetables and burnt garlic This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

INGREDIENTS:
  - 15-20 minutes
  - 10-
  - 5-6 French beans
  - 1/4 medium Cabbage
  - 1 stalk Spring onion greens to taste Salt
  - 1 tablespoon Oil
  - 1 teaspoon Soy sauce
  - 1 teaspoon Vinegar

METHOD:

RECIPE 31: Caramel Walnut Fudge

  - 4 tbsps + for drizzling Caramel syrup
  - 1/4 cup Walnuts , chopped
  - 1 tbsp + to grease Ghee
  - 2 tablespoons Butter
  - 1/2 cup Khoya , grated
  - 1 cup Condensed milk
  - 100 grams Dark chocolate , chopped

RECIPE 33: Chaat Quiche
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chaat-Quiche-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A fusion delight combining the flaky goodness of quiche with the tangy, spicy flavors of Indian chaat, perfect for a unique and satisfying snack or appetizer. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Soya bean flour, dried white peas (matara) | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2½ cups soya bean flour Salt to taste
  - 4 tablespoons ghee
  - 1 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 1 cup black eyed beans (lobia) Filling
  - 1 cup yogurt Salt to taste A pinch of black salt ½ teaspoon chaat masala
  - 2 tablespoons powdered sugar ¼ cup roasted peanuts, peeled
  - 1 cup dried white peas (matara), soaked overnight, boiled with salt and turmeric powder
  - 2 medium sweet potatoes, boiled, peeled and cut into ½ inch cubes
  - 1 medium carrot, peeled and grated
  - 1 medium beetroot, peeled and grated Chaat masala to sprinkle Tamarind chutney to drizzle Green chutney to drizzle Nylon sev for garnish Blanched carrot, cut into star shaped pieces for garnish Blanched beetroot, cut into star shaped pieces for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Preheat the oven to 180˚C.
  2. To prepare short crust dough, take soyabean flour in a bowl.
  3. Add salt, ghee and mix well.
  4. Add carom seeds.
  5. Add little water and knead to semi soft dough.
  6. Divide the dough into equal portions, place each on the worktop and roll into a thick disc.
  7. Place it in a quiche mould and press lightly on all sides.
  8. Trim the edges which are bulging out of the mould.
  9. Spread a parchment paper on it and spread black eyed beans over the paper.
  10. Place the mould in the preheated oven and blind bake for 12-15 minutes.
  11. Take yogurt, salt, black salt, chaat masala and powdered sugar in a bowl.
  12. Mix well and set aside.
  13. Lightly crush roasted peanuts and set aside in another bowl.
  14. Remove quiche mould from the oven and allow it to cool down completely.
  15. Unmould the quiche base from the mould.
  16. Spread boiled matara evenly over it.
  17. Add sweet potato cubes, grated carrot and beetroot.
  18. Sprinkle chaat masala and crushed peanuts.
  19. Pour the yogurt mixture on top and cover the filling completely.
  20. Drizzle tamarind chutney and green chutney.
  21. Sprinkle nylon sev, garnish with carrot and beetroot stars and serve.

RECIPE 34: Chakna Platter
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chakna-Platter---SK-Khazana.html

An assortment of spicy and crunchy snacks commonly enjoyed with drinks in India, featuring items like peanuts, fried lentils, chickpea flour noodles (sev), and seasoned nuts or seeds. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Masala peanuts, Unsalted roasted peanuts | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup salted roasted peanuts ½ teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon black salt Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala Oil for deep-frying Wasabi Makhana
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 2 cups puffed lotus seeds (makhana)
  - 1 papad
  - 2 cups chana, boiled
  - 1 tomato, finely chopped
  - 1 green chilli, finely chopped ½ teaspoon black salt
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon chopped coriander Juice of half lemon Sev for garnish Coriander leaves for garnish Cheesy Nuts
  - 1 cup cashews, whole
  - 1 cup almonds, whole ¼ cup cheese powder ½ teaspoon black salt Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala Cheeseling Bhel
  - 2 cups cheeseling
  - 1 medium tomato, finely chopped
  - 1 ½ teaspoon chaat masala
  - 1 tablespoon chopped coriander ¼ cup sev Schezwan Chakli
  - 1 cup rice flour ¼ cup split skinless black gram (dhuli urad dal), ground
  - 4 teaspoons Schezwan sauce ¼ teaspoon cumin powder ¼ teaspoon red chilli powder Salt to taste Oil for deep frying and greasing

METHOD:
  1. Masala Peanuts Heat sufficient oil in a kadai and deep-fry the peanuts till golden brown.
  2. Transfer to a bowl.
  3. In a separate bowl add chilli powder, black salt, salt to taste, chaat masala and prepare a masala for the peanuts.
  4. Mix the prepared masala in the peanuts well, transfer to a cutting glass filled till top and serve.
  5. Wasabi Makhana Heat oil in a non-stick pan and add the makhana, toss for 2-3 minutes.
  6. Add wasabi powder and toss again.
  7. Transfer to a cutting glass, filled till top and serve.
  8. Masala Papad Heat a non-stick tawa.
  9. Cut the papad into half and roast on the heated tawa until cooked.
  10. Fold into a cone, once cooked.
  11. Add boiled chana, onion, tomato, green chilli, black salt, chaat masala, salt to taste, chopped coriander and lemon juice in a bowl and mix well.
  12. Fill this mixture in the prepared papad cones.
  13. Garnish with sev and coriander leaves, place the cones in a cutting glass and serve.
  14. Cheesy Nuts Heat sufficient oil in a kadai and deep-fry the cashews and almonds till golden.
  15. Drain on an absorbent paper and transfer to a bowl.
  16. Add cheese powder, black salt, salt to taste and chaat masala and mix well.
  17. Transfer to a cutting glass filled till top and serve.
  18. Cheeseling Bhel Add cheeselings, tomatoes, onion, raw mango, black salt, salt, lemon juice and chaat masala in a bowl and mix well together.
  19. Add chopped coriander and sev.
  20. Transfer to a cutting glass filled till top and serve.
  21. Schezwan Chakli Add rice flour, ground split skinless black gram (urad dal aata), schezwan sauce, salt to taste, cumin seeds, chilli powder and some water in a bowl.
  22. Knead it to make soft dough.
  23. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  24. Grease the chakli press with some oil.
  25. Put some dough, at a time, in a chakli press and press out chaklis in strips directly in the oil.
  26. Deep-fry on medium heat till crisp.
  27. Drain on absorbent paper and cool down to room temperature.
  28. Serve in a cutting glass.

RECIPE 35: Chana Cheese Roti Turnover
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chana-Cheese-Roti-Turnover-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A delightful fusion of Indian and Western cuisines, featuring a savory turnover made with roti crust filled with a hearty mixture of spiced chickpeas and cheese. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Chickpeas (kabuli chane), whole wheat tortillas or rotis | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups chickpeas (kabuli chane), soaked overnight, drained and boiled with salt and drained
  - 2-3 tablespoons oil + to drizzle
  - 1 tablespoon grated ginger
  - 1 large onion, finely chopped
  - 1½ tablespoons coriander powder Salt to taste ½ bunch fresh coriander leaves
  - 4 whole wheat tortillas or rotis Chana jor garam as required Cheese cubes as required Ginger strips for garnish Fresh mint sprigs for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add ginger and sauté till raw flavour goes away.
  2. Add onion and sauté till it turns golden brown.
  3. Add capsicum and sauté for 1 minute.
  4. Add chickpeas, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, coriander powder and salt.
  5. Mix well.
  6. Crush the chickpeas slightly with a masher.
  7. Transfer the mixture into a bowl.
  8. Chop coriander leaves and add to the chickpea mixture and mix well.
  9. Allow the mixture to cool down.
  10. Keep each roti on the worktop, place some mixture on one side, place chana jor garam and cheese cubes on top.
  11. Fold the roti into half.
  12. Heat a non-stick tawa, place the folded rotis on it, drizzle some oil all around and cook on medium heat till the underside becomes crisp.
  13. Turnover and cook till the other side becomes evenly golden and the cheese melts.
  14. Cut into half and transfer on a serving plate.
  15. Sprinkle some red chilli powder, crush some chana jor garam and sprinkle on top.
  16. Serve hot, garnished with ginger strips and mint sprigs.

RECIPE 36: Cheese Kurkure
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Cheese-Kurkure.html

Got guests coming over for Diwali? This recipe will come in handy. Mozzarella and cheddar cheese stuffed rolls deep-fried till the outside is crisp and the cheese inside has melted. These are a definite hit at any party, especially with kids! This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Mozzarella cheese, Processed cheese | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 tablespoons grated mozzarella cheese
  - 30 grams processed cheese, cut into ½ cm small cubes
  - 1 cup +
  - 1 tablespoon refined flour + for coating Salt to taste ¼ teaspoon baking soda
  - 2 tablespoons yogurt
  - 1 tablespoon oil + for deep-frying
  - 1 teaspoon dried oregano ½ teaspoon red chilli flakes Crushed black peppercorns to taste Tomato ketchup as required

METHOD:
  1. Take 1 cup flour in a bowl.
  2. Add salt, baking soda, yogurt and some water and knead into a soft dough.
  3. Add oil and knead well.
  4. Set aside for 5-10 minutes.
  5. Take mozzarella cheese in a bowl.
  6. Add processed cheese, dried oregano, chilli flakes, crushed peppercorns and salt and lightly mix.
  7. Heat sufficient oil in a pan.
  8. Divide the dough into equal portions, coat with some flour and roll them out to make thin discs.
  9. Cut each disc into rectangles.
  10. Take 1 tablespoon flour in another bowl.
  11. Add 2-3 tablespoons water to make a thick slurry.
  12. Apply some slurry on 2 sides of each rectangle.
  13. Put some cheese mixture in the center, and fold, applying some slurry on the edges to make thick rolls.
  14. Deep-fry the prepared rolls in hot oil till golden and crisp.
  15. Drain on absorbent paper.
  16. Line a serving platter with individual shot glasses and put some tomato ketchup in each glass.
  17. Place one fried roll in each glass and serve hot.

RECIPE 37: Cheesy Roesti
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Cheesy-Roesti.html

A crispy Swiss delight, marrying golden-brown potatoes with gooey melted cheese for a comforting and indulgent treat. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Mixed cheese (processed, cheddar, mozzarellla), Potatoes | Cuisine: Other Cuisines | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 large potatoes, peeled
  - 1 teaspoon dried mixed herbs ½ teaspoon red chilli flakes Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon crushed black peppercorns ⅓ cup refined flour
  - 2 teaspoons butter Fresh parsley sprig for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Grate potatoes on a plate and soak in a bowl of ice cold water for 15-20 minutes.
  2. Drain the potatoes thoroughly, put them on a kitchen towel and dab excess water.
  3. Transfer into another bowl, add mixed herbs, red chilli flakes, salt, crushed black peppercorns and refined flour and mix well.
  4. Divide the potato mixture into two portions.
  5. Heat a non-stick pan and spread one portion of the potato mixture on it.
  6. Sprinkle cheese evenly on top and spread the remaining potato mixture over the cheese.
  7. Add butter and let it cook until crisp and golden in colour.
  8. Turn and cook similarly on the other side as well.
  9. Turn it out onto a serving dish, garnish it with parsley sprig and serve hot.

RECIPE 38: Chickoo Walnut Kulfi with Salted Caramel Sauce
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chickoo-Walnut-Kulfi-with-Salted-Caramel-Sauce--Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Chickoo and walnuts add a wonderful flavour and texture to this ice cream and the salted caramel sauce is an added attraction This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Sapodilla (chickoo), Walnuts | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 5-6 Sapodilla (chickoo) , quartered, seeded and pureed with skin
  - 2 litres Whole fat milk
  - 2-3 tablespoons Milk powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 1 cup Khoya , grated
  - 3/4 cup Sweet condensed milk Salted caramel sauce
  - 1 pinch Salt
  - 1/4 cup Sugar
  - 3/4 cup Fresh cream
  - 1 tablespoon Butter

METHOD:
  1. Heat milk in a deep non-stick pan.
  2. Once it comes to a boil, reduce heat and simmer, stirring continuously, till it reduces to half its original volume.
  3. Scrape the sides of pan and put it back into the pan.
  4. Grind walnuts to a fine powder.
  5. Take milk powder in a bowl, add 4 tbsps of hot milk and mix well.
  6. Add this mixture to the simmering milk and mix.
  7. Add green cardamom powder and khoya and mix well.
  8. Continue to simmer till the mixture thickens.
  9. Switch the heat off, transfer the mixture into a bowl and set aside to cool down to room temperature.
  10. Add condensed milk and walnut powder to the milk mixture and mix well.
  11. Add sapodilla puree and mix well.
  12. Transfer into a tall jug.
  13. Pour the mixture into metal kulfi moulds till they are ¾ full.
  14. Cover them with their lids and keep the moulds in the freezer for 2 hours or till semi set.
  15. Now insert sticks into kulfi mixture and keep them in the freezer again till completely set.
  16. To prepare salted caramel sauce, heat a non-stick pan, add sugar and caramelize it on low heat.
  17. Gradually add cream and whisk continuously so that no lumps are formed.
  18. Add salt and mix well.
  19. Remove from heat.
  20. Add butter and whisk again.
  21. Demould the kulfis, place them in individual serving bowls and serve with salted caramel sauce.

RECIPE 39: Chilli Chana Aloo
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chilli-Chana-Aloo-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

This tangy preparation will satiate even the most discerning palate. Indo - Chinese preparation made with boiled brown Bengal gram and potatoes. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Red chilli sauce, Red chilli powder | Cuisine: Indo- Chinese | Course: Main | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 tablespoons red chilli sauce
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 2 tbsps schezwan sauce + to garnish
  - 1 cup brown Bengal gram (kala chana) , soaked overnight and boiled
  - 2 medium potatoes (aloo) , boiled and peeled
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 medium onion , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon soy sauce
  - 1 tablespoon vinegar
  - 2 tbsps roughly chopped spring onion greens + to garnish Fried noodles to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add cumin seeds, garlic and ginger, mix well and sauté for 2 minutes.
  2. Add onions, mix and sauté till translucent.
  3. Cut potatoes into small cubes, add and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  4. Add red chilli sauce, soy sauce, vinegar, red chilli powder, Schezwan sauce and brown Bengal gram, mix well and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  5. Add spring onion greens and toss.
  6. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with spring onion greens, Schezwan sauce and fried noodles and serve hot.

RECIPE 41: Chocolate and Coconut Dim sums
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-and-Coconut-Dim-sums-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

You will definitely relish these dimsums in their sweet avatar This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Chocolate syrup, Fresh coconut | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 tbsps + for drizzling Chocolate syrup
  - 1/2 cup Fresh coconut , scraped
  - 250 grams Readymade dim sum dough for brushi tablespoons Ghee
  - 1/4 cup Mixed dried nuts , coarsely powdered
  - 1/2 cup Khoya , grated

METHOD:
  1. Place a banana leaf in a steamer, pour sufficient water in the lower compartment and heat.
  2. Heat 1 tbsp ghee in a non-stick pan, add powdered nuts and saute for a minute.
  3. Add coconut, mix and saute till light brown.
  4. Remove from heat and transfer the mixture into a bowl.
  5. Add khoya and 2 tbsps chocolate syrup and mix well.
  6. Divide the dim sum dough into medium equal portions and roll out each into a disc.
  7. Place a spoonful of coconut mixture in the centre of each disc, brush a little water on the edges, seal and shape into dim sums.
  8. Brush some ghee on the banana leaf, place the dim sums on it, cover the steamer and steam for 5-6 minutes.
  9. Heat 1 tbsp ghee in another non-stick pan, add steamed dim sums and pan-fry till lightly browned on all sides.
  10. Add 2 tbsps chocolate syrup and toss.
  11. Transfer into a serving platter, drizzle some Hersheys Chocolate Syrup on top and serve immediately.

RECIPE 42: Chocolate Bread Bomb
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-Bread-Bomb.html

Chocolate shavings and cheese stuffed between bread roundels and crumb fried till crisp This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

INGREDIENTS:
  - 16 White bread slices
  - 100 grams Processed cheese , grated as required Refined flour slurry
  - 2 cups Dried breadcrumbs to deep fry Oil for dusting Icing sugar

METHOD:

  2. Then cut the bread slices in roundels with a round cutter.

  6. Press the edges to seal.
  7. Dip this bread bomb in refined flour slurry and then coat with breadcrumbs.
  8. Slide these bombs gently into hot oil and deep fry until golden brown and crisp.

RECIPE 43: Chocolate Diya
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-Diya-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

This Diwali you can make edible diyas which the kids will simply love This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Khoya/mawa (375 grams), Sugar (125 grams) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups +
  - 1 tablespoon Khoya/mawa (
  - 375 grams) , grated
  - 1/2 cup Sugar (
  - 125 grams)
  - 2 tablespoons Cocoa powder
  - 7-8 Almonds , slivered and soaked in saffron water

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick pan, add khoya and saute till it melts.
  2. Add sugar and mix well and cook, on medium heat, stirring continuously, till sugar dissolves and mixture starts leaving the sides of pan.
  3. Transfer a small portion of cooked mixture into a small bowl and the remaining mixture into another bowl.
  4. Add cocoa powder to the mixture in the second bowl and mix well.
  5. Add liquid chocolate food colour and mix well.
  6. Refrigerate both mixtures for 10-15 minutes or till they are set.
  7. Divide cocoa-khoya mixture into medium equal portions and shape each into a ball.
  8. Flatten each ball slightly, raise the edges and shape into a diya.
  9. Take small portions of the plain khoya mixture, roll and shape into vaatis.
  10. Place them on the diyas.
  11. Stick soaked almond slivers on vaatis to form jyot (flame).
  12. Transfer the prepared diyas on a serving plate and serve.

RECIPE 44: Chocolate Gulab Jamun
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-Gulab-Jamun-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Chocolate ganache balls stuffed into gulab jamuns give them a delicious make over This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Readymade frozen dark chocolate ganache balls, Hariyali khoya | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 1-1.30 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups Cottage cheese (paneer) , grated
  - 2 cups Sugar
  - 1/2 teaspoon Cornflour
  - 2 tablespoons Refined flour (maida)
  - 1/4 teaspoon Baking soda
  - 1/4 teaspoon Green cardamom powder to deep fry oIL
  - 1 tablespoon Milk to garnish Pistachio slivers

METHOD:
  1. To make sugar syrup cook 2 cups sugar and 2 cups water in a deep kadai on low heat.
  2. Meanwhile take mawa and cottage cheese in a bowl.
  3. Sift together cornflour, refined flour, baking soda and green cardamom powder into this bowl and knead lightly to make smooth dough.
  4. Shape 10 small portions of the dough into balls.
  5. Cover the rest of the dough with a damp muslin cloth and also cover balls with damp muslin cloth.
  6. Add milk to the sugar syrup and let it boil.
  7. Discard the scum that may rise to the top.
  8. Switch off heat just before the syrup reaches one string consistency.
  9. Keep the syrup warm.
  10. Heat sufficient oil in a pan.
  11. Make a dent in the centre of each ball, keep a chocolate ganache ball in it, gather the edges, seal and shape into a ball again.
  12. To remove cracks, moisten palms with water and roll the balls between them.
  13. Set aside covered with muslin cloth.
  14. Place a muslin cloth over a strainer kept over a bowl and strain the sugar syrup.
  15. Slide the balls into hot oil and deep-fry, on low heat, stirring constantly till golden brown.
  16. Drain the fried jamuns and soak them in the lukewarm sugar syrup for 1 hour.
  17. Drain and transfer the gulab jamuns into serving bowls.
  18. Pour a few spoons of sugar syrup over the jamuns.
  19. Garnish with pistachio slivers and serve immediately.

RECIPE 47: Chocolate Pakode
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-Pakode-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A decadent twist on the classic Indian snack, pakode. Chocolate bars batter fried and served garnished with rabdi and chocolate sauce. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup refined flour (maida) ½ cup cornflour ½ teaspoon cinnamon powder + to sprinkle A pinch of baking soda
  - 1 tablespoon powdered sugar + for garnish ¼ teaspoon vanilla essence
  - 8 frozen chocolate bars Cocoa powder for garnish Rabdi for garnish Chocolate sauce to drizzle

RECIPE 48: Chocolate Peanut Chikki
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-Peanut-Chikki.html

Indulge in the perfect fusion of chocolate, peanuts, and jaggery with this chikki- a delightful treat that brings joy to both children and adults alike!

Main Ingredients: Cocoa powder, Roasted peanut powder | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 51-60 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cup cocoa powder
  - 1 cup roasted peanut powder
  - 1 cup chopped jaggery
  - 1 tbsp ghee + for greasing

METHOD:
  1. Line a baking tray with parchment paper and grease a rolling pin with ghee.
  2. Heat 1 tablespoon ghee in a non-stick pan, add jaggery and mix well.
  3. Let the jaggery melt completely.
  4. To test whether the syrup is ready, put a drop of it in cold water.
  5. If it forms a firm ball then the syrup is ready.
  6. Add cocoa powder and mix well, add roasted peanuts and mix well.
  7. Pour the mixture into the lined tray and spread it evenly with the greased rolling pin.
  8. Cut into squares while it is still hot.
  9. Allow to cool and then break the squares.
  10. Serve or store in an air-tight container.

RECIPE 49: Chocolate Sandwich Biscuits
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Chocolate-Sandwich-Biscuits.html

The children will simply enjoy these biscuits sandwiched with chocolate icing and so will the adults This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: For the dough, Cocoa powder | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 51-60 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 tablespoons Cocoa powder
  - 1/3 cup Butter
  - 1/4 teaspoons Baking powder a pinch Salt
  - 1/4 teaspoon Vanilla essence
  - 3 tablespoons Milk to sprinkle Granulated sugar For the icing
  - 1/4 cup Butter
  - 1 cup Icing sugar
  - 3 tablespoons Cocoa powder

METHOD:
  1. To make the dough, take butter and powdered sugar in a bowl and beat till light and fluffy.
  2. Sift refined flour, baking powder, cocoa powder and salt directly in the same bowl and mix well.
  3. Add vanilla essence and milk and mix well to form a dough.
  4. Place a butter paper on the worktop, transfer the dough on it, cover with another piece of butter paper and roll out thinly.
  5. Cut into 1 inch × 3 inch rectangles and arrange them on a greased baking tray keeping a little distance between each.
  6. With the back of satay stick, make small holes at equal distance on each rectangle.
  7. Refrigerate for 10-15 minutes.
  8. Preheat the oven at 180° C.
  9. Place the tray in the preheated oven, sprinkle granulated sugar over the rectangles and bake for 7 minutes.
  10. Transfer the biscuits onto a wire rack and allow to cool down completely.
  11. Meanwhile, for the icing, take butter and icing sugar in another bowl and beat till light and fluffy.
  12. Add cocoa powder and mix till well combined.
  13. Apply the prepared icing evenly on half the biscuits, cover each of them with one of the remaining biscuits.
  14. Arrange the biscuits on a serving platter and serve.
  15. Or store in an airtight container to serve whenever needed.

RECIPE 50: Coconut Moong Soup
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/coconut-moong-soup-7189109

Our 'Coconut Moong Soup' is a delicious and nutritious option that brings together the best of both worlds. This high protein recipe, made with protein-rich moong dal and creamy coconut, results in a soup that's both flavorful and good for you.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Soups Prep time 10-15 minutes | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 cups thin coconut milk ¾ cup soaked whole green gram (sabut moong)
  - 1 tablespoon ghee
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic ½ tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 medium onion, chopped
  - 1 fresh red chilli, diagonally sliced
  - 2 tablespoons chopped spring onions greens Fresh coriander sprigs for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a nonstick deep pan, add garlic, ginger and onion and sauté till translucent.
  2. Add bay leaf and cinnamon and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  3. Add the carrot, sweetcorn kernels and salt, mix and cook for 1 minute.
  4. Add the soaked green gram and mix well.
  5. Stir in the thin coconut milk and 1 cup water and mix well.
  6. Add crushed black peppercorns and red chilli and mix well.
  7. Bring the mixture to a boil, reduce the heat to low and cook for 10-12 minutes.
  8. Add spring onion greens and mix well.
  9. Transfer the soup in a serving bowl, garnish with coriander sprigs and serve hot.

  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped ½ cup gram flour (besan)

RECIPE 52: Corn Halwa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Corn-Halwa-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

This combination of corn kernels and khoya will result in a delicious halwa that will satiate the most discerning palate This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Corn kernels, Ghee | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 6-10 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Corn kernels , boiled
  - 4 tablespoons Ghee
  - 1/4 cup + to garnish Mixed nuts , chopped
  - 1/2 cups Khoyta (mawa) a pinch Saffron strands
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 1/2 cup Jaggery , grated
  - 1 cup Milk

METHOD:
  1. Put corn kernels into a blender jar and blend into a fine paste.
  2. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan, add nuts and sauté till lightly browned and crisp.
  3. Add semolina, mix and sauté till fragrant.
  4. Add corn paste and cook for 4-5 minutes, stirring continuously.
  5. Add khoya and mix till it melts.
  6. Add saffron strands and green cardamom powder and mix well.
  7. Add jaggery and mix till it melts.
  8. Add milk, mix and cook till the mixture thickens.
  9. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with nuts and serve hot.

RECIPE 54: Couscous and Mixed Vegetable Salad with Orange Vinaigrette
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Couscous-and-Mixed-Vegetable-Salad-with-Orange-Vinaigrette.html

Combine couscous, colorful veggies, and a sweet orange vinaigrette into a vibrant salad, topped with fresh microgreens and edible flowers for a refreshing and elegant dish. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Couscous, Orange segments | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Salads | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet &amp; Sour | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 orange segments ½ medium red capsicum, finely chopped ½ medium green capsicum, finely chopped ½ medium tomato, finely chopped
  - 2-3 beetroot microgreens Salt to taste Black pepper powder to taste
  - 2 tablespoons olive oil
  - 1 tablespoon sugar
  - 1 teaspoon lemon juice
  - 1 tablespoon chopped coriander Edible flowers for garnishing

METHOD:
  1. Put water in a bowl, add microgreens and iceberg lettuce leaves.
  2. Keep in the refrigerator for 15-20 minutes.
  3. Boil some water in a non-stick pan.
  4. Put couscous in a large bowl, add salt pepper powder and 1 tablespoon olive oil and mix well.
  5. Add boiling water and mix well.
  6. Cover with cling film.
  7. Set aside for 15 minutes.
  8. Heat orange juice in a 2nd non-stick pan, add sugar and cook till thickens.
  9. Transfer into a bowl.
  10. Cool.
  11. Drain water from the salad leaves and microgreens.
  12. Put couscous in another large bowl, add green and red capsicum, tomato, coriander, orange segments reserving some for garnishing and mix well.
  13. Add orange vinaigrette and mix well.
  14. Place a ring mould on a serving plate, put the prepared couscous salad at the bottom of the ring, put microgreens and iceberg lettuce leaves over it.
  15. Gently remove the ring mould.
  16. Arrange reserved orange segments and edible flowers on the sides and serve immediately

========================================================================

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 tsps Pro V Cranberries
  - 2 lemons, halved
  - 4 pinches of black salt
  - 16-20 ice cubes Fresh mint sprigs for garnish

METHOD:

  2. Make one serving glass of cranberry shikanji at a time.

  7. Garnish with a lemon slice and a fresh mint sprig.

RECIPE 56: Creole Mushroom Rice
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Creole-Mushroom-Rice.html

Rice cooked with mushrooms and some other ingredients in the Creole style. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Button mushrooms, Rice | Cuisine: American, , , , | Course: Rice | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Button mushrooms
  - 2 cups Rice , cooked
  - 1 tablespoon Oil
  - 1 medium Onion , finely chopped
  - 1 medium Green capsicum , diced to taste Salt
  - 1 teaspoon Roasted cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon Paprika powder ½ teaspoon Sugar
  - 2 medium Tomatoes , blanched and chopped
  - 1 teaspoon Lemon juice
  - 4 tablespoons Saffron (kesar) milk
  - 1 tablespoon Butter
  - 3 tablespoons Processed cheese , grated
  - 2 tablespoons Fresh parsley , chopped

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 180º C.
  2. To make Creole sauce, heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  3. Add onion and sauté till it turns translucent Add capsicum, mix and sauté.
  4. Add mushrooms, mix and sauté on lower heat for a minute.
  5. Add salt, cumin powder, paprika powder and sugar and mix well.
  6. Add tomatoes and mix well.
  7. Add ½ cup water, mix and cook on low heat for 2 minutes.
  8. Add 1 tablespoon chopped olives and lemon juice.
  9. Mix well and remove from heat.
  10. To make buttered rice, heat butter in another non-stick pan.
  11. Add rice and toss gently.
  12. Add saffron milk and salt.
  13. Mix well and let it get heated through and switch off the heat.
  14. Spread the buttered rice in a glass baking dish.
  15. Top with a layer of Creole sauce, cheese, remaining olives and chopped parsley.
  16. Put the dish in the preheated oven and bake for 5-8 minutes.
  17. Serve hot.
