RECIPE 57: Crispy Crunchy Baby Corn
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Crispy-Crunchy-Baby-Corn-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Bite-sized bursts of flavor, perfectly fried to golden perfection, offering a delightful crunch with every munch. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Baby corns, Red chilli powder | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 6-10 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1¼ teaspoon red chilli powder + to sprinkle ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder ½ teaspoon crushed black peppercorns
  - 1 tablespoon ginger-garlic paste Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon oil + for deep frying
  - 1 cup refined flour (maida) ½ cup cornflour A pinch of baking soda
  - 1 cup cornflakes Chaat masala to sprinkle Green chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take baby corns in a bowl, add 1 teaspoon red chilli powder, turmeric powder, garam masala powder, crushed black peppercorns, ginger-garlic paste and salt and mix well.
  2. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai Take refined flour, cornflour, baking soda, remaining red chilli powder and a pinch of salt in another bowl.
  3. Add ½ cup water and 1 tablespoon oil and mix well to make a thick batter.
  4. Crush the cornflakes and add to the batter and mix well.

RECIPE 58: Crispy Spinach and Coriander Bites
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Crispy-Spinach-and-Coriander-Bites-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Kothimbir wadi is a well-loved Maharashtrian snack and here we have made it healthier with the addition of spinach This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fresh spinach leaves, Fresh coriander leaves, Gram flour | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup chopped spinach leaves
  - 2 cups chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 cup gram flour (besan) ½ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon ginger -green chilli paste Salt to taste ¼ teaspoon dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 2 tablespoons yogurt
  - 2 teaspoons oil + to grease ½ teaspoon mustard seeds ¼ teaspoon asafoetida
  - 1 teaspoon white sesame seeds (safed til)
  - 1 tablespoon scraped fresh coconut + for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat 4 cups water in a steamer.
  2. Mix coriander leaves, spinach and besan in a bowl.
  3. Add turmeric powder, ginger green chilli paste, salt, dried mango powder and yogurt and mix well.
  4. Add little water and make a dropping consistency mixture.
  5. Grease a thali with some oil.
  6. Transfer the mixture in it.
  7. Tap the thali to level the mixture.
  8. Place the thali in the steamer and steam for 12-15 minutes on medium heat.
  9. Release the steamed mixture from sides of the thali with a palette knife and invert the thali on the worktop.
  10. Trim the edges of the wadi.
  11. Cut into squares.
  12. Heat 2 teaspoons oil in a non-stick pan, add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  13. Add asafoetida, white sesame seeds and wadis and cook on low heat for 2-3 minutes.
  14. Flip and cook till golden brown on both the sides.
  15. Add coconut and cook for few seconds.
  16. Switch off heat.
  17. Transfer the vadis onto a serving platter, garnish with scraped coconut and serve hot.

RECIPE 59: Dal Amboli
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/dal-amboli-7373948

Discover the delightful flavors of Dal Amboli, a classic South Indian comfort food. This dish combines fluffy, fermented rice pancakes with a flavorful dal made from lentils, tomatoes, and aromatic spices, making it perfect for any time of day.

Main Ingredients: Rice, Pressed Rice, Split Pigeon Peas, Split Skinless Green Gram, Split Green Gram with Skin, Split Bengal Gram, Split Red Lentils | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 16-18 hours | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup short grain rice ½ cup pressed rice (poha) ¼ cup split pigeon peas (toovar dal) ¼ cup split skinless green gram (dhuli moong dal) ¼ cup split green gram with skin (chilkewali moong dal) ¼ cup split Bengal gram (chana dal) ¼ cup split red lentils (masoor dal)
  - 1 tablespoon flax seeds
  - 2 teaspoons fenugreek seeds
  - 4 cups buttermilk Salt to taste Onion for greasing Oil as required

METHOD:
  1. Take rice in a bowl.
  2. Add pressed rice, pigeon peas, green gram, green gram with skin, Bengal gram, red lentils, flax seeds, and fenugreek seeds.Wash for 2-3 times.
  3. Add 3 cups buttermilk and soak for 6-8 hours.
  4. Transfer the mixture in a grinder and grind coarsely.
  5. Transfer in a bowl, add remaining buttermilk and mix well.
  6. Set aside to ferment for 8-10 hours.
  7. Add salt and mix well.
  8. Heat a cast iron tawa.
  9. Dip onion half in oil and grease tawa.
  10. Pour a ladleful of batter, drizzle oil, cover and cook for 3-4 minutes on medium heat.
  11. Flip and cook for 2-3 minutes more.
  12. Serve hot with coconut chutney.

RECIPE 60: Dal Baati Churma
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/dal-baati-churma-7080576

This trio of sweet and savoury dishes on a platter is among the finest and most popular offerings from Rajasthan. Served with generous amounts of ghee is metaphorically a way of showing love to the guests.

Cuisine: Rajasthani | Course: Main Course- Vegetarin Prep time 20-5 minutes | Cook Time: 35-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups whole wheat flour (atta) ½ cup semolina Salt to taste ½ cup ghee Melted ghee as required Churma
  - 2 cups whole wheat flour (atta)
  - 4 tablespoons semolina ½ cup pure ghee + to deep fry + to serve
  - 10 raisins Dal
  - 2 cups cooked split red lentils (masoor dal)
  - 2-3 tablespoons oil
  - 2 teaspoons cumin seeds
  - 3 green chillies, chopped
  - 6-8 garlic cloves, chopped
  - 1 tablespoon red chilli powder
  - 2 teaspoons garam masala powder
  - 1 medium tomato, chopped Salt to taste Onion rings for serving Slit green chillies for serving

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 180° C.
  2. To make baatis, take whole wheat flour in a parat.
  3. Add semolina, salt, ½ cup ghee and mix well.
  4. Add 1¼ cups water knead into stiff dough.
  5. Divide the dough into small equal portions and roll into balls and arrange them on a baking tray.
  6. Bake them in the preheated oven for 15-20 minutes.
  7. Dip the baked baatis in melted ghee and let them soak for 5-10 minutes.
  8. To make churma, mix whole wheat flour and semolina in a parat.
  9. Add ½ cup melted ghee and mix well.
  10. Add milk and knead into a stiff dough.
  11. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape into cylinders.
  12. Heat sufficient ghee in a kadai and deep-fry the balls on medium heat, till they are golden brown and crisp.
  13. Drain on absorbent paper and cool.
  14. Transfer in a grinder jar and grind coarsely Add powdered sugar, cardamom powder, cashew nuts, almonds and raisins and mix.
  15. The churma is ready.
  16. To make dal, heat oil in deep non-stick pan and add cumin seeds.
  17. Once they start to change the colour, add green chillies, garlic and sauté for 30 seconds, Add red chilli powder, garam masala powder, tomato and sauté till tomatoes turn soft and pulpy.
  18. Add boiled dal, salt, 2 cups water and mix well.
  19. Cook on low heat for 5 minutes.
  20. Drizzle ghee on dal, baati, churma and serve hot with onion and green chillies.

RECIPE 61: Dal Dhokli
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Dal-Dhokli--.html

Dal Dhokli is an authentic Guajarati dish which is luscious in flavour and tastes best when served hot. A family favourite, it appeases all age groups This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Split pigeon peas (tuvar dal), Turmeric powder | Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Main | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups split pigeon peas (tuvar dal)
  - 1/4 teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste
  - 1/2 tablespoons ghee
  - 1 teaspoon mustard seeds
  - 1/4 teaspoon fenugreek seeds (methi dana)
  - 16-18 curry leaves
  - 1 teaspoon ginger-green chilli paste
  - 15 minutes
  - 1 tsp lemon juice+ for drizzling
  - 1 small onion , finely chopped Fresh coriander leaves , chopped to garnish Dhokli
  - 3/4 cup whole wheat flour (atta)
  - 1/2 cup gram flour (besan) Salt to taste
  - 1/4 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon red chilli powder A pinch of asafoetida
  - 1/2 teaspoon ginger-green chilli paste to apply + teaspoons Oil

METHOD:
  1. Pressure cook pigeon peas in some water with ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder, salt and peanuts till 3-4 whistles are given out.
  2. Open the lid when the pressure is completely released.
  3. To prepare dhokli, combine wheat flour and gram flour in a bowl.
  4. Add salt, ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder, chilli powder, asafoetida, ginger-garlic paste and sufficient water and knead into a semi-soft dough.
  5. Add 2 teaspoons oil and knead again.
  6. Heat ghee in a deep non-stick pan, add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  7. Add fenugreek seeds, asafoetida, broken dried red chillies, curry leaves and cooked pigeon peas and mix well.
  8. Add 1½ cups water and cook till the mixture comes to a boil.
  9. Cover and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  10. Divide the dough into equal portions, apply some oil on each portion and roll out into large thin discs.
  11. Transfer onto the worktop and cut each disc into diamonds.
  12. These are dhoklis.
  13. Add ginger-green chilli paste, and salt to pigeon peas mixture and mix well.
  14. Add dhokli pieces to the pan and mix.
  15. Add jaggery and kokum petal, mix, cover and cook for 10-15 minutes or till dhokli pieces are done.
  16. Switch off heat, add lemon juice and mix well.
  17. Transfer into a serving bowl, top with some onion and coriander leaves, drizzle some lemon juice and serve hot.

RECIPE 62: Dal Soya Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Dal-Soya-Parantha-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Paranthas stuffed with a highly flavoured and nutritious mixture of chana dal and soya chunks will leave you asking for more and more and… This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Split Bengal gram (chana dal), Soya chunks | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3/4 cup Split Bengal gram (chana dal) , soaked and boiled
  - 1 cup Soya chunks , soaked in hot water
  - 250 grams Readymade whole wheat flour dough
  - 1 tbsp + for basting Ghee
  - 1 teaspoon Fennel seeds (saunf)
  - 1 teaspoon Cumin seeds (jeera)
  - 1 teaspoon Carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 2-3 Green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon Red chilli powder
  - 1 tablespoon Coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon Cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon Garam masala powder
  - 1 Dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 10-12 Fresh coriander sprigs to taste Salt

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan, add fennel seeds, cumin seeds and carom seeds, mix and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  2. Add ginger and green chillies, mix and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  3. Add Bengal gram and soya chunks and mix.
  4. Add red chilli powder, coriander powder, cumin powder, garam masala powder, black salt, dried mango powder and crushed peppercorns, mix and cook for 3-4 minutes.
  5. Transfer the mixture into a blender jar and blend to a coarse paste.
  6. Transfer the paste into a bowl.
  7. Chop coriander leaves, add to the bowl and mix well.
  8. Add salt and mix again.
  9. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  10. Divide the dough into equal portions and roll each portion into a ball.
  11. Roll out each portion to a disc, place a portion of dal-soya mixture in the centre, bring edges together, press to seal and roll into a ball.
  12. Dust each stuffed ball with dry flour and roll out into a parantha.
  13. Place the paranthas on the hot tawa, one at a time, and cook, basting with ghee, till evenly cooked and golden on both sides.
  14. Transfer onto individual serving plates and serve hot with your choice of pickle.

RECIPE 64: Deconstructed Vada Pav
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Deconstructed-Vada-Pav-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A modern twist on the iconic Indian street food, featuring separated elements like spiced potato patties, bread, and spicy chutney for a unique culinary experience. This recipe is from Food Food TV channel

Main Ingredients: French baguette , Sweet potato | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8 slices of French baguette, toasted with butter till golden
  - 1½ tablespoons ginger-garlic-green chilli-coriander leaves paste ½ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 5-6 medium sweet potatoes, boiled, peeled and roughly chopped Salt to taste Green chutney as required Vada pav chutney as required
  - 1 cup salted boondi Chives, halved for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a deep non-stick pan, add mustard seeds and curry leaves.
  2. Once the mustard seeds splutter, add ginger-garlic-green chilli-coriander leaves paste.
  3. Saute on medium heat till oil separates.
  4. Add turmeric powder and mix well.
  5. Add sweet potatoes and mix well.
  6. Add salt and sauté for a minute.
  7. Switch off heat.
  8. Place 2 baguette slices on a worktop.
  9. Spread some green chutney over them.
  10. Sprinkle vada pav chutney on top.
  11. Spread some cooked mixture in a dome shape on top.
  12. Take boondis in a bowl and roll the prepared bread slices, upside down, in it till well coated with boondi.
  13. Make more deconstructed vada pavs in the same way.
  14. Transfer deconstructed vada pavs on a serving platter.
  15. Serve immediately, garnished with chives.

RECIPE 65: Double Decker Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Double-Decker-Parantha-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Just one such parantha will satiate you completely stuffed as it is with masaledar rajma and paneer This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Ready whole wheat flour dough, Whole wheat flour | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Red kidney beans (rajma) , soaked overnight, boiled and mashed
  - 1 teaspoon Garam masala powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Red chilli powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon Dried mango powder (amchur_)
  - 1/4 teaspoon Chaat masala
  - 1/2 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1 medium Onion , chopped to taste Salt paneer stuffing
  - 1 cup Cottage cheese (paneer) , grated
  - 1/2 cup Mozzarella cheese , grated
  - 1/2 cup Cheddar cheese , grated
  - 1 tablespoon Fresh mint leaves , finely chopped to sprinkle Chaat masala to shallow fry Ghee grams Yogurt

METHOD:
  1. Take kidney beans in a bowl, add garam masala powder, red chilli powder, dried mango powder, chaat masala and turmeric powder and mix well.
  2. Add onion salt and mix well.
  3. Take cottage cheese in another bowl, add mozzarella cheese, cheddar cheese, mint leaves and chaat masala and mix well.
  4. Divide the dough into 4 small equal portions, 4 slightly bigger equal portions and 4 bigger equal portions.
  5. To prepare the middle layer rotis, sprinkle flour on a worktop, take each small portion of dough and roll it thinly.
  6. Heat a non-stick tawa, put this roti on it and cook, turning sides, till light brown specs appear on both sides.
  7. To prepare the first layer rotis, sprinkle flour on the worktop, take each bigger portion and roll thinly, ensuring that it is bigger than the middle layer roti.
  8. To prepare the third layer rotis, sprinkle flour and take each slightly big portion of dough and roll thinly into a size that is bigger than the middle layer roti but smaller than the first layer roti.
  9. Take the first layer roti, spread spoonful of rajma mixture all over it.
  10. Place the middle layer cooked roti over it.
  11. Spread the cheese mixture all over it.
  12. Cover with third layer roti.
  13. Press completely.
  14. Heat the non-stick tawa again, place a parantha on it and cook, on medium heat, turning sides, till golden brown specs appear on both sides.
  15. Drizzle ghee and continue to cook for 30 seconds on each side.
  16. Make more paranthe similarly.
  17. Keep each parantha on separate serving plates and serve hot with yogurt.

RECIPE 66: Dum ka Tinda
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Dum-ka-Tinda-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Scooped out tindas stuffed with a spicy paneer mixture and cooked in a rich gravy This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Apple gourds (tinda), Ginger | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8-9 Apple gourds (tinda)
  - 2 Green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1 cup Cottage cheese (paneer) , grated
  - 3 teaspoons Red chilli powder to taste Salt
  - 1/4 bunch Fresh coriander leaves
  - 3-4 tablespoons Sunflower oil
  - 1 teaspoon Cumin seeds
  - 1/2 tablespoons Ginger-garlic paste
  - 1/2 tablespoons Coriander powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon Garam masala powder
  - 2 teaspoons Dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 2-3 Green chillies , cut into thin strips
  - 6 Big green chillies , stems removed and halved
  - 1/4 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1 Lemon to garnish Fresh mint sprig

METHOD:
  1. Peel the apple gourds.
  2. Cut off a thin slice from the top and reserve them.
  3. Scoop out the inner pulp with a scooper.
  4. Take ginger, green chillies, cottage cheese, 1 tsp red chilli powder and salt in a bowl.
  5. Blend the scooped portion of apple gourds to a fine paste and add to the cottage cheese mixture.
  6. Chop coriander leaves and add and mix well.
  7. Stuff the apple gourds with this mixture.
  8. Heat a non-stick grill pan, place the stuffed apple gourds on it with the reserved sliced off tops.
  9. Add 2 tbsps sunflower oil and grill, turning sides, till golden on all sides and till grill marks appear.
  10. Heat remaining oil in a non-stick kadai, add cumin seeds and sauté till it changes colour.
  11. Add onions and sauté till it turns golden brown.
  12. Add ginger-garlic paste and sauté for a minute.
  13. Add tomatoes and salt.
  14. Cook till tomatoes turn pulpy.
  15. Sprinkle a little salt over the grilled apple gourds.
  16. Add coriander powder, 1 tsp red chilli powder, cumin powder, garam masala powder, 1 tsp dried mango powder in the kadai and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  17. Add 10-12 cashewnuts and sauté till oil separates.
  18. Switch off heat.
  19. Let the mixture cool down.Transfer the mixture into blender jar and blend to a fine paste.
  20. In same kadai, add ginger strips, green chilli strips, onion and halved big green chillies and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  21. Add the apple gourds and cook on medium heat for 4-5 minutes.
  22. Add remaining red chilli powder, turmeric powder and remaining dried mango powder.
  23. Add sufficient water.
  24. Cover and cook on medium heat for 4-5 minutes.
  25. Add sufficient water and add the ground paste.
  26. Add khoya, remaining cashewnuts, remaining ginger strips and juice of ½ lemon.
  27. Cover and cook on medium heat for 4-5 minutes.
  28. Transfer the apple gourds into a serving bowl along with the chillies and gravy.
  29. Serve hot garnished with cashewnuts and mint sprig.

RECIPE 67: Easy Lentil Salad
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/easy-lentil-salad-7189143

Elevate your salad game with our 'Lentil Salad,' a fantastic high protein recipe that’s both quick to prepare and loaded with nutrients. Whether you’re looking for a quick lunch or a healthy side, this recipe has you covered.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Salads Prep time 8-10 hours | Cook Time: 4-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups boiled whole red lentils (akkha masoor)
  - 3 tablespoons olive oil
  - 2 teaspoons finely chopped garlic
  - 1 teaspoon chopped ginger
  - 2 green chillies, chopped
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped Salt to taste Black pepper powder to taste ½ teaspoon cumin powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 tablespoon lemon juice
  - 20-25 fresh mint leaves
  - 2 teaspoons honey A large pinch of chaat masala Roasted peanuts for garnish Fresh mint sprigs for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat olive oil in pan.
  2. Add garlic, ginger, green chillies and onion and sauté till translucent.
  3. Add salt, black pepper powder, cumin powder and red chilli powder and sauté for 1 minute.
  4. Add ¼ cup water and bring to a boil.
  5. Switch the heat off, add the lemon juice, mix and set aside to cool completely.
  6. Cut the carrot into ½ in cubes, cut the red capsicum and yellow capsicum into ½ inch cubes as well.
  7. And cut the cucumber into ½ inch pieces.
  8. Transfer the chopped vegetables into a large bowl, add the boiled lentils, mint leaves and cooled onion mixture.
  9. Stir in the honey and add chaat masala and mix well till combined.
  10. Garnish with roasted peanuts and mint sprigs and serve.

RECIPE 68: Energy Bar
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Energy-Bar.html

Fuel up with these energy bars packed with a myriad of nutritious ingredients, delivering a powerhouse of energy in every bite. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Oats, Almonds | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 1.30-2 hour | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup oats
  - 2 tablespoons chopped almonds
  - 2 tablespoons chopped cashewnuts
  - 2 tablespoons chopped walnuts
  - 2 tablespoons chopped pistachios
  - 2 tablespoons flax seeds
  - 2 tablespoons pumpkin seeds
  - 2 tablespoons sunflower seeds ¼ cup chopped cranberries ½ cup date paste ⅓ cup honey ¼ teaspoon salt
  - 1 teaspoon butter + for greasing

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick pan, add oats and dry roast on medium heat for 3-4 minutes.
  2. Transfer onto a plate and set aside to cool.
  3. In a same pan add almonds, cashewnuts, walnuts, pistachios, flax seeds, pumpkin seeds and sunflower seeds and dry roast on medium heat for 2-3 minutes, Transfer onto another plate and set aside to cool.
  4. Grease a barfi tray with butter.
  5. Take cranberries in a mixing bowl, add oats, mixed nuts and seeds and date paste and mix well.
  6. Gradually add honey and mix well.
  7. Transfer this mixture onto the greased barfi tray, spread it evenly and keep it in refrigerator for 1½ hours.
  8. Cut into required shape, demould and serve.

RECIPE 69: Farali Paniyaram
========================================================================

Farali Paniyaram is a savory South Indian snack made especially during fasting days or festivals like Navratri. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Rajgira flour, Potato | Cuisine: South Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 tablespoon ghee + ¼ cup ghee

METHOD:

RECIPE 70: Flax Seed Laddoo
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Flax-Seed-Laddoo.html

Powerhouse of nutrition, you can enjoy these laddoos without feeling guilty This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Flax seeds, Jaggery | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups Jaggery , chopped
  - 1/2 cup Raw peanuts
  - 1/2 cup Almonds
  - 1/2 cup Dried coconut , grated
  - 1/2 cup Oats
  - 1/2 cup White sesame seeds
  - 2 tablespoons Black sesame seeds
  - 2 tablespoons Garden cress (alive) seeds
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 1 tablespoon Ghee

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick pan, add jaggery and ¼ cup water, cook, stirring, till a syrup of one string consistency is formed.
  2. Heat another non-stick pan, add flax seeds and dry roast on medium heat for 1-2 minutes and set aside on a plate to cool down.
  3. In the same pan dry roast raw peanuts on medium heat for 2-3 minutes, set aside with flax seeds.
  4. Dry roast almonds, on medium low heat, for 2-3 minutes, keep along with flax seeds mixture.
  5. Dry roast dried coconut and oats for 1-2 minutes and set aside along with the flax seed mixture, let it cool down completely.
  6. Further dry roast white sesame seeds, black sesame seeds and aliv together for 1-2 minutes, set aside in a bowl.
  7. Grind together the flax seed mixture to a coarse powder.
  8. Transfer into a bowl, add the sesame seeds mixture and jaggery syrup and mix well Divide the mixture into equal portions and shape each portion into a laddoo and set aside on a plate to cool down to room temperature.
  9. Once cooled completely store in an airtight container or serve.

RECIPE 71: Fresh Spring Roll Wrappers
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Fresh-Spring-Roll-Wrappers.html

Elevate your appetizers with our Fresh Spring Roll Wrappers, perfect for crafting light and vibrant rolls bursting with crisp veggies and aromatic herbs. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida), Salt | Cuisine: Chinese | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups boiled and shredded chicken
  - 1½ tablespoons finely chopped garlic
  - 1 spring onion, chopped with the greens
  - 1 small carrot, cut into thin strips
  - 150 grams shredded cabbage
  - 1 cup mixed coloured capsicum strips
  - 1 teaspoon vinegar
  - 1 teaspoon dark soy sauce Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste Refined flour slurry for applying Sliced spring onion greens for garnish Schezwan sauce to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take refined flour in a large bowl.
  2. Add salt and 1¼ cups water little by little and mix with a wooden spoon till a smooth batter is formed.
  3. Continue to mix for 5 minutes.
  4. Cover and set aside to rest for 1½ hours.
  5. To make the stuffing, heat oil in a non-stick wok.
  6. Add garlic and ginger and sauté for a minute.
  7. Add spring onion bulb and sauté for a few seconds.
  8. Add carrot and cabbage and mix well.
  9. Sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  10. Add coloured capsicum strips, vinegar, dark soy sauce, salt and crushed black peppercorns and mix well.
  11. Add chicken and mix well.
  12. Add spring onion greens and toss.
  13. Take the pan off the heat and allow the mixture to cool.Mix the rested batter well with your hand for 1-2 minutes.
  14. Heat a non-stick tawa¬ on low heat.
  15. Take a big portion of the dough and spread a thin layer of the batter in a circular motion and collect the excess dough and keep it aside.
  16. Cook for 10-15 seconds, flip and cook for 1-2 seconds.
  17. Remove from heat and set aside.
  18. Similarly, make the remaining spring roll wrappers.
  19. Use as required.
  20. To make spring rolls, place a spring roll sheet on a worktop, place a generous portion of the stuffing in the centre.
  21. Apply some refined flour slurry on the edges, fold the sides and tightly roll it.
  22. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  23. Gently slide in the rolls a few at a time and deep fry till golden brown and crisp.
  24. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  25. Arrange them on a serving platter and serve hot with Schezwan sauce.

RECIPE 72: Fresh Tuvar Green Masala
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Fresh-Tuvar-Green-Masala-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

This is a winter recipe when fresh tuvar pods are available – absolutely delicious. Fresh pigeon peas cooked with Indian spices and potatoes. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fresh tuvar pods, Fresh coriander-coconut-ginger-green chilli paste | Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Main | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 200 grams fresh tuvar pods , shelled
  - 1/2 cup fresh coriander-coconut-ginger-green chilli paste
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 medium onion , chopped
  - 1 medium potato
  - 1/2 teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste Fresh coriander sprig to garnish

METHOD:

  2. Meanwhile slice potato and soak in a bowl of water.
  3. Add turmeric powder to the onion mixture and mix well.
  4. Add fresh coriander-coconut-ginger-green chilli paste, mix and sauté well.
  5. Drain and add potato and fresh tuvar and mix well.
  6. Add salt and mix well.
  7. Add 1 cup water, mix well, cover and cook till both potato and tuvar are cooked completely.

RECIPE 73: Fried Cheese Burger
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Fried-Cheese-Burger.html

Mozzarella cheese squares rolled in spiced breadcrumbs, deep-fried and served sandwiched in burger buns This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Mozzarella cheese block, Mini burger buns | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 mini burger buns
  - 1 cup bread crumbs ½ teaspoon garlic power
  - 1 teaspoon onion powder ½ teaspoon dried mixed herbs Salt to taste ½ teaspoon red chilli flakes ½ cup refined flour (maida) Crushed black peppercorns to taste Butter for toasting Oil for deep fryingLayering Ketchup- mayo for applying Lettuce leaves as required Tomato slices as required Onion slices as required Crushed black peppercorns to taste Salt to taste Pickled jalapeno slices as required Black olives for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Spread bread crumbs on a plate.
  2. Add garlic powder, onion powder, dried mixed herbs, salt and red chilli flakes and mix well.
  3. Take refined flour in a bowl.
  4. Add crushed black peppercorns, salt and pour ½ cup water and mix till well combined.
  5. Dip the mozzarella squares into the refined flour mixture, coat with the bread crumbs mixture, and repeat the process one more time.
  6. Place the prepared mozzarella squares into the freezer for 1-2 hours.
  7. Slit the burger buns in half.
  8. Heat butter in a non-stick grill pan, place the burger buns and toast for 30 seconds.
  9. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai, gently slide in the frozen mozzarella squares and deep fry on medium heat till golden brown and crisp.
  10. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  11. To make the burger, apply some ketchup-mayo on the burger bun base and place some lettuce leaves.
  12. Place the fried cheese and arrange tomato slice and onion rings.
  13. Sprinkle crushed black pepper corns, salt and arrange some pickled jalapeno slices over it.
  14. Arrange some more lettuce leaves on top.
  15. Apply some ketchup-mayo on the base of the remaining burger half and place it on top to make a burger.
  16. Secure it with a toothpick and garnish with black olives.
  17. Serve immediately.

RECIPE 74: Gahat ka Shorba
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Gahat-ka-Shorba-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Made from nutrient-rich horse gram lentils simmered to perfection with aromatic spices, this hearty broth boasts a velvety texture and a depth of flavor that is truly unforgettable.

Main Ingredients: Horse gram (kulith) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Soups | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups horse gram (kulith), soaked overnight and boiled
  - 1 tablespoon oil ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing)
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds (jeera)
  - 1 teaspoon mustard seeds (rai)
  - 1 tablespoon coriander seeds
  - 2-3 green chillies, finely chopped
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander stems Crushed black peppercorns to taste Salt to taste Fresh mint sprigs for garnishing

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add asafoetida, garlic, ginger, cumin seeds, mustard seeds and coriander seeds and sauté till fragrant.
  3. Add green chillies and coriander stems and mix.
  4. Add horse gram, crushed peppercorns and salt, mix well.
  5. Add some water, cover and cook for 6-8 minutes.
  6. Switch off heat, blend the gram mixture with a hand blender and strain.
  7. Garnish with mint sprigs and serve hot.

Kulfis coated with gajar halwa and deep fried to a lovely golden crispiness This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

RECIPE 76: Gatte ki Sabzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/gatte-ki-sabzi-7080702

The very popular Gatte ki Sabzi from Rajasthan, made easy for you to prep at home. Try this recipe, you'll love it. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Rajasthani | Course: Main Course- Vegetarian Prep time 15-20 minutes | Cook Time: 30-35 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Milld Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian Gatte Gatte 1¼ cups gram flour (besan) A pinch of carom seeds (ajwain) ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ¼ teaspoon red chilli powder Salt to taste 1 teaspoon garam masala powder ½ teaspoon cumin powder A pinch of baking soda 2 tablespoons yogurt 1 teaspoon ginger-garlic-green chilli paste 2 tablespoons + ½ teaspoon oil Sabzi 1 cup yogurt ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon cumin powder Salt to taste ½ teaspoon ginger-garlic-green chilli paste 2 tablespoons ghee 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing) 2 dried red chillies 1 large onion, finely chopped 1 cup fresh tomato puree ¼ teaspoon dry fenugreek leaves (kasuri methi) ½ teaspoon garam masala powder 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves Fresh coriander sprig for garnish

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1¼ cups gram flour (besan) A pinch of carom seeds (ajwain) ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ¼ teaspoon red chilli powder Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder ½ teaspoon cumin powder A pinch of baking soda
  - 2 tablespoons yogurt
  - 1 teaspoon ginger-garlic-green chilli paste
  - 2 tablespoons + ½ teaspoon oil Sabzi
  - 1 cup yogurt ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon cumin powder Salt to taste ½ teaspoon ginger-garlic-green chilli paste
  - 2 tablespoons ghee
  - 2 dried red chillies
  - 1 large onion, finely chopped
  - 1 cup fresh tomato puree ¼ teaspoon dry fenugreek leaves (kasuri methi) ½ teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves Fresh coriander sprig for garnish

METHOD:
  1. For making the gatte, take gram flour in a bowl, add carom seeds, turmeric powder, red chilli powder, salt, garam masala powder, cumin powder, baking soda, yogurt, ginger-garlic-green chilli paste, 2 tbsps oil, and ¼ cup water and knead to a semi-soft dough.
  2. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  3. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape each into an oblong shape.
  4. Boil sufficient water in a non-stick deep pan, add salt and remaining oil along with the shaped dough portions and boil for 8-10 minutes.
  5. Drain on to a plate, pour 2 cups cooking liquor over it and cut the cooked dough portions into ½ inch discs, these are called gatte.
  6. Set aside until in use.
  7. For the sabzi, heat ghee in a kadai, add cumin seeds and let them change colour.
  8. Add asafoetida, dried red chillies and sauté for a few seconds.
  9. Add onion, mix and sauté till it turns golden brown.
  10. Add tomato puree, mix and cook for 4-5 minutes.
  11. Add yogurt mixture, mix and cook till the fat separates.
  12. Add dry fenugreek leaves, mix and cook for a minute.
  13. Add the cooked gatte, mix and cook further for 6-8 minutes.
  14. Add garam masala powder and coriander leaves and mix well.
  15. Take the kadai off the heat and transfer into a serving bowl.
  16. Garnish with coriander sprig and serve hot.

RECIPE 77: Gluten Free Biscuit Khakra
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Gluten-Free-Biscuit-Khakra.html

These are not only for the gluten intolerant people – they are so tasty that you are sure to enjoy them This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Amaranth (rajgira) flour, Barnyard millet (samo) flour | Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup amaranth (rajgira) flour ½ cup barnyard millet (samo) flour Salt to taste
  - 2½ tablespoons ghee

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a small pan.
  2. Take amaranth flour in a large bowl, add barnyard millet flour, salt, dried fenugreek leaves, red chilli powder, cumin powder, coriander powder, ginger-green chilli paste, sugar and dried mango powder.
  3. Add hot ghee to the flour mixture and mix well.
  4. Add 1 cup water and knead into a soft dough.
  5. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 5 minutes.
  6. Take a large portion of the dough and roll into a large thick disc.
  7. Cut out roundels with a cookie cutter.
  8. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  9. Place a few discs on it and cook on medium heat for 2 minutes, flip and cook the other side for 2 minutes as well.
  10. Press the discs with a wooden spoon so that the discs do not puff up.
  11. Flip again and continue to press lightly.
  12. Repeat the process till the discs turn golden and crisp on both sides.
  13. Place them on a cooling wire rack for a few minutes or till they cool down to room temperature.
  14. Arrange them on a serving platter and serve or store in an airtight container.

RECIPE 78: Gobhi 65
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Gobhi-65.html

Spicy and crispy with just the right amount of sauce, this drool-worthy dish is an ideal starter! This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Cauliflower (gobhi) , Ginger-garlic paste, yogurt | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 large cauliflower (gobhi), cut into medium florets
  - 1 tablespoon ginger-garlic paste
  - 2 teaspoons red chilli powder ¾ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 3 teaspoons cumin powder
  - 3 teaspoons coriander powder Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 2 tablespoons lemon juice Salt to taste
  - 1 cup yogurt
  - 3 tablespoons cornstarch
  - 1 tablespoon refined flour (maida)
  - 1 tablespoon oil + for deep-frying
  - 6-8 curry leaves
  - 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon chopped garlic
  - 1 tablespoon red chilli paste
  - 2-3 tablespoons sliced spring onion greens + for garnishing

METHOD:
  1. To prepare the marinade, mix together ginger-garlic paste, 2 teaspoons chilli powder, ½ teaspoon turmeric powder, 2 teaspoons cumin powder, 2 teaspoons coriander powder, crushed peppercorns and 1 tablespoon lemon juice in a bowl.
  2. Add salt and 2-3 tablespoons water and mix well.
  3. Add cauliflower florets to the marinade and mix till well coated.
  4. Set aside to marinate for 25-30 minutes.
  5. Mix together yogurt, remaining chilli powder, remaining turmeric powder, cumin powder, coriander powder, salt and 2 tablespoons cornstarch alongwith 2-3 tablespoons water in another bowl.
  6. Add remaining cornstarch and refined flour to the marinated cauliflower florets and mix well.
  7. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  8. Put the marinated cauliflower florets and deep-fry till golden brown and crisp.
  9. Drain on absorbent paper.
  10. Heat 1 tablespoon oil in non-stick pan.
  11. Add mustard seeds and let it splutter.
  12. Add dried red chillies and sauté for 30 seconds.
  13. Add curry leaves and when it crackles, add green chillies, ginger and garlic and sauté for 1 minute.
  14. Add red chilli paste and sauté for 1 minute.
  15. Add yogurt mixture, mix and cook on low heat for 1-2 minutes.
  16. Add 3-4 tablespoons water, mix and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  17. Add salt and mix.
  18. Add fried cauliflower florets, mix and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  19. Add spring onion greens and mix.
  20. Switch off heat, add remaining lemon juice and mix well.
  21. Serve hot garnished with spring onion greens.

RECIPE 79: Gobhi Aloo Chaat Pakoda
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Gobhi-Aloo-Chaat-Pakoda-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

It is a delicious Indian street food snack made from cauliflower (gobhi) and potato (aloo), mixed with spices, gram flour (besan), and herbs. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Cauliflower (gobhi), Potatoes (aloo) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 large cauliflower (gobhi)
  - 4 medium potatoes (aloo), boiled and peeled
  - 1 tablespoon red chilli sauce ½ tablespoon tomato ketchup
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 2 teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 2 teaspoons chaat masala Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon chopped ginger
  - 2-3 green chillies, chopped
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon green chilli sauce
  - 1 tablespoon green chutney + for topping Oil for deep-frying
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander leaves Grated radish (mooli) for topping Green capsicum strips for topping Red capsicum strips for topping Batter
  - 1 cup gram flour
  - 1 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain) ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon ginger-garlic paste Salt to tasteSauce
  - 1 tablespoon grated radish (mooli)
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped onion
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon finely chopped ginger
  - 2 green chillies, finely chopped
  - 3 tablespoons green chilli sauce
  - 2 tablespoons red chilli sauce
  - 2 tablespoons tomato ketchup
  - 2 tablespoons sugar Juice of ½ lemon

METHOD:
  1. Take cauliflower florets in a bowl, add red chilli sauce, tomato ketchup, red chilli powder, 1 teaspoon dried mango powder, 1 teaspoon chaat masala and salt and mix well.
  2. Mash potatoes in another bowl.
  3. Add ginger, green chillies, onion, green chilli sauce, green chutney, remaining dried mango powder, remaining chaat masala and salt and mix well.
  4. To make batter, take gram flour in a bowl, add carom seeds, turmeric powder, chilli powder, ginger-garlic paste, salt and water as required and whisk well to make a lump free batter of coating consistency.
  5. Divide the potato mixture into equal portions, stuff each portion with a cauliflower floret and shape into balls.
  6. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  7. To make sauce, heat oil in a non-stick pan, add ginger and green chillies and sauté till fragrant.
  8. Add green chilli sauce, red chilli sauce, tomato ketchup and sugar, mix and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  9. Transfer into a bowl.
  10. Add lemon juice, radish, onion and coriander leaves and mix well.
  11. Dip the balls in the batter and deep-fry in hot oil for a minute.
  12. Drain on absorbent paper and flatten a little.
  13. Deep-fry once again till golden brown.
  14. Drain on absorbent paper.
  15. Halve the pakodas and place them on a serving platter.
  16. Serve them topped with green chutney, sauce, coriander leaves, radish, green and red capsicum strips.

RECIPE 82: Gulab Jamun Kheer
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Gulab-Jamun-Kheer-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Main Ingredients: Mini gulab jamuns, Milk | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 litres Milk
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 3 tablespoons Mixed nuts , chopped
  - 2 hours and coarsely ground
  - 300 grams Kalakand , crumbled

METHOD:

RECIPE 84: Hare Pyaaz , Neem aur Imli ki Chutney
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Hare-Pyaaz-,-Neem-aur-Imli-ki-Chutney--Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A very unique combination of spring onions, neem leaves and tamarind made into a chutney. Best enjoyed with missi roti.

Main Ingredients: Spring onion greens, Neem leaves | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Pickles, Jams and Chutneys | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 15-20 neem leaves Marble siz tamarind , soaked in warm water
  - 1/2 tablespoons garlic , chopped
  - 1 tablespoon ginger , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon white sesame seeds (safed til)
  - 6-7 green chillies , chopped
  - 1/2 teaspoon asafoetida Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon black salt
  - 1 teaspoon roasted cumin powder Missi roti to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic, ginger and white sesame seeds.
  2. Sauté for a minute on medium heat, stirring continuously.
  3. Add green chillies and sauté for a minute.
  4. Add asafoetida and mix well.
  5. Add neem leaves and sauté for a minute.
  6. Roughly chop spring onions greens and add to the pan.
  7. Squeeze tamarind pulp and add to the pan and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  8. Add salt and mix well.
  9. Cook for 1-2 minutes on medium heat.
  10. Add black salt and roasted cumin powder and mix well.
  11. Cook for 1-2 minutes and switch off heat.
  12. Let the mixture cool slightly.
  13. Transfer the mixture into a blender jar and grind into fine paste.
  14. Transfer into a small serving bowl and set aside to cool.
  15. Serve with missi roti.

RECIPE 85: Hercules Bar
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Hercules-Bar-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A powerhouse of flavor with a mighty combination of nuts, caramel, and chocolate, guaranteed to satisfy your cravings and fuel your day. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Walnuts, Ghee | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup walnuts
  - 3 tablespoons ghee + for greasing
  - 1 cup finger millet (nachni) flour ½ cup roasted peanuts
  - 1½ cups chopped jaggery ½ teaspoon green cardamom powder

METHOD:
  1. Grease a tray with ghee.
  2. Blend walnuts to a coarse powder.
  3. Heat ghee in a deep stainless steel pan, add nachni flour and California walnut powder, mix and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  4. Blend peanuts to a fine powder and add to the pan.
  5. Mix and cook on low heat for 2-3 minutes, stirring continuously.
  6. Chop amla candies and add to the pan.
  7. Mix and cook, stirring continuously, on low heat for 4-5 minutes or till the colour of mixture changes to brown.
  8. Add jaggery and green cardamom powder and mix.
  9. Cook till jaggery melts and mixture leaves the sides of the pan.
  10. Pour the mixture into the greased tray and spread evenly.
  11. Set aside to cool down.
  12. Cut into bars and serve immediately.

  - 1 cup Fresh cream

Popular Punjabi sweet made with arrowroot biscuits instead of whole wheat flour This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

  - 1 pinch Salt

RECIPE 88: Instant Rice Dhokla
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/instant-rice-dhokla-6856101

Do you have some rice left at home? Here is an amazing way to give your leftover rice a new life. This instant dhokla as the name suggests can be made instantly and tastes delicious.

Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 20-25 minutes | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup leftover cooked rice ¾ cup yogurt
  - 1 cup semolina (rawa)
  - 1½ tablespoons finely chopped spring onion bulbs
  - 2 tablespoons finely chopped spring onion greens Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon sugar Oil for greasing
  - 1 teaspoon fruit salt Tempering
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 1½ teaspoons white sesame seeds

METHOD:
  1. Put cooked rice in a blender jar.
  2. Add yogurt and blend to a fine paste.
  3. Transfer this into a large bowl.
  4. Add ginger-green chilli paste, green capsicum, yellow capsicum, red capsicum, carrot, spring onion bulbs, spring onion greens, salt, sugar and 1 cup water and mix till well combined.
  5. Heat sufficient water in a steamer.
  6. Grease a dhokla thali with some oil.
  7. Add fruit salt into the batter and mix well.
  8. Transfer this into the greased thali and place it in the steamer and steam for 10-15 minutes or till done.
  9. Switch the heat off and allow to cool.
  10. Cut the dhokla into squares.
  11. To make the tempering, heat oil in a small pan.
  12. Add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  13. Add asafoetida, curry leaves and white sesame seeds and sauté for a few seconds.
  14. Pour this immediately over the dhokla.
  15. Arrange on a serving plate and serve with green chutney.

RECIPE 89: Jackfruit Seed Sambhar
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Jackfruit-Seed-Sambhar.html

A unique sambhar loaded with flavours that will leave you asking for more This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Ripe jackfruit kernels, Salt | Cuisine: South Indian | Course: Dals and Kadhis | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 41-50 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 20-25 Ripe jackfruit kernels to taste Salt
  - 1/4 teaspoon Turmeric powder Sambhar
  - 1 tablespoon Oil
  - 20-25 Curry leaves
  - 1/2 tablespoons Sambhar masala powder
  - 3/4 cup Tamarind water , (lemon sized tamarind ball soaked in
  - 3/4 cup war
  - 20 minutes, boiled with
  - 1 cup water,
  - 1 tablespoon Jaggery , chopped
  - 1/4 teaspoon Asafoetida
  - 2 tablespoons Fresh coriander leaves , chopped Tempering
  - 1 tablespoon Ghee
  - 10-12 Curry leaves To serve as required Steamed rice for drizzling Ghee as required Pappadums , fried

METHOD:
  1. Remove the seeds from each jackfruit kernel and wash them well.
  2. Put the seeds in a pressure cooker, add 1½ cups water, salt and turmeric powder, mix, and cook for 3-4 whistles.
  3. Open the cooker once the pressure has reduced completely.
  4. Drain the seeds and let them cool slightly.
  5. Peel them and keep them in the strainer.
  6. To make the sambhar, heat oil in a non-stick deep pan, add fenugreek seeds and sauté for a few seconds.
  7. Add madras onions and 10-12 curry leaves, mix and sauté till onions turn golden brown.
  8. Add the peeled jackfruit seeds, mix and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  9. Add turmeric powder and sambhar powder, mix and sauté for 30 seconds Add tamarind water and 1 cup water and mix well.
  10. Add salt and mix well.
  11. Bring it to a boil.
  12. Continue to cook on medium heat for 15-20 minutes.
  13. Add boiled pigeon peas and mix well.
  14. Add 1 cup water, jaggery, asafoetida and remaining curry leaves and mix well.
  15. Bring the mixture to a boil.
  16. Add coriander leaves and mix well.
  17. To make the tempering, heat ghee in a small non-stick pan, add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  18. Add curry leaves and sauté for a few seconds.
  19. Immediately pour this into the prepared sambhar and mix well.
  20. Transfer the sambhar into a serving bowl, garnish with coriander leaves and serve hot with steamed rice drizzled with ghee and fried papadams.

RECIPE 90: Jaggery Cake
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Jaggery-Cake.html

Whole wheat flour and jaggery made this cake healthy This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Jaggery powder, Yogurt | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3/4 cup Jaggery powder
  - 1/2 cup Yogurt
  - 1/4 cup Oil
  - 1 teaspoon Vanilla essence
  - 1 cup Whole wheat flour (gehun ka atta)
  - 1 teaspoon Baking powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Baking soda a pinch Cinnamon powder
  - 1/4 cup Milk

METHOD:
  1. Preheat an oven to 180° C Take the yogurt in a bowl, add oil, vanilla essence and jaggery powder and beat with an electric beater till the jaggery melts.
  2. Sift the whole wheat flour, baking powder, baking soda and cinnamon powder directly into the yogurt mixture and mix and fold in.
  3. Add milk and mix gently till a smooth batter is formed.
  4. Pour the batter into a 6 x 2 x 2 inch silicon rectangular cake mould and tap a few times.
  5. Place the cake mould on a baking tray, keep the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 25-30 minutes.
  6. Bring the baking tray out of the oven and allow the cake to cool completely.
  7. De-mould and slice.
  8. Arrange the slices on a serving platter and serve.

RECIPE 91: Jain Corn Tamatar Nu Shaak
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/jain-corn-tamatar-nu-shaak-7092241

Spicy, creamy and yet superbly Jain, even without the onion and garlic. Serve hot with parathas. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main Course- Veg Prep time 15-20 minutes | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 corn on the cob
  - 4 medium tomatoes, roughly chopped Gravy
  - 1 inch cinnamon stick
  - 1 dried red chilli
  - 1 tablespoon melon seeds
  - 1 tablespoon roasted unsalted peanuts, peeled ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste Tempering
  - 2 medium tomatoes, finely chopped
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing)
  - 1 medium green capsicum, finely chopped
  - 2-3 green chillies, chopped
  - 1 teaspoon coriander powder ½ teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 1 teaspoon cumin powder ¼ teaspoon chaat masala ½ teaspoon red chilli powder ½ cup grated cottage cheese (paneer) Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon sugar
  - 2 tablespoons fresh cream ¼ teaspoon green cardamom powder
  - 1 teaspoon dried fenugreek leaves (kasuri methi)
  - 1½ tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves Fresh coriander sprig for garnish Paranthe to serve

METHOD:
  1. Roast the corn on the cob on direct flame till well charred from all sides.
  2. Place the corn on the worktop and remove the corn kernels with the help of a knife.
  3. Put the corn kernels into a blender jar.
  4. Blend to a coarse paste.
  5. Heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  6. Add cinnamon stick, cloves, black peppercorns, and dried red chilli and sauté for a few seconds.
  7. Add tomatoes and mix well.
  8. Cook till soft and pulpy.
  9. Add melon seeds and roasted peanuts and mix well.
  10. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  11. Add turmeric powder and salt and mix well.
  12. Add ½ cup water, mix and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  13. Switch the heat off, discard the cinnamon stick and allow the mixture to cool slightly.
  14. Put the mixture into a blender jar and blend to a fine paste.
  15. For the tempering, heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  16. Add cumin seeds and asafoetida and mix well.
  17. Add green capsicum and mix, cook for 1-2 minutes.
  18. Add green chillies, and tomatoes and mix well.
  19. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  20. Add blended paste, mix and cook for 1 minute.
  21. Add blended corn mixture and mix well.
  22. Add 1 cup water and mix.
  23. Add coriander powder, garam masala powder, cumin powder, chaat masala, and red chilli powder and mix well.
  24. Cook for 2-3 minutes.
  25. Add cottage cheese and mix.
  26. Add salt, sugar and fresh cream and mix well.
  27. Add green cardamom powder, dried fenugreek leaves and lemon juice and mix well.
  28. Add coriander leaves, mix and switch the heat off.
  29. Transfer the mixture into a serving bowl.
  30. Garnish with coriander sprig.
  31. Serve hot with paranthe.

RECIPE 93: Jain Pakoda
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/jain-pakoda-7090850

Simple and delicious pakodas made with cabbage and gram flour. Simply irresistible ! In this Jain version, onions are replaced with cabbage . This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 10-15 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 small cabbage, thinly shredded
  - 1 cup gram flour (besan)
  - 2 tablespoons rice flour
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 teaspoon sugar ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing)
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon crushed black peppercorns
  - 1 teaspoon lemon juice Salt to taste
  - 2 teaspoons oil + for deep frying Jain green chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take cabbage in a large bowl.
  2. Add gram flour, rice flour, coriander leaves, sugar, asafoetida, red chilli powder, crushed black peppercorns, lemon juice, salt, and oil and mix well.
  3. Add ½ cup water and mix till a thick mixture is formed.
  4. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  5. Gently slide in small portions of the mixture and deep fry till golden brown and crisp.
  6. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  7. Arrange the pakodas on a serving plate and serve hot with Jain green chutney.

RECIPE 94: Jain Seekh Kebab
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/jain-seekh-kebab-7092314

Finger food gets a Jain twist. The joy of a pure veg seekh kebab with veggies and raisins that are very succulent. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 15-20 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3-4 medium raw bananas, boiled, peeled and mashed
  - 4 tablespoons oil
  - 2-3 green chillies, finely chopped ½ cup finely chopped cabbage ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 4-5 raisins (kismis)
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 tablespoons finely chopped fresh mint leaves
  - 2 tablespoons roasted gram flour Cabbage salad to serve Jain green chutney to serve Fresh mint leaves for garnish Lemon wedges to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add green chillies and cabbage and mix well.
  3. Add turmeric powder and mix well.
  4. Cook for 1 minute.
  5. Take the pan off the heat and allow to cool slightly.
  6. Take boiled raw banana in a large bowl, add the cabbage mixture, red chilli powder, chaat masala, salt, green cardamom powder, raisins, coriander leaves, mint leaves, and roasted gram flour and mix till well combined.
  7. Dip your fingers in some water and take a portion of the mixture and spread it on to a satay stick and shape it like a seekh.
  8. Heat remaining oil in a non-stick pan.
  9. Place the seekh on it and cook for 3-4 minutes, rotating the seekh in between till golden brown on all sides.
  10. Arrange the seekhs on a serving plate, garnish with mint leaves and serve hot with salad, Jain green chutney, and lemon wedges.

RECIPE 95: Jeera Kulcha Biscuits
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Jeera-Kulcha-Biscuits-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

The delightful fusion of Indian spices and buttery goodness in every crunchy nibble. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Cumin seeds, Salted butter | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds Caraway seeds (shahi jeera) to sprinkle
  - 170 grams salted butter, softened
  - 100 grams powdered sugar
  - 1 teaspoon vanilla essence
  - 190 grams refined flour (maida)
  - 100 grams rice flour
  - 2 tablespoons chopped mixed nuts (almonds and pistachios) + to sprinkle White sesame seeds (safed til) to sprinkle Sea salt to sprinkle

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 180º C.
  2. Take butter and powdered sugar in a bowl and cream with a wooden spoon till the mixture becomes light in colour.
  3. Add vanilla essence and cumin seeds and mix well.
  4. Sift together refined flour, rice flour into the butter mixture.
  5. Add mixed nuts and mix well.
  6. Sprinkle little water and make medium soft dough.
  7. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape into thick discs.
  8. Grease a baking tray with oil.
  9. Place the discs on it.
  10. Sprinkle caraway seeds, white sesame seeds and sea salt and press lightly.
  11. Sprinkle chopped mixed nuts and press lightly.
  12. Place the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 15-20 minutes.
  13. Allow to cool.
  14. Arrange on a serving platter and serve.

RECIPE 96: Jowar Pumpkin Gnocchi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Jowar-Pumpkin-Gnocchi-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

A wholesome twist on classic gnocchi, this dish blends sweet potato, pumpkin, and sorghum flour, tossed in a fragrant garlic-herb pumpkin sauce and topped with parmesan.

Main Ingredients: Sorghum flour (jowar ka atta), Boiled pumpkin puree | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Noodles and Pastas | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups sorghum flour (jowar ka atta)
  - 2 cups boiled pumpkin puree
  - 2 medium sweet potatoes , boiled, peeled and cut into medium sized pieces Salt to taste Black peppercorns to taste
  - 3 tablespoons olive oil
  - 2 tablespoons finely chopped garlic
  - 8-10 fresh basil leaves + for garnish
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli flakes
  - 20 grams parmesan cheese

METHOD:
  1. Take sorghum flour in a mixing bowl, add sweet potatoes and mash with a fork.
  2. Add 1 cup pumpkin puree, salt and crushed black peppercorns, and knead into a dough.
  3. To make gnocchi, take small portions of the dough and shape them into cylinders.
  4. Flatten the edges.
  5. Heat sufficient water in a deep non-stick deep pan and let it come to a boil.
  6. Drop in the gnocchis into the boiling water and cook till they float on the surface.
  7. Meanwhile to make the sauce, heat oil in a shallow non-stick pan, add garlic and sauté well.
  8. Add the remaining pumpkin puree and mix well.
  9. Strain the cooked gnocchi and add to the sauce and toss gently till they are well coated with the sauce.
  10. Add salt and mixed herbs.
  11. Tear basil leaves and add to the gnocchi.
  12. Add red chilli flakes and gently toss on high heat.
  13. Transfer into a serving plate, grate parmesan cheese on top and garnish with basil leaves.
  14. Serve hot.

RECIPE 97: Kadai Kala Chana
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Kadai-Kala-Chana-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Freshly ground kadai masala makes this kala chana dish extra special. Brown Bengal gram cooked with Indian spices. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Brown Bengal gram (kala chana), Coriander seeds | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups brown Bengal gram (kala chana) , soaked overnight and boiled
  - 1 tablespoon coriander seeds
  - 4 dried red chillies
  - 2 teaspoons cumin seeds
  - 2 bay leaves
  - 2 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1/2 cup tomato puree
  - 1/2 teaspoons rried mango powder (amchur)
  - 1/2 tablespoons coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala Salt to taste
  - 8-10 fresh coriander sprigs to garnish
  - 1/2 tablespoon lemon juice

METHOD:
  1. To make the kadai masala, dry roast coriander seeds, fennel seeds, 2 dried chillies and 1 tsp cumin seeds till fragrant.
  2. Remove from heat, cool and grind to a coarse powder.
  3. Heat mustard oil in a non-stick kadai till it begins to smoke.
  4. Cool it slightly, add bay leaves and remaining dried chillies and sauté for 10 seconds.
  5. Add green chillies and remaining cumin seeds, mix and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  6. Add tomato puree, mix well and cook for 2 minutes.
  7. Add red chilli powder, dried mango powder, turmeric powder, coriander powder and chaat masala and mix well.
  8. Add salt and mix.
  9. Roughly chop tomatoes, add, mix and cook till they turn soft and pulpy.
  10. Add ginger strips and mix well.
  11. Add brown Bengal gram and mix.
  12. Add water as required, mix and cook for 5-6 minutes.
  13. Chop some coriander sprigs, add and mix.
  14. Add the kadai masala and lemon juice and mix well.
  15. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with ginger strips and coriander sprigs and serve hot.

RECIPE 98: Kaddu ki Khatti Meethi Subzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Kaddu-ki-Khatti-Meethi-Subzi-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Red pumpkin is a vegetable not many like to eat, but when cooked this way they will not be able to resist This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Red pumpkin (kaddu), Tamarind paste | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 10-15 minutes | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet &amp; Sour | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 inch cubes
  - 3 tablespoons tamarind paste
  - 1/2 cup grated jaggery
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger ,
  - 1-2 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1/4 teaspoon asafoetida
  - 1/4 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 2 teaspoons garam masala powder Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander leaves ,
  - 1 green chilli , slit Fresh coriander sprig for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add ginger and green chillies, mix and sauté till fragrant.
  2. Add asafoetida, mix and sauté for a minute.
  3. Add pumpkin cubes and cook for 4-5 minutes.
  4. Add turmeric powder, red chilli powder, 1 tsp garam masala powder and salt, mix well and sauté for a few minutes.
  5. Add tamarind paste and jaggery, mix and cook till the jaggery melts.
  6. Add some water, mix, cover and cook for 8-10 minutes.
  7. Mash the pumpkins slightly, add coriander leaves and remaining garam masala powder and mix well.
  8. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with slit green chilli and coriander sprig and serve hot.

RECIPE 99: Kalakand Fruit Custard
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Kalakand-Fruit-Custard-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

If you have lots of leftover kalakand, don’t despair. Just follow this recipe and turn out a unique dessert This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Kalakand, Red apple | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups Milk
  - 4-5 tablespoons Caster sugar to garnish Orange segments to garnish Fresh pomegranate pears to garnish Red grapes , seeded and halved

METHOD:
  1. Roughly chop walnuts.
  2. Dry roast the walnuts in a non-stick pan till crisp.
  3. Transfer into a bowl.
  4. Take milk in another bowl, add custard powder and mix well.
  5. Transfer the custard mixture into a deep non-stick pan and cook on medium heat, whisking continuously till the mixture starts thickening and reaches pouring consistency.
  6. Add castor sugar.
  7. Break kalakand pieces and add and mix well with a whisk till the mixture thickens further.
  8. Add half the roasted walnuts and apple and mix well.
  9. Pour half the custard into a deep serving plate.
  10. Add pears and pour the remaining custard mixture.
  11. Garnish with orange segments, pomegranate pearls, remaining roasted walnuts and red grapes.
  12. Refrigerate for 1-2 hours or till set.
  13. Serve chilled.

RECIPE 100: Kale Chane ki Kadhi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/kale-chane-ki-kadhi-7081206

Kale chane simmered in a flavoured curd gravy and served with steamed rice is an absolute soul food. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Rajasthani | Course: Dals and Kadhis Prep time 25-30 minutes | Cook Time: 20-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups yogurt
  - 2 tablespoons gram flour (besan) ½ teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 2 teaspoons coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 2 green chillies, chopped
  - 2 tablespoons ghee
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing)
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves Red chilli oil for drizzling Steamed rice to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take yogurt in a large bowl, add gram flour, turmeric powder, salt, red chilli powder, coriander powder, garam masala powder and green chillies and whisk till a lump free mixture is formed.
  2. Add 3 cups water and mix well.
  3. Heat ghee in a deep pan.
  4. Add cumin seeds and let them change colour.
  5. Add asafoetida and cook for a few seconds.
  6. Add boiled brown chickpeas and mix well.
  7. Add the yogurt mixture and mix well.
  8. Cook for 10-15 minutes or till done.
  9. Add coriander leaves, mix and cook for 1 minute.
  10. Transfer the kadhi into a serving bowl and serve hot with steamed rice.

RECIPE 101: Kale Chane with Rajgira Puri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/kale-chane-with-rajgira-puri-cook-smart-4772991

Whole black gram soaked and cooked with simple spices. This flavourful bowl is best had with rajgira puris. This recipe featured on Food Food Channel.

Main Ingredients: Black Bengal Gram, Amaranth Flour, Potatoes | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main Course- Vegetarain Prep time 8-10 hours | Cook Time: 20-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups black Bengal gram (kale chane), soaked overnight, drained and boiled in fresh water
  - 1 cup amaranth (rajgira) flour
  - 1 tablespoon +
  - 1 teaspoon oil + for deep-frying
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 tablespoon coriander powder Black salt to taste ½ teaspoon red chilli powder ¼ cup black gram stock ½ medium potato, boiled and peeled Salt to taste

METHOD:
  1. Heat 1 tbsp oil in a non-stick pan, add cumin seeds and once the seeds change colour, add ginger and sauté for ½ a minute.
  2. Add coriander powder and mix well.
  3. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  4. Add black gram, black salt, red chilli powder and black Bengal gram stock to the pan and mix well.
  5. Cook till the black gram is done.
  6. Put amaranth flour into a bowl, grate potato into it.
  7. Add salt and mix well.
  8. Add ½ cup water and knead into a soft dough.
  9. Add 1 tsp oil and knead again.
  10. Divide the dough into equal portions, shape them into balls and roll out into small pooris.
  11. Deep-fry pooris in hot oil till brown and crisp on both the sides.
  12. Drain on absorbent paper.
  13. Transfer the chane into a serving bowl, place it on one side of the serving plate, place fried pooris on the other side and serve immediately.

RECIPE 102: Kapnya
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Kapnya.html

Traditional Maharashtrian snack – ideally should be served with cups of hot tea This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Whole wheat flour (gehun ka atta), Jaggery | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Whole wheat flour (gehun ka atta)
  - 1/4 cup Jaggery , chopped
  - 1/4 cup Gram flour (besan) a pinch Salt
  - 1/2 tablespoon Fennel sees (saunf)
  - 1/2 tbsp + to deep fry Hot oil to sprinkle Poppy seeds

METHOD:
  1. Heat ¼ cup water in a deep non-stick pan, add jaggery and cook till it melts.
  2. Take whole wheat flour in a bowl, add gram flour, salt, fennel seeds and hot oil and mix well.
  3. Add the jaggery mixture and knead into stiff dough.
  4. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  5. Roll out the dough into a thin disk and sprinkle poppy seeds on top.
  6. Press lightly.
  7. Cut into diamonds, slide them into hot oil and deep fry, on medium heat, till crisp.
  8. Drain on absorbent paper.
  9. Allow to cool and serve or store in airtight containers.

RECIPE 103: Karachi Halwa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Karachi-Halwa-KhaanaKhazana.html

Chewy rich halwa. This recipe has featured on the show Khanakhazana.

Main Ingredients: Cornflour, Sugar | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Difficult | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/4 cup Cornflour Sugar
  - 2 cups Sugar
  - 1-2 drops Orange essence
  - 10-12 Pistachios finely chopped

METHOD:
  1. Dissolve cornflour in three fourth cup of water.
  2. Grease a tray.
  3. Mix sugar with one cup of water and bring it to a boil.
  4. Add lemon juice, bring it to a boil again and then remove scum.
  5. Add edible orange colour and mix.
  6. Reduce heat to medium, add a little cornflour mixture and stir continuously.
  7. When it boils add a little cornflour mixture again.
  8. Continue the same process until all the cornflour mixture is used up.
  9. Cook till mixture is thickened and starts sticking.
  10. Reduce heat to low.
  11. Add a little melted ghee to it and mix well.
  12. When ghee is absorbed, add a little more and let it absorb.
  13. Continue till all the ghee is used up.
  14. Take one teaspoon of mixture onto a plate, cool it and if it does not stick to the plate, remove pan from heat.
  15. Add rose water, mix well and then spread it on a greased tray.
  16. Sprinkle chopped almonds and pistachios on top.
  17. Cut into desired size and shape.
  18. Serve when cool.
  19. Nutrition Info Calories 3434 Carbohydrates 576.8 Protein 21.9 Fat 115

RECIPE 104: Kayloli
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Kayloli.html

Dosa with a twist! Enjoy a tantalizing snack with spiced batter, promising a deliciously unique flavor experience. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Rice flour, Semolina | Cuisine: Karnataka | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups rice flour ½ cup semolina (rawa)
  - 1½ cups milk Oil for cooking Coconut chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take rice flour in a bowl, add semolina, green chillies, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, salt and mix well.
  2. Add milk, 1½ cups water and mix well.
  3. Set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  4. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  5. Spread a ladleful of batter evenly.
  6. Drizzle some oil around and cook on medium heat for 2-3 minutes or till the underside is golden brown.
  7. Flip and cook on other side for 2-3 minutes more.
  8. Serve hot with coconut chutney.

RECIPE 105: Kharzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/kharzi-8699855

Check out this cheesy and easy Rice recipe kharzi from Arunachal Pradesh. Mozzarella cheese, chillies and ginger are blended to make a fine paste. Then cooked rice is tossed in this paste along with spring onion.

Cuisine: Arunachal Pradesh | Course: Rice Prep time 35-40 minutes | Cook Time: 8-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 inch ginger, chopped
  - 2 spring onion bulbs, chopped Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 3 cups cooked rice
  - 2 tablespoons chopped spring onion greens + for garnish
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli flakes

METHOD:
  1. Transfer mozzarella cheese in a blender jar.
  2. Drain dried red chillies and add along with ginger.
  3. Add ¾ cup water and grind to a fine paste.
  4. Heat oil in a nonstick pan.
  5. Add spring onion bulbs and sauté for a minute.
  6. Add the prepared paste and sauté for 3-4 minutes.
  7. Add salt, crushed black peppercorns and mix well.
  8. Add rice and mix well.
  9. Cook for 2-3 minutes.
  10. Add spring onion greens, red chilli flakes and mix well.
  11. Serve hot garnished with spring onion greens.
