RECIPE 107: Kuttu ka Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/kuttu-ka-parantha-6595457

A healthy and wholesome buckwheat flour paratha. Kuttu ka paratha is a flatbread that can be eaten with some condiment or as it is alone. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 20-25 minutes | Cook Time: 8-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup buckwheat flour (kuttu)
  - 4 medium potatoes, boiled and peeled ½ cup chopped fresh coriander leaves ¼ cup roasted and crushed peanuts Rock salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon ginger-green chilli paste Ghee as required

METHOD:
  1. Grate potatoes in a bowl.
  2. Add chopped coriander, peanuts, rock salt, ginger-green chilli paste and buckwheat flour and mix well.
  3. Add some water and knead into a stiff dough.
  4. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 15 minutes.
  5. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape them into balls.
  6. Put some ghee on a non-stick tawa.
  7. Place a ball over, dip palms in water and spread the ball to make a thin disc.
  8. Switch on the heat, spread some ghee, cover and cook from both sides on medium heat till golden and crisp.
  9. Serve hot.

RECIPE 108: Lachchedar Aloo Tikki Chaat
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Lachchedar-Aloo-Tikki-Chaat-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A very popular chaat in North India – potato tikkis served with yogurt and other chaat ingredients. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Potatoes, Yogurt | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 large potatoes, boiled and peeled
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 4 green chillies, finely chopped Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala + to sprinkle
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder + to sprinkle
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ½ teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 1½ tablespoons powdered sugar
  - 1 teaspoon rose water Tamarind chutney as required Green chutney as required Nylon sev as required Pomegranate pearls as required Fresh mint sprig for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Grate potatoes into a bowl.
  2. Add ginger, green chillies, salt, chaat masala, red chilli powder, cumin seeds, carom seeds and raisins and mix the mixture lightly.
  3. Divide the mixture equal portions and shape them into tikkis.
  4. Heat ghee in a pan, add the tikkis and shallow fry, turning sides, on medium heat till evenly golden brown on both sides.
  5. They should be soft from inside and crisp on the outside.
  6. Take yogurt in a bowl, add powdered sugar and rose water and mix well.Drain tikkis on absorbent paper.
  7. Spread a spoon of yogurt mixture on a serving platter with back of a spoon.
  8. Place tikkis over it, drizzle yogurt, a spoon of tamarind chutney and few drops of green chutney over the tikkis.
  9. Sprinkle sev and add pomegranate pearls on top.
  10. Sprinkle chaat masala and red chilli powder.
  11. Garnish with a mint sprig and serve immediately.

RECIPE 109: Lachchedar Mathri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Lachchedar-Mathri-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Crispy layers of indulgence, boasting a flaky texture and a tantalizing blend of spices for a snack that's both crunchy and addictive. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida), Carom seeds (ajwain) | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups refined flour (maida) + for dusting
  - 1 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 1 teaspoon crushed black peppercorns Salt to taste
  - 6 tablespoons ghee + as required Green Thai curry paste as required Red Thai curry paste as required Oil for greasing and brushing

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 180˚ C.
  2. Mix together refined flour, carom seeds, crushed peppercorns, salt and 6 tablespoons ghee in a bowl.
  3. Add water as required and knead into a stiff dough.
  4. Divide the dough into two equal portions and roll out each into a thin sheet.
  5. Spread some green Thai curry paste on one sheet, top with some ghee, dust some flour and roll into a cylinder.
  6. Spread some red Thai curry paste on the other sheet, top with some ghee, dust some flour and roll into a cylinder.
  7. Cut both cylinders into 1 inch pieces and flatten out each piece into small discs or mathris.
  8. Grease a baking tray with some oil and place the mathris on it.
  9. Brush the mathris with ghee on top.
  10. Place the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 15-20 minutes.
  11. Remove from oven, brush some ghee, flip and brush some more ghee on mathris.
  12. Put the tray back in the preheated oven and bake for 5-6 minutes.
  13. Remove from oven and cool.
  14. Arrange the mathris on a serving platter and serve or store in an airtight container to serve when required.

RECIPE 110: Leftover Dal Appe
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/leftover-dal-appe-7368439

Wondering how to give your leftover dal a makeover? We’ve got the perfect recipe for you! Transform it into crispy and delicious 'Dal Appe' by following this simple and easy recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 20-25 minutes | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups leftover dal ¼ cup blanched and crushed green peas ¼ cup grated carrots
  - 1 cup semolina (suji)
  - 2 green chillies, crushed Salt to taste
  - 2-3 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 2-3 tablespoons yogurt ½ teaspoon baking soda Ghee as required Coconut chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take leftover dal in a bowl.
  2. Add green peas, carrots, semolina, green chillies, salt, coriander, yogurt and 1 cup water and mix well.
  3. Set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  4. Add baking soda and mix well.
  5. Heat a paniyaram pan and drizzle ghee.
  6. Put a spoonful of batter in each dent, cover and cook for 5-6 minutes.
  7. Flip and cook for 5-6 minutes more.
  8. Serve hot with coconut chutney.

RECIPE 111: Leftover Rice Muthia
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/leftover-rice-muthia-7368412

A delicious snack using leftover rice, gram flour and a few Indian spices to enjoy during your chai-time. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 8-10 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups leftover cooked rice ½ cup gram flour (besan)
  - 1½ teaspoons coriander Powder Salt to taste ½ teaspoon turmeric powder ¼ teaspoon red chilli powder ¼ teaspoon cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon sugar ¼ cup yogurt A pinch of baking soda
  - 2 teaspoons oil
  - 3 tablespoons whole wheat flour Tempering
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 1 teaspoon mustard seeds
  - 10-15 curry leaves
  - 2-3 green chillies, slit
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves

METHOD:
  1. Take rice in a bowl, add gram flour, ginger-green chilli paste, coriander powder, salt, turmeric powder, chilli powder, cumin powder, sugar and yogurt and mix well.
  2. Add baking soda and oil, mix well.
  3. Add whole wheat flour and knead into soft dough.
  4. To make muthia, grease your palms with oil, take a portion of the dough and shape into a cylinder.
  5. Heat sufficient water in a steamer.
  6. Place the muthia in the steamer basket and steam for 12-15 minutes.
  7. Switch the heat off and allow to cool completely.
  8. Cut muthiya into 1 inch roundels.
  9. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add mustard seeds once they splutter, add cumin seeds, sesame seeds, asafoetida, curry leaves and green chillies and sauté for a few seconds.
  10. Add muthiya roundels and coriander leaves and toss well.
  11. Take the pan off the heat and transfer into a serving bowl.
  12. Serve hot.

RECIPE 112: Leftover Roti Halwa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/leftover-roti-halwa-7368579

You wont believe that you can make such a delicious and amazing halwa with your leftover Rotis. It is a very quick and simple recipe. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Desserts Prep time 6-8 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8 leftover rotis
  - 2 tablespoons ghee
  - 1 cup milk ½ cup sugar ¼ teaspoon green cardamom powder A pinch of salt
  - 1 tablespoon chopped almonds
  - 1 tablespoon chopped cashew nuts
  - 1 tablespoon chopped pistachios + for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Put the rotis in a blender jar and blend to a coarse powder.
  2. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan, add the bended powder and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  3. Add milk, mix and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  4. Add sugar, mix and cook for 3-4 minutes.
  5. Add almonds, cashew nuts and pistachios and mix well.
  6. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  7. Serve warm garnished with pistachios.

RECIPE 113: Leftover Upma Cutlets
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/leftover-upma-cutlets-7368651

Got leftover upma? Make these stunning tikkis and enjoy a fabulous snack! Serve these cutlets hot with tomato ketchup. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 8-10 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups leftover rava upma
  - 1 tablespoon oil + for shallow frying
  - 1 tablespoon butter
  - 2-3 garlic cloves, chopped
  - 2 spring onion bulbs, finely chopped with the greens ½ cup chopped cabbage
  - 1 medium carrot, chopped
  - 1 medium capsicum, chopped Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste ¼ teaspoon chaat masala ½ teaspoon red chilli flakes ½ teaspoon roasted cumin powder
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves ½ lemon ¼ cup bread crumbs Tomato ketchup to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil and butter in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add garlic and green chilli and sauté for a few seconds.
  3. Add chopped spring onion bulbs and sauté for a few seconds.
  4. Add cabbage, carrot, capsicum and a pinch of salt and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  5. Add crushed black peppercorns, chaat masala, and red chilli flakes and roasted cumin powder and mix well.
  6. Take the pan off the heat and allow this mixture to cool slightly.
  7. Take the leftover upma in a large bowl.
  8. Add the vegetable mixture, coriander leaves, spring onion greens and squeeze the juice of lemon.
  9. Add bread crumbs and mix well.
  10. Take a portion of the mixture and shape it into a ball and gently flatten it to make triangle shaped cutlets.
  11. Heat sufficient oil in a shallow pan.
  12. Place the cutlets and cook for 1-2 minutes on each side till golden brown and crisp.
  13. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  14. Serve hot with tomato ketchup.

RECIPE 114: Lotus Stem Honey Crunch
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Lotus-Stem-Honey-Crunch-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Indulge in the tantalizing combination of crispy lotus stem slices delicately coated in the rich sweetness of honey. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Lotus stems (bhen/bhee, bhein), Honey | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 250 gms lotus stems (kamal kakdi/bhein), scrubbed clean Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon cornflour
  - 6 dried Kashmiri red chillies
  - 3 tablespoons tomato ketchup
  - 3-4 stalks of spring onion greens
  - 1 teaspoon vinegar

METHOD:
  1. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  2. Cut lotus stems into thin diagonal slices and put them in a bowl.
  3. Add salt, cornflour and mix well.
  4. Slide these into hot oil, taking care not to crowd the kadai, and deep fry till crisp and golden.
  5. Drain on absorbent paper.
  6. Roughly chop red chillies and remove seeds.
  7. Heat 2 tablespoons oil in a non stick wok, add red chillies and sauté.
  8. Add tomato ketchup, honey and salt and mix.
  9. Chop spring onion greens.
  10. Add fried lotus stems to the sauce and toss.
  11. Add vinegar and mix.
  12. Transfer into a serving dish, garnish with spring onion greens and serve hot.

RECIPE 115: Malai Broccoli
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Malai-Broccoli-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Broccoli florets marinated with fresh cream and some spices and cooked on the barbecue This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Broccoli florets, Cream cheese | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8-10 large broccoli florets, blanched
  - 2 tablespoons ginger-garlic paste
  - 3 tablespoons fresh cream Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste ½ lemonDressing
  - 2 tablespoons cream cheese ½ tablespoon finely chopped garlic Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 2 teaspoons mustard sauce
  - 2-3 tablespoons milk Salad to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take ginger-garlic paste, fresh cream and salt in a large bowl and mix well.
  2. Add crushed black peppercorns and mix well.
  3. Squeeze the juice of ½ lemon and mix well.
  4. Add broccoli pieces and mix well so that all the broccoli florets are well coated with the marinade.
  5. Light sufficient charcoal in a barbeque, meanwhile, skewer the broccoli pieces on skewers and place them on the barbeque grill and cook for 10-12 minutes.
  6. To make the dressing, take cream cheese, garlic, crushed black peppercorns and mustard sauce in a bowl and mix well.
  7. Add milk and mix.

RECIPE 116: Masala Aloo Kulcha + Tamatar ki Chutney
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Masala-Aloo-Kulcha-+-Tamatar-ki-Chutney-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Kulchas stuffed with a spicy potato mixture and cooked and served with a pungent tomato chutney – absolutely delicious This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Whole wheat flour (atta), Potatoes, Tomatoes | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup whole wheat flour (atta) ½ cup refined flour (maida) + for dusting
  - 2½ tablespoons Oil + as required Filling
  - 2 medium potatoes, boiled and peeled
  - 1 tablespoon coriander seeds
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds (jeera)
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 2-3 green chillies, finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped fresh mint leaves
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 1 tablespoon oilTamatar ki chutney
  - 2 medium tomatoes (tamatar), finely chopped
  - 3 tablespoons tomato ketchup
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala Juice of ½ lemon
  - 2 tablespoons finely chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 2 teaspoons sugar

METHOD:
  1. Mix together wheat flour, refined flour, carom seeds, salt and 2 tablespoons oil in a parat.
  2. Add water as required and knead a soft dough.
  3. Add remaining oil, knead and set aside.
  4. To make the filling, dry roast coriander seeds and cumin seeds till fragrant.
  5. Crush in a mortar with pestle to a coarse powder and put in a bowl.
  6. Add ginger, green chillies, chilli powder, dried mango powder, onion, coriander leaves, mint leaves, potatoes and garam masala powder.
  7. Mash and mix well.
  8. Add oil and mix again.
  9. To make the tamatar ki chutney, mix together tomatoes, tomato ketchup, chilli powder, dried mango powder, chaat masala, lemon juice, coriander leaves and sugar in a bowl.
  10. Place an aluminium kadai upside down on heat.
  11. Divide the dough into equal portions and brush with some oil.
  12. Stuff each with a portion of the filling and shape into balls.
  13. Dust the worktop with some refined and sprinkle some coriander leaves on it.
  14. Place the stuffed balls on it and flatten them into discs.
  15. Apply some oil on the inverted kadai, stick the kulchas on it and roast till fully done, basting with oil.
  16. Serve hot with tamatar ki chutney.

RECIPE 117: Masala Rawa Puri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Masala-Rawa-Puri.html

These super crisp puris are made with a dough of rawa and some spice powders This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Fine semolina (barik rawa), Ginger-green chilli paste | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Fine semolina (barik rawa)
  - 2 teaspoons Ginger-green chilli paste
  - 1 teaspoon Red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon Coriander powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Cumin powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon Turmeric powder to taste Salt for greasi to deep fry Oil to serve Chai

METHOD:
  1. Put the semolina in a mixer jar and grind to a fine powder.
  2. Transfer into a large bowl.
  3. Add ginger-green chilli paste, red chilli powder, coriander powder, cumin powder, turmeric powder and salt and mix well.
  4. Add ½ cup water and knead into soft dough.
  5. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  6. Grease the worktop with some oil.
  7. To make puris, divide the dough into small equal portions and shape them into balls.
  8. Roll out each ball, on the greased worktop, into a small thin disc.
  9. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  10. Gently slide the discs, one at a time, into the hot oil and deep fry till they puff up and turn crisp.
  11. Drain on absorbent paper.
  12. Arrange them on a serving platter and serve hot with chai.

RECIPE 118: Mawa Gujiya
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Mawa-Gujiya-SK-Khazana.html

These gujiyas stuffed with a rich stuffing is a must at Holi celebrations. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Khoya/mawa, Castor sugar | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups Khoya/mawa grated
  - 2 tablespoons Castor sugar
  - 1 tablespoon Walnuts chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Cashewnuts chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Dried figs chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Almonds chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Dates chopped
  - 2 cups Refined flour (maida)
  - 3 tablespoons Ghee to deep fry Oil

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick pan.
  2. Add khoya and castor sugar, mix and cook till khoya melts.
  3. Add walnuts, cashewnuts, figs, almonds and dates, mix well and cook for a minute.
  4. Remove from heat and set aside to cool.
  5. Knead together flour and 3 tablespoons ghee with sufficient cold water to a stiff dough.
  6. Divide the dough into equal portions, grease with some ghee and roll out into small discs.
  7. Stuff each disc with a portion of khoya mixture and shape into gujiyas.
  8. Heat sufficient ghee in a kadai.
  9. Deep-fry gujiyas on medium heat till golden brown.
  10. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  11. Serve hot.

RECIPE 119: Mawa Muffin with Shrikhand Frosting
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Mawa-Muffin-with-Shrikhand-Frosting-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A jolly good fusion of two different cuisines. The little ones are going to gobble up these muffins within no time This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Mawa / khoya, Refined flour (maida) | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 150 grams Mawa / khoya , grated
  - 160 grams Refined flour (maida)
  - 120 grams Butter , softened
  - 200 grams Sweet condensed milk
  - 1/2 teaspoon Baking powder
  - 75 millilitres Milk
  - 1 teaspoon Vanilla essence as required Kesar shrikhand to garnish Sutarfeni to garnish Wafer biscuits to garnish Chocolate chips to garnish Small carrot triangles , blanched

METHOD:
  1. Preheat the oven to 180° C.
  2. Take butter in a bowl and cream it lightly with an electric hand blender.
  3. Add khoya and continue to cream with the hand blender at a low speed.
  4. Add condensed milk and mix well.
  5. Sift together refined flour, baking powder and baking soda into another bowl.
  6. Gradually add this flour mixture to the butter mixture and mix in cut and fold method ensuring there are no lumps formed.
  7. Add milk and vanilla essence and continue to mix.
  8. Put this mixture into muffin moulds till they are ¾ full.
  9. Keep the moulds on a baking tray.
  10. Keep the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 20-25 minutes.
  11. Remove the tray from the oven and let them cool down to room temperature.
  12. Remove the muffins from the moulds and keep them on a serving plate.
  13. Put the shrikhand in a piping bag and pipe out over each muffins.
  14. Garnish each muffin with sutarfeni, a wafer biscuit, chocolate chips and carrot triangles and serve.

RECIPE 120: Mawa Wale Aloo
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Mawa-Wale-Aloo-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A rich potato dish fit for a royal banquet. Rich gravy made from mawa, tomatoes and Indian spices and cooked with potatoes. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Mawa, Potatoes | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup grated mawa + to garnish
  - 4 medium potatoes , boiled and peeled
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 1 tbsp +
  - 1 teaspoon ghee
  - 1/4 cup raisins
  - 1/4 cup cashewnuts , roughly chopped
  - 2 medium onions , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 1/2 teaspoons red chilli powder
  - 2 tablespoons coriander powder
  - 1 tablespoon garam masala powder
  - 1 teaspoon cumin powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 3 tablespoons roughly crushed cashewnuts
  - 1 cup milk
  - 2-3 green chillies , finely chopped

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil and 2 tbsps ghee in a deep non-stick pan.
  2. Cut the potatoes into thick slices, add to the pan and cook on medium heat shallow-fry, turning sides, till potatoes turn light golden brown on both sides.
  3. Drain into a bowl and set aside.
  4. Add raisins to the same pan, sauté for a few seconds.
  5. Drain into another bowl.
  6. Add ¼ cup roughly chopped cashewnuts to the same pan and sauté till lightly brown.
  7. Drain into a bowl.
  8. Add onions, ginger and garlic to the same pan and sauté till onions turn golden brown.
  9. Add tomatoes, salt, red chilli powder, coriander powder, garam masala powder and cumin powder and mix well.
  10. Add turmeric powder and crushed cashewnuts, mix and cook till tomatoes are pulpy.
  11. Switch off heat and transfer the mixture into a blender and ½ cup milk and blend to a fine paste.
  12. Switch on heat, add remaining ghee and green chillies to the same pan.
  13. Add remaining milk to the ground mixture and add the mixture to the pan.
  14. Rinse the blender jar with ½ cup water and add to the remaining gravy.
  15. Add ½ cup water to the gravy and mix well.
  16. Add the fried potatoes, half the fried cashewnuts, 1 tbsp fried raisins and mawa, mix and cook on medium heat for 4-5 minutes.
  17. Transfer into a serving plate, garnish with mawa, remaining fried cashewnuts and remaining fried raisins.
  18. Serve hot.

RECIPE 121: Methi Tamatar ki Sabzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Methi-Tamatar-ki-Sabzi-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A healthy meal – fenugreek and tomatoes cooked with tomatoes, Indian spices and served with missi rotis. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fenugreek leaves (methi), Tomatoes | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 20-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 Large bunch fenugreek leaves (methi) , cleaned
  - 2-3 medium tomatoes , finely chopped
  - 2 tbsps mustard oil + for drizzling
  - 1/2 teaspoon asafoetida
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 tablespoon chopped ginger
  - 1 tablespoon chopped garlic
  - 2-3 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 2 medium onions , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste Readymade missi roti dough as required Whole wheat flour (atta) for dusting
  - 1 tablespoon lemon juice Fresh mint leaves to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat kachchi ghani mustard oil in a metal kadai till it begins to smoke.
  2. Cool it slightly, add asafoetida, cumin seeds, ginger and garlic, mix and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  3. Add green chillies and onions, mix and sauté till onions turn translucent.
  4. Add fenugreek leaves and mix well.
  5. Add coriander powder, red chilli powder, turmeric powder and salt, mix and sauté for 4-5 minutes.
  6. Add tomatoes, mash and cook till it turns soft and pulpy.
  7. Divide the dough into equal portions and roll out into medium size discs or rotis dusting with flour.
  8. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  9. Place the discs on it, one at a time, and roast till well browned and evenly cooked from both the sides.
  10. Keep them on a serving platter.
  11. Add lemon juice to the sabzi and mix well.
  12. Drizzle some mustard oil on top.
  13. Brush some mustard oil on the missi rotis Transfer sabzi into a serving bowl, garnish with mint leaves and serve hot with missi rotis.

RECIPE 122: Methi Thalipeeth
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Methi-Thalipeeth-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A nutritious Indian flatbread made with fenugreek leaves and a blend of spices, cooked to perfection on a griddle, offering a delightful burst of flavors in every bite. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fresh fenugreek leaves (methi), Bhajanee flour | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 cups bhajnee flour Salt to taste
  - 1 medium onion, chopped ½ teaspoon turmeric powder Ghee as required Yogurt to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take fenugreek leaves in a bowl, add salt and set aside.
  2. Take bhajnee flour, onion, turmeric powder and salt in a mixing bowl.
  3. Squeeze water from the methi leaves and add to the bhajnee mixture.
  4. Add sufficient water and knead to medium soft dough.
  5. Place a plastic sheet on a worktop and grease it with ghee.
  6. Take a big portion of mixture and place it on the sheet.
  7. Apply ghee on another sheet, place it over the mixture and flatten the mixture.
  8. Make more thalipeeth with the remaining mixture in the same way.
  9. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  10. Place a star shaped cookie cutter over the thalipeeth and cut out stars.
  11. Gently remove the cut outs and place them on the heated tawa.
  12. Make a cavity in centre of each star.
  13. Pour little ghee into the cavities and shallow fry, turning sides, till crisp.
  14. Serve hot with yogurt.

========================================================================

A fusion delight blending the tangy, spicy flavors of traditional Indian pani puri with the creamy richness of Mexican cheese. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Processed cheese, Crisp puris | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

  - 24 crisp puris
  - 4 tablespoons oil
  - 2 medium onions, finely chopped
  - 1mediumgreen capsicum, chopped
  - 2 medium tomatoes, chopped
  - 1cup corn kernels, boiled
  - 1 cup green peas, blanched Salt to taste ¾ cup tomato ketchup
  - 3 tablespoons red chilli sauce
  - 1 tablespoon +
  - 2 teaspoons dried mixed herbs + to sprinkle
  - 1tablespoon +
  - 2 teaspoons red chilli flakes + to sprinkle
  - 2 cups milk ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder Chaat masala to sprinkle Micro greens for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add onions,capsicum, tomatoes, corn kernels, green peas, salt, tomato ketchup, red chilli sauce, 1tablespoon mixed herbs and 1tablespoon red chilli flakes and sauté on medium heatfor 2-3 minutes.
  2. Transfer the filling into a bowl.
  3. Add processed cheese cubesand mix well.
  4. To prepare cheese sauce, heat milk in a non-stick pan.

RECIPE 124: Millet Phirni
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/millet-phirni-6712583

This is the recipe for the classic sweet pudding with a healthy twist - Black Raisin & Millet Phirni, Yumm! This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Desserts Prep time 2-2.5 hours | Cook Time: 20-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 cups milk ¼ cup barnyard millet (samo) ¼ cup sugar ½ teaspoon green cardamom powder Silver warq for garnish Blanched, peeled, and slivered pistachios for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Take ProV Premium Black Raisins in a bowl.
  2. Add 1 cup water, set aside to soak for 10-15 minutes.
  3. Bring milk to a boil in a deep non-stick pan.
  4. Add barnyard millet, mix and cook for 8-10 minutes while stirring in between.
  5. Meanwhile, put the soaked raisins into a blender jar and blend to a fine paste.
  6. Once the millet is cooked and the mixture thickens, add the blended paste and mix well.
  7. Add sugar, mix and cook for 2-3 minutes or till sugar melts.
  8. Add green cardamom powder and mix well.
  9. Switch the heat off, transfer into individual serving earthen bowls and allow to cool.
  10. Once cooled, refrigerate for 1-2 hours or till chilled.
  11. Garnish with silver warq, ProV Premium Black Raisins and slivered pistachios.

RECIPE 125: Mini Uttapam
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Mini-Uttapam-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

An integral part of South Indian breakfast snack menu, these uttapams are made especially to lure the kids to eat healthy. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Finger millet (ragi) flour, Rice flour | Cuisine: South Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup finger millet (ragi) flour ¼ cup rice flour
  - 1½ cups yogurt Salt to taste A pinch of asafoetida (hing) ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder Oil to cook ¼ cup boiled green peas ½ medium carrot, peeled cut into small triangles and blanched ½ medium beetroot, peeled cut into small crescents and blanched Sambhar to serve Coconut chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take nachni flour, rice flour, urad dal flour and yogurt in a bowl and mix well.
  2. Add sufficient water and make a semi thick batter.
  3. Set aside to ferment overnight.
  4. Add salt, asafoetida and turmeric powder to the batter and mix well.
  5. Heat oil in a non-stick pan and spread small portions of batter with a small spoon.
  6. Place 2 green peas as eyes, small carrot piece as nose, small beetroot crescent as smiling face.
  7. Press slightly and turn it over and cook on other side.
  8. Cook on medium heat till golden brown on both sides Line a serving platter with a banana leaf.
  9. Transfer the uttapams on it.
  10. Serve hot with sambhar and coconut chutney.

RECIPE 126: Mixed Palak Soya Saag
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Mixed-Palak-Soya-Saag-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Rich in all the essential nutrients, this delicious dish is a winner. A seasonal recipe made from spinach and mustard leaves. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fresh spinach leaves, Fresh mustard leaves | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium bunches fresh spinach leaves , shredded
  - 2 medium bunches fresh mustard leaves , shredded
  - 1 medium bunch fresh bathua leves , roughly chopped
  - 1 medium bunch fresh fenugreek leaves , shredded
  - 2 cups soya chunks , soaked and boiled
  - 4 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 2-3 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 2 medium onions , finely chopped
  - 1/2 tablespoons coriander powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder + to sprinkle
  - 1 teaspoon lemon juice Cottage cheese (paneer) , grated to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat soya oil in a metal kadai, add cumin seeds and sauté till fragrant.
  2. Add ginger, garlic and sauté till garlic turns light brown.
  3. Add green chillies and onions, mix and sauté till onions turn light brown.
  4. Add tomatoes and mix.
  5. Add salt, mix well and cook till tomatoes turn soft and pulpy.
  6. Add coriander powder, turmeric powder, cumin powder, red chilli powder and garam masala powder, mix and cook till the oil separates.
  7. Add spinach leaves, mustard leaves, bathua leaves and fenugreek leaves, mix well and cook till the leaves wilt.
  8. Transfer half the cooked saag into a blender jar leaving the remaining in the kadai, blend into a fine paste and add back to the kadai.
  9. Mix well.
  10. Add water as required mix well.
  11. Add soya chunks, mix well and cook on low heat for 6-8 minutes.
  12. Add lemon juice and mix well.
  13. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with cottage cheese, sprinkle some garam masala powder on top and serve hot.

RECIPE 127: Moongphalli ka Halwa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Moongphalli-ka-Halwa-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Halwas can be made variously and this one is as tasty as the rest of them This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Peanuts (moongphalli), Peanut butter | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 0-5 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/4 cup Peanuts (moongphalli)
  - 3/4 cup Peanut butter
  - 1/2 cup Ghee
  - 1/4 cup Semolina (suji/rawa)
  - 1/2 cup Jaggery , grated
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder a pinch Saffron strands
  - 1 cup Khoya (mawa)

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan, add semolina and sauté till fragrant.
  2. Meanwhile heat another non-stick pan, add some water, jaggery and green cardamom powder, mix and cook, stirring, till jaggery melts.
  3. Add peanuts and peanut butter to the semolina and mix well.
  4. Add jaggery water and cook till the mixture thicken, stirring continuously.
  5. Add saffron and mix.
  6. Add khoya and mix till it melts.
  7. Transfer into a serving bowl and serve warm.

RECIPE 128: Mughal Sarai Dal Kachori
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Mughal-Sarai-Dal-Kachori-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Deep fried spicy moong dal stuffed kachoris served with a tangy chutney This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Split skinless green gram (dhuli moong dal), Readymade kachori dough | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 1.30-2 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 hour and boiled with turmeric powder and salt
  - 250 grams readymade kachori dough
  - 2 tablespoons oil + for deep-frying
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds (jeera)
  - 1 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 1 teaspoon fennel seeds (saunf)
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1½ tablespoons coriander powder
  - 1½ teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 1 small potato, boiled, peeled and mashed
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped Salt to tasteChutney
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon fennel seeds (saunf)
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds (jeera)
  - 1 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 3 tablespoons tamarind paste
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder ½ cup sugar
  - 1 small potato, boiled and finely chopped
  - 1 small onion, finely choppedA few fresh coriander sprigs

METHOD:
  1. To make filling, heat 2 tablespoons oil in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add cumin seeds and sauté till fragrant.
  3. Add carom seeds, fennel seeds and ginger, mix and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  4. Add green gram, turmeric powder, red chilli powder, coriander powder, garam masala powder and dried mango powder, mix well and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  5. Transfer into a bowl.
  6. Add potato, onion and salt and mix well.
  7. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  8. Divide the kachori dough into equal portions and roll out into small discs.
  9. Place a spoonful of filling in the centre and bring the edges together to make a potli.
  10. Flatten a little into kachoris.
  11. Slide the kachoris, a few at a time, into hot oil and deep-fry till golden brown.
  12. Drain on absorbent paper.
  13. To make chutney, heat oil on a non-stick pan, add fennel seeds, cumin seeds, carom seeds and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  14. Add tamarind paste and mix.
  15. Add 1½ cups water, red chilli powder, garam masala powder and sugar.
  16. Mix, bring to a boil and strain into a bowl.
  17. Add potato and onion and mix well.
  18. Chop coriander sprigs and add.
  19. Crack the kachoris from centre, fill in the prepared chutney, arrange them on a serving plate and serve.

RECIPE 129: Multi Grain Dal Dhokli
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Multi-Grain-Dal-Dhokli-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A popular Gujarati one meal dish made healthier by using multi grain flour This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Multi grain flour, Split pigeon pes (tuvar dal) | Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Dals and Kadhis | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Multi grain flour
  - 1/2 hour to taste Salt
  - 1/2 tsp + pinches Turmeric powder
  - 1/2 cup Raw peanuts
  - 2 tablespoons Gram flour (besan)
  - 1 pinch Red chilli powder
  - 1 tablespoon Ghee
  - 1/2 teaspoon Mustard seeds
  - 1/4 teaspoon Asafoetida (hing)
  - 1/2 tablespoons Dal tadka masala
  - 1 teaspoon Jagger , chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Fresh coriander leaves , chopped to serve Khakras

METHOD:
  1. Heat a pressure cooker, add split pigeon peas, salt, ½ tsp turmeric powder, peanuts and 2 cups water.
  2. Cover the cooker and cook under pressure till 4-5 whistles are released.
  3. Meanwhile take multigrain flour, gram flour, salt, remaining turmeric powder and red chilli powder in a bowl and mix well.
  4. Add sufficient water and knead into stiff dough.
  5. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  6. Take small portions of dough and roll them on back of a fork to shape into gnocchis.
  7. Uncover the cooker when the pressure settles completely.
  8. Heat ghee in a deep non-stick pan, add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  9. Add asafoetida, fenugreek seeds, curry leaves, dried red chillies and the cooked pigeon peas.
  10. Mix well for 1 minute on medium heat.
  11. Add dal tadka masala and mix well.
  12. Add sufficient water to get the required consistency and mix well.
  13. Add the gnocchis and mix well.
  14. Cover and cook on medium heat for 15-20 minutes.
  15. Adjust salt, add jaggery and coriander leaves and mix till jaggery dissolves.
  16. Switch the heat off.
  17. Put ladles full of cooked dal dhokli into serving plates and serve hot with khakras.

========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/mushroom-walnut-sliders-6595275

Looking for a meatless yet incredibly satisfying meal? Look no further! These sliders are packed with umami goodness and the goodness of ProV Walnuts.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 15-20 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8 toasted slider buns
  - 1½ tablespoons chopped garlic
  - 2-3 fresh thyme sprigs Crushed black peppercorns to taste Salt to taste ½ teaspoon paprika powder
  - 1 teaspoon Worcestershire sauce ½ cup dried breadcrumbs Mayonnaise as required Lettuce leaves as required Pickled purple cabbage as required Tomato slices as required Cheese slices as required

METHOD:
  1. Transfer Pro V Regal Walnuts in a chopper and crush coarsely.
  2. Heat oil in a small nonstick pan.
  3. Add garlic, onion, mushrooms, crushed walnuts, thyme sprigs and sauté for 4-5 minutes.

  6. Add dried breadcrumbs and mix well.

RECIPE 131: Nachni Idiappam
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Nachni-Idiappam-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Finger millet or nachni is very high in proteins and very good for growing children. When the idiappams resemble nests, the children will simply devour them without complaint This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Finger millet (ragi / nachni) flour, Ghee | Cuisine: South Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 51-60 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup finger millet (ragi /nachni) flour ½ tablespoon ghee + for greasing Salt to taste Tomato chutney for garnish Peeled and tempered baby potatoes for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Boil 1 cup water in a deep non-stick pan.
  2. Add ghee and salt and mix well.
  3. Add nachni flour and mix well, stirring continuously till the mixture is smooth with no lumps.
  4. Cover and cook on low heat for 2-3 minutes till mixture thickens and forms soft dough.
  5. Grease the inner portion of chakli press with ghee.
  6. Transfer the cooked mixture into a bowl and spread it to let it cool down.
  7. Grease your palms with ghee and knead the dough lightly.
  8. Divide the dough into 2 portions.
  9. Shape a portion into a cylinder and put it into the chakli press fitted with sev attachment.
  10. Heat sufficient water in a steamer.
  11. Grease the idli moulds with ghee.
  12. Press the dough through the chakli press into greased moulds.
  13. Place the idli moulds in the steamer and steam for 8-10 minutes.
  14. Pour chutney in center of each idiyappam, and place the tempered potatoes in the centre of the nest.
  15. Serve immediately.

RECIPE 132: Nargisi Kofta
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Nargisi-Kofta--Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Golden-fried hard-boiled eggs enveloped in a flavorful spiced meat mixture, served in a rich and aromatic gravy. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Minced mutton (keema), Eggs | Cuisine: Moghlai | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Non-Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 white bread slices
  - 1½ tablespoons chopped fresh mint leaves
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 teaspoon coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon crushed black peppercorns
  - 1 teaspoon roasted cumin powder
  - 1½ cups breadcrumbs Oil to deep fry Lettuce leaves for garnish Halved red cherry tomatoes for garnish Whole red cherry tomato for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Put mutton in a blender jar.
  2. Trim the edges and break the bread slices into small pieces and add to the blender jar along with green chilli, mint leaves, coriander leaves, coriander powder, red chilli powder, crushed black peppercorns, roasted cumin powder, garam masala powder, ginger -garlic paste and salt and blend to a fine paste.
  3. Transfer the blended mixture into a bowl.
  4. Break eggs into a separate bowl and beat lightly.
  5. Take breadcrumbs in another bowl.
  6. Take a portion of blended mixture on your palm, place a boiled egg on it and completely coat the egg with the mixture to make kofta.
  7. Grease your hands with little water and smoothen the outer layer.
  8. Coat koftas lightly with breadcrumbs and rub off excess breadcrumbs.
  9. Dip them in egg mixture and coat them with breadcrumbs again and shake off the excess breadcrumbs.
  10. Set aside.
  11. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai, slide in the koftas and deep fry on medium heat till golden brown.
  12. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  13. Spread the lettuce leaves on a serving plate, add halved red cherry tomatoes and arrange nargisi koftas over them and place a whole red cherry tomato in center.
  14. Serve hot.

RECIPE 133: Neyyappam
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Neyyappam.html

A traditional sweet from Kerala – it is a sweet deep-fried rice and jaggery dumpling. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Raw rice, Refined flour (maida) | Cuisine: Kerala | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 5-6 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4-5 hours
  - 1½ cups chopped jaggery
  - 2 teaspoons ghee ⅓ cup coconut slices
  - 1 tablespoon black sesame seeds
  - 1 teaspoon green cardamom powder ½ teaspoon cumin seeds ½ teaspoon dried ginger powder ¼ teaspoon nutmeg powder A pinch of salt ½ teaspoon soda bicarbonate Oil for deep frying

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick pan, add jaggery and ½ cup water and cook, stirring till a thick syrup is formed.
  2. Remove the impurities and set aside to cool down.
  3. Heat ghee in another non-stick pan, add coconut slices and saute till light brown.
  4. Drain rice and put it in a blender jar, add jaggery syrup and grind to a fine paste.
  5. Transfer into a mixing bowl, add refined flour and mix well.
  6. Add fried coconut slices, sesame seeds, cardamom powder, cumin seeds, ginger powder, nutmeg powder, salt and soda bicarbonate, mix well.
  7. Let the batter rest for 1 hour.
  8. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai, pour a ladleful of batter and deep fry on a medium low heat till golden brown in colour.
  9. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  10. Make more neyyappam with the remaining batter.
  11. Arrange them on a serving platter and serve hot with tea.

RECIPE 134: Nimboo Mirch Wale Chane
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Nimboo-Mirch-Wale-Chane-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

An excellent starter – marinated boiled chickpeas batter fried and sautéed with a spicy mixture . This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Chickpeas (kabuli chane), Lemon | Cuisine: Punjabi | Course: Main | Prep Time: 7-8 hours | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 teaspoons chaat masala
  - 3 tablespoons Punjabi chole masala
  - 1/2 cups refined flour (maida)
  - 1 cup cornflour
  - 1 pinch baking soda
  - 2 tablespoons finely chopped garlic
  - 1 inch ginger , cut into thin strips
  - 1 teaspoon crushed black peppercorns
  - 1/4 bunch fresh coriander leaves Green capsicum , thinly sliced to garnish Red capsicum , thinly sliced to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Take chickpeas in a bowl.
  2. Add 1½ tsps red chilli powder, salt, 1 tsp chaat masala and 2 tbsps Punjabi chole masala and mix well.
  3. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  4. Take refined flour, cornflour, baking soda, salt and 1 tbsp oil in another bowl.
  5. Add little water and mix well to make a thick batter.
  6. Take 1 cup water in another bowl.
  7. Add marinated chickpeas to the batter and mix well.
  8. Dampen your fingers with water and pick each chickpea along with batter and slide into the hot oil.
  9. Separate the chickpeas with a spoon and deep fry till they are half done and float on top.
  10. Drain on absorbent paper.
  11. Reheat the oil in kadai to high temperature.
  12. Meanwhile heat 1 tbsp oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic and sauté till lightly brown.
  13. Add green chillies, ginger strips and sauté till the mixture turns a light brown.
  14. Add the half fried chickpeas back in kadai, and deep fry till golden and crisp.
  15. Drain on absorbent paper.
  16. Add chickpeas to the pan.
  17. Add remaining red chilli powder, remaining Punjabi chole masala, remaining chaat masala, crushed black peppercorns and lemon juice.
  18. Chop coriander leaves and add, mix well and cook on medium heat for 1-2 minutes.
  19. Transfer into a serving bowl.
  20. Garnish with green and red capsicum slices and serve hot.

RECIPE 135: Noon Chai Kashmiri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Noon-Chai-Kashmiri-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A warm hug from the valley in every sip, blending tradition and comfort seamlessly. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Regular tea leaves, Salt | Cuisine: Kashmiri | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: Preparation Time | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups milk ½ teaspoon salt Salted jeera biscuits to serve

METHOD:
  1. Mix tea leaves and baking soda in a bowl.
  2. Boil 2 cups water in a small stainless steel saucepan, add the tea leaves mixture.
  3. Constantly lift ladle full of mixture and pour it back into the pan on medium heat till colour changes.
  4. Add sugar as required and bring the mixture to a boil.
  5. Add milk and again lift ladle full of mixture and pour it back into the pan till colour changes.
  6. Add salt and again lift ladle full of mixture and pour it back into the pan.
  7. Strain the tea into serving cups and serve hot with salted jeera biscuit.

RECIPE 136: Oats Thalipeeth
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Oats-Thalipeeth.html

One of the most popular breakfast snacks amongst the Maharashtrian, this thalipeeth has oats flour replacing the traditional bhajanee flour This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Oats flour, Green chillies | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups oats flour
  - 1 small carrot, grated
  - 1 large onion, finely chopped
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves ½ teaspoon cumin powder ½ teaspoon coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chili powder ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon garam masala powder Salt to taste
  - 2-3 green chillies, chopped Oil for drizzling Green chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take oats flour in a bowl.
  2. Add carrot, onion, coriander leaves, cumin powder, coriander powder, red chili powder, turmeric powder, garam masala powder, salt and green chillies and mix well.
  3. Add 1 cup water, and knead into soft dough.
  4. Take a non-stick tawa, add a portion of the dough, dip your fingers in water and spread it into a thick disc.
  5. Make a few holes in the center.
  6. Place the non-stick tawa on heat and cook for 4-5 minutes on medium heat.
  7. Drizzle a little oil.
  8. Flip and cook the other side for 2-3 minutes or until golden and crisp.
  9. Serve hot with green chutney.

RECIPE 137: Onion Capsicum Arachuvitta Sambhar
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Onion-Capsicum-Arachuvitta-Sambhar.html

Arachuvitta means freshly ground and this traditional sambhar from Tamil nadu is made with freshly ground masala This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Onion, Green capsicum | Cuisine: Tamil Nadu | Course: Dals and Kadhis | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium Onion , thickly sliced
  - 1 medium Green capsicum , thickly sliced
  - 1/2 cup Split pigeon peas (tuvar dal) , pressure cooked with ¼ tsp turmeric powder
  - 10-12 Curry leaves
  - 1/4 teaspoon Asafoetida
  - 1 lemon si Tamarind , soaked in
  - 20 minutes
  - 1 tablespoon Jaggery , chopped
  - 2 tablespoons Fresh coriander leaves , chopped Masala paste
  - 1/4 cup Coriander seeds
  - 1 tablespoon Cumin seeds
  - 2 tablespoons Split pigeon peas (tuvar dal)
  - 1 tablespoon Split Bengal gram (chana dal)
  - 1/2 cup Fresh coconut , scraped
  - 5-6 Dried red chillies (pandi) Tempering
  - 1 tablespoon Ghee
  - 5-6 Curry leaves

METHOD:
  1. To make the masala paste, dry roast coriander seeds and cumin seeds till fragrant in a non-stick pan.
  2. Transfer onto a plate and set aside to cool.
  3. Similarly, dry roast pigeon peas and Bengal gram in the same pan till they turn golden brown.
  4. Transfer onto the same plate and let them cool.
  5. Dry roast coconut in the same pan till it turns golden brown.
  6. Transfer onto the same plate and let it cool.
  7. Heat oil in the same pan, add the dried red chillies and saute for a minute.
  8. Transfer onto the same plate and let them cool completely.
  9. Put all these ingredients into a mixer jar, add ½ cup water and blend to a semi-smooth paste.
  10. To make the sambhar, heat oil in a non-stick deep pan.
  11. Add fenugreek seeds and 5-6 curry leaves and sauté for a few seconds.
  12. Add the onion and sauté till translucent.
  13. Add the capsicum and sauté till the onions turn golden brown.
  14. Add turmeric powder, sambhar masala and salt and sauté for a minute.
  15. Squeeze the soaked tamarind to extract the pulp and add along with the water and mix well.
  16. Let the mixture come to a boil.
  17. Continue to cook for 10-12 minutes.
  18. Add the ground paste and mix well.
  19. Cook for 2-3 minutes.
  20. Add the cooked pigeon peas and mix.
  21. Add the remaining curry leaves and mix well.
  22. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  23. Add jaggery and mix, cook till it melts.
  24. Add coriander leaves and mix well.
  25. To make the tempering, heat ghee in a small pan.
  26. Add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  27. Add asafoetida and curry leaves and mix.
  28. Pour this into the sambhar and mix well.
  29. Serve hot with steamed rice.

RECIPE 138: Orange and Quinoa Salad
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Orange-and-Quinoa-Salad-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

This vibrant quinoa salad combines juicy orange segments, roasted walnuts, and crisp radishes with tender cherry tomatoes and crunchy microgreens. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Oranges, Quinoa | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Salads | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet &amp; Sour | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium oranges
  - 2 cups quinoa , cooked
  - 8-10 red radishes , thinly sliced
  - 1/2 cup microgreens Feta cheese to sprinkle Dressing
  - 3 tablespoons orange marmalade Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 4 lemons
  - 3 tablespoons honey

METHOD:
  1. Peel orange and separate the segments.
  2. Remove seeds and halve them.
  3. Thinly slice onion and gently separate the layers.
  4. To make the dressing, take marmalade in a small jar, add salt, crushed black peppercorns, olive oil and mix till well combined.
  5. Halve the lemons and squeeze their juice directly into the jar and mix well.
  6. Add honey, place the lid on and shake the mixture till everything is well combined.
  7. Halve the cherry tomatoes.
  8. Take quinoa in a large bowl, add walnuts, onion, cherry tomatoes, red radishes, micro greens and halved orange segments.
  9. Pour the dressing into it and toss lightly.
  10. Transfer the salad onto a serving plate, crumble and sprinkle feta cheese on top.
  11. Serve immediately.

========================================================================

A refreshing and fizzy beverage made using fresh oranges and tonic water! Check out this fizzy nonalcoholic drink - Orange Fizz.

INGREDIENTS:
  - 9 oranges
  - 8 teaspoons powdered sugar Ice cubes as required Mint sprigs as required Tonic water as required

RECIPE 140: Orange Pineapple Chia Drink
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/orange-pineapple-chia-drink-7095045

A refreshing nutritious drink made with Orange, Pineapple and #ProVFoods Chia tastes amazing as well as looks great. So whip up a quick drink to sip on this afternoon.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Beverages Prep time 30-40 minutes | Cook Time: 0 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian Igredients 3 oranges 1 medium pineapple 2 tablespoons Pro V Premium Chia Seeds 1 lemon 3 tablespoons honey Black salt to taste ½ teaspoon red chilli powder Crushed ice as required Fresh mint leaves as required Drinking soda as required

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 oranges
  - 1 medium pineapple
  - 1 lemon
  - 3 tablespoons honey Black salt to taste ½ teaspoon red chilli powder Crushed ice as required Fresh mint leaves as required Drinking soda as required

METHOD:

  2. Add ½ cup water and set aside to soak for 30 minutes.

RECIPE 141: Palak Moongphalli Til Pulao
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Palak-Moongphalli-Til-Pulao-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Appearance of a dish is as important as its taste and this pulao scores high on both points This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fresh spinach (palak), Spinach puree | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Rice | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium bunch Fresh spinach (palak) , shredded
  - 1 cup Spinach puree
  - 1 cup Raw peanuts (kachchi moongphalli) , soaked and boiled
  - 1 tablespoon White sesame seeds (til)
  - 3 cups Basmati rice , cooked
  - 1 tablespoon Oil
  - 10-12 Black peppercorns
  - 4 medium Potatoes , peeled
  - 1 tablespoon Garlic , chopped
  - 1 teaspoon Red chilli powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1 teaspoon Garam masala powder to taste Salt
  - 1 tablespoon Lemon juice to garnish Fresh red chilli to garnish Tomato wedges

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a deep non-stick pan, add sesame seeds and saute till light brown.
  2. Add cumin seeds, bay leaf and peppercorns, mix and sauté for a few minutes.
  3. Cut potatoes into cubes, add to the pan and mix.
  4. Add garlic, mix and cook till the potatoes turn golden.
  5. Add peanuts, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, garam masala powder and salt, mix well and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  6. Add spinach leaves, mix and cook till the leaves wilt.
  7. Add spinach puree, lemon juice and Fortune Biryani Rice, mix lightly and cook till rice gets heated through.
  8. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with red chilli and tomato wedges and serve hot.

RECIPE 142: Palak Paneer
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Palak-Paneer-Khazana-of-Indian-Recipes.html

Cottage cheese cooked in spinach-based gravy and fresh Indian spices is a household staple. Master the art of making this simple, wholesome and nutritious veg dish by following this recipe.

Main Ingredients: paneer (cottage cheese), Spinach (palak) | Cuisine: Punjabi | Course: Main Course-Veg | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Medium | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 300 grams paneer (cottage cheese)
  - 2 medium bunches of spinach
  - 1 large onion
  - 1 green chilli
  - 1 tablespoon chopped garlic
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds Salt to taste
  - 1/4 teaspoon garam masala
  - 2 tablespoons fresh cream + for garnish A large pinch of dried fenugreek leaves (kasuri methi) powder Parantha to serve

METHOD:
  1. Finely chop onion and cut paneer into 1-inch cubes.
  2. Boil sufficient water in a deep pan.
  3. Add spinach leaves and blanch fir 1 minute.
  4. Drain into iced cold water.
  5. Drain the spinach leaves and squeeze out excess water and put into a mixer jar.
  6. Add green chilli and 1/2 cup water and grind to a fine paste.
  7. Heat oil in a non stick pan, add cumin seeds and let them change colour.
  8. Add the chopped onions and sautè till translucent.
  9. Add garlic, mix and cook for a minute.
  10. Add the ground spinach paste, mix and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  11. Add salt, garam masala powder, paneer cubes and fresh cream and gently mix.
  12. Cook for 1 minute.
  13. Add dried fenugreek leaves powder, mix and cook for 1 minute.
  14. Take the pan off the heat.
  15. Garnish with fresh cream and serve hot with parantha.

RECIPE 143: Paneer Matar Makhana
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Paneer-Matar-Makhana---SK-Khazana.html

This vegetarian main course recipe is made with cottage cheese, green peas and lotus seeds cooked in a rich velvety gravy. You can enjoy this with hot paranthas, chapatis or rotis. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: paneer (cottage cheese), Green peas | Cuisine: Indian,Fusion | Course: Main | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 200 grams Paneer (cottage cheese) cut into small cubes
  - 1/4 cup Green peas boiled
  - 2 cups Lotus seeds
  - 4-5 Garlic cloves to taste Salt
  - 1 teaspoon Cumin seeds
  - 1 teaspoon Red chilli pepper
  - 1 tablespoon Coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon Cumin powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon Garam masala powder
  - 1/4 teaspoon Dried fenugreek leaves (kasoori methi) powder
  - 2 tablespoons Fresh cream
  - 1 tablespoon Honey for garnish Fresh coriander sprigs to serve Paranthe to serve Onion wedges to serve Green chillies to serve Lemon wedges

METHOD:
  1. Heat 1 tsp ghee in a non-stick pan, add lotus seeds and saute on low heat for 5-6 minutes or till crisp.
  2. Transfer onto a plate and set aside.
  3. Heat 2 tsps ghee in the same pan, add onion and saute till golden brown.
  4. Add tomato, green chilli, ginger and garlic cloves and saute well.
  5. Add salt and mix well.
  6. Cover and cook for 5-6 minutes.
  7. Set aside to cool slightly.
  8. Transfer the mixture into a blender jar and add ¼ cup water and blend to a smooth paste.
  9. Heat remaining ghee in the same pan, add cumin seeds and sauté till their colour changes.
  10. Add the ground paste, mix well, cover and cook for 5-6 minutes.
  11. Add red chilli powder, coriander powder, cumin powder and turmeric powder, mix well and saute for a few seconds.
  12. Add ¾ cup water, mix, and cook for a minute.
  13. Add green peas, cottage cheese and the roasted lotus seeds and mix well.
  14. Sprinkle garam masala powder, dried fenugreek leaves powder and fresh cream and mix well.
  15. Add honey and mix and take the pan off the heat.
  16. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with coriander sprigs and serve hot with paranthe, onion wedges, green chillies and lemon wedges.


========================================================================
RECIPE 144: Paneer Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Paneer-Parantha.html

Paranthe can be stuffed with different stuffings. Paneer paranthe is one of them that is both healthy and delicious This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Full cream milk, Fresh cream | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 2-2.30 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 litre full cream milk
  - 1 cup fresh cream
  - 1/2 cups whole wheat flour
  - 1/2 cup grated processed cheese
  - 1 small onion , chopped
  - 2 green chillies , chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoons chaat masala
  - 1/2 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves Salt to taste Ghee for shallow frying

METHOD:
  1. To make paneer heat milk in a deep non-stick pan, add cream and bring it to a boil.
  2. Add vinegar and mix well.
  3. Keep a large sieve over a bowl and line it with a muslin cloth.
  4. When the milk curdles, pour it in the sieve and strain the excess whey.
  5. Gather the edges of the cloth together and put it in cold water.
  6. Remove from water, keep it again in the sieve and keep a heavy weight over it.
  7. Set aside for 2 hours to let all the water drain away.
  8. To make the stuffing, crumble the paneer into a bowl.
  9. Add cheese, onion, green chillies, red chilli powder, garam masala, chaat masala, carom seeds, fresh coriander leaves and salt and mix well.
  10. Divide the dough into equal portions.
  11. Shape into balls and press between your palms, make a cavity in the centre of each ball and add spoonful of paneer stuffing, bring the edges together and seal completely.
  12. Roll them out into five inch diameter paranthe.
  13. Heat a non-stick tawa, place one parantha at a time on it and cook for ½ minute.
  14. Flip it and apply ghee on the cooked side.
  15. Turn it over again and spread a little more ghee on the other side too.
  16. Cook, turning sides, till both sides are evenly cooked and golden brown.
  17. Wrap the paranthe in Freshwrapp and pack it in tiffin with yogurt packed in a small container with lid.


========================================================================
RECIPE 145: Pani Puri
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/PANI-PURI.html

Pani puri is a popular Indian street food snack, crispy puri shells filled with spicy, tangy flavored water (pani), along with a mixture of mashed potatoes, chickpeas, onions, and a tamarind chutney. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Puris, Potatoes | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups moong sprouts, blanched
  - 1 teaspoon roasted cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala + for sprinkling
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder Black salt to taste Salt to taste ½ cup salted boondi
  - 2 cups ragda Fried papdis as required Sev for sprinkling Imli chutney
  - 30 minutes
  - 30 minutes ¼ cup melted jaggery
  - 1½ teaspoons red chilli powder Salt to taste Pudine ka pani
  - 1 small bunch fresh mint leaves (pudina) ½ small bunch fresh coriander leaves
  - 4-5 green chillies Salt to taste
  - 2 teaspoons roasted cumin powder
  - 2 teaspoons chaat masala Black salt to taste
  - 1 lemon Ice cubes as required

METHOD:
  1. To prepare imli chutney, drain the excess water from tamarind and dates.
  2. Strain the tamarind in a bowl and squeeze to get the pulp.
  3. Grind dates alongwith some water into a smooth and thick puree.
  4. Add the date puree, melted jaggery, cumin powder, chilli powder and salt to the tamarind pulp and mix.
  5. Add 1 cup water and mix well.
  6. To prepare pudine ka pani, separate the mint leaves from the sprigs.
  7. Blend together coriander sprigs, mint leaves and broken green chillies alongwith some water into a smooth mixture.
  8. Transfer in a bowl.
  9. Add salt, cumin powder, chaat masala, black salt, pani puri masala, lemon juice and 4 cups water to the ground mint leaves mixture and mix well.
  10. Add few ice cubes and mix well.
  11. Mash the potatoes in another bowl.
  12. Add moong sprouts and mix.
  13. Add cumin powder, 1 teaspoon chaat masala, chilli powder, black salt and salt and mix well.
  14. Add salted boondi to pudine ka pani and mix well.
  15. Crack the top of each puri, put some radga, potato-moong mixture, pour some imli chutney and pudine ka pani and serve immediately.
  16. To prepare sukka puri, put some potato-moong mixture on fried puris, sprinkle some salt, chaat masala, black salt and sev on top and serve immediately.

RECIPE 146: Papaya Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Papaya-Parantha-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Begin your day with these healthy paranthas - an ideal breakfast snack This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Raw papaya, Whole wheat flour (atta) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Breads | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium Raw papaya , peeled and grated
  - 250 grams Whole wheat flour (atta)
  - 1 medium Onion , finely choppped
  - 2-3 Green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1/4 cup Salted peanuts , coarsely crushed
  - 1 teaspoon Red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon Garam masala powder
  - 1 tablespoon Sugar
  - 1 tablespoon Lemon juice to taste Salt for basting Oil to serve Yogurt

METHOD:
  1. Mix together raw papaya, whole wheat flour, onion, ginger, green chillies, salted peanuts, red chilli powder, garam masala powder, sugar, lemon juice and salt in a bowl.
  2. Add sufficient water and knead into a dough.
  3. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  4. Divide the dough into equal portions and roll out into large discs.
  5. Place the paranthas on the hot tawa, one at a time, and cook, basting with oil and turning sides, till evenly browned on both the sides.
  6. Cut each parantha into 4 pieces, arrange them on a serving platter and serve hot with yogurt.

RECIPE 147: Pav Bhaji Pull Apart
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pav-Bhaji-Pull-Apart-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Indulge in the ultimate comfort food hug with our Pav Bhaji Pull Apart – a spicy, buttery delight that'll have you coming back for more with every tear! This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Multigrain pavs, Oil | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 6 multigrain pavs
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 2 teaspoons butter + for brushing
  - 2 medium onions, finely chopped Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon ginger-garlic paste
  - 1 large tomato, finely chopped
  - 1 medium green capsicum, finely chopped ½ cup grated carrot ½ cup grated cauliflower
  - 1½ tablespoons pav bhaji masala
  - 1 green chilli, finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli paste
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 2 teaspoons lemon juice
  - 2 cheese slices

METHOD:
  1. Preheat the oven at 180º C.
  2. Heat oil and 2 teaspoons butter in a non-stick pan.
  3. Add onions and sauté till translucent.
  4. Add a pinch of salt and sauté till onions turn golden brown.
  5. Add ginger-garlic paste and sauté for a while.
  6. Add tomato and cook till it turns pulpy.
  7. Add capsicum, carrot and cook for a while.
  8. Add cauliflower, potatoes and frozen green peas.
  9. Mix well.
  10. Add salt, pav bhaji masala, green chilli, red chilli paste and garam masala powder.
  11. Sauté well.
  12. Mash the mixture well.
  13. Add lemon juice and coriander leaves.
  14. Add little water and mash again.
  15. Line a baking tray with parchment paper.
  16. Take the set of pavs on a worktop and halve it horizontally.
  17. Place the base layer on the tray lined with parchment paper and spread bhaji all over it.
  18. Sprinkle mozzarella cheese all over and place the cheese slices.
  19. Cover with top layer.
  20. Brush top of pavs with butter.
  21. Keep the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 4-5 minutes or till cheese melts.
  22. Place on a serving wooden platter with the parchment paper.
  23. Pull apart individual pav from the whole set and serve hot.

RECIPE 148: Pesarattu
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pesarattu-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A traditional Andhra snack made from green gram (mung bean) batter, typically served with chutney or spicy fillings.This is healthy and tasty too. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Whole green gram (sabut moong), Rice | Cuisine: Andhra | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup whole green gram (sabut moong), soaked overnight
  - 2 tbsps rice, soaked overnight
  - 7-8 curry leaves
  - 2 tbsps chopped fresh coriander leaves Salt to taste Oil for shallow frying
  - 1½ inch cubes
  - 2-3 medium tomato, sliced Gunpowder (molaga podi) to sprinkle Tomato ketchup to serve Coconut chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Blend green gram, rice, green chilli, ginger, curry leaves and coriander leaves with sufficient water to a fine paste.
  2. Transfer into a bowl and set aside for 1 hour.
  3. Add salt and mix well.
  4. Heat a non-stick pan, drizzle and little oil rub with muslin cloth.
  5. Pour a ladle of batter, and spread it evenly.
  6. Drizzle some more oil all around.
  7. Flip when the underside is golden and cook the other side till golden brown, Place paneer cubes and tomato slices alternately and sprinkle gunpowder over them.
  8. Fold and remove the pesarattu from the pan onto a serving plate.
  9. Serve hot with tomato ketchup and coconut chutney.

RECIPE 149: Pindi Chole Gujiya
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pindi-Chole-Gujiya-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A fusion delicacy combining the flavors of Pindi Chole with the concept of Gujiya, resulting in a savory pastry filled with spiced chickpeas, often enjoyed as a festive snack or appetizer. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Chickpeas (kabuli chane), Ghee | Cuisine: Punjabi | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 41-50 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups chickpeas (kabuli chane), soaked overnight, boiled with teabags
  - 1 tablespoon ghee
  - 2 medium onions, chopped
  - 1 tablespoon ginger-garlic paste Salt to taste
  - 1 cup tomato puree
  - 1 tablespoon Punjabi chole masala Whole wheat flour dough as required Oil for deep-frying Green chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add onions and sauté on medium heat till onions turn golden brown.
  3. Add ginger-garlic paste and sauté till fragrant.
  4. Add tomato puree, mix well and sauté for 3-4 minutes till oil separates.
  5. Add salt and mix well.
  6. Add chole masala, mix well and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  7. Add boiled chickpeas with cooking liquor and mix well.
  8. Cook on medium heat for 2-3 minutes.
  9. Divide the dough into equal portions, apply little ghee on worktop, apply ghee on each portion and roll out into thin discs.
  10. Cut out medium round discs with a cookie cutter Mash the chole slightly and cook till the mixture dries up.
  11. Transfer into a plate and set aside to cool.
  12. Place a little pindi chole in the centre of each disc.
  13. Apply water on edges, fold into half and seal the edges and shape into gujiyas by slightly pinching the sealed edges and folding inwards.
  14. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai on medium heat, slide in gujiyas, a few at a time, and deep-fry till golden brown.
  15. Drain on absorbent paper.
  16. Transfer into a serving basket lined with butter paper and serve hot with green chutney.

RECIPE 151: Pineapple Sandesh
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pineapple-Sandesh-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A signature mithai from Bengal, sandesh can be made in different flavours – here pineapple graces it This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Milk, Canned pineapple slices | Cuisine: Bengali | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 litre Milk , curdled with
  - 7-8 Canned pineapple slices , soaked in water
  - 4 tablespoons Powdered sugar
  - 1/2 teaspoon Green cardamom powder to garnish Almonds , blanched, peeled and slivered to garnish Pistachios , blanched, peeled and slivered to garnish Saffron strands

METHOD:
  1. Strain the curdled milk (chenna) through a muslin cloth and squeeze out excess water completely.
  2. Transfer the chenna onto a large plate and knead lightly.
  3. Add powdered sugar and green cardamom powder and knead again.
  4. Transfer chenna into a piping bag.
  5. Drain the pineapple slices on an absorbent paper till they are completely dry and place on a serving platter.
  6. Pipe out the chenna mixture on the edges of pineapple slices in floral shape.
  7. Garnish each slice with almond slivers, pistachio slivers, few saffron strands and serve.
