RECIPE 152: Pink Khandvi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pink-Khandvi-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

A vibrant twist on the traditional Indian snack, featuring delicate rolls made from gram flour and yogurt, infused with a hint of beetroot puree for a visually appealing and flavorful treat This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Beetroot puree, Gram flour (besan) | Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/4 cup Beetroot puree
  - 1 cup Gram flour (besan)
  - 1 tablespoon Refined flour (maida)
  - 1/2 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoon Ginger-green chilli paste to taste Salt
  - 3 cups Buttermilk for greasing Oil to garnish Fresh coconut , scraped to garnish Fresh coriander leaves , chopped Tempering
  - 2 tablespoons Oil
  - 1 teaspoon Mustard seeds
  - 1 sprigs Curry leaves

METHOD:
  1. Put gram flour in a bowl, add refined flour, turmeric powder, red chilli powder, ginger-green chilli paste and salt and mix well.
  2. Add buttermilk and mix till there are no lumps.
  3. Heat a deep non-stick pan.
  4. Pour the batter into it and cook on medium heat, whisking continuously till the mixture thickens.
  5. Grease the back side of steel thalis with some oil.
  6. Add beetroot puree to the cooking mixture and mix well and cook further on medium heat for 1-2 minutes.
  7. While the mixture is still hot spread a thin layer of the batter with a palette knife on the greased thalis and set aside to cool.
  8. After the mixture cools down, sets and the colour deepens, cut the layers vertically into thick strips, and roll each strip starting from one end to another.
  9. Insert coloured toothpick in center of each khandvi and arrange them on a plate.
  10. To prepare the tempering, heat oil in a non-stick tempering pan.
  11. Add mustard seeds and let them sputter.
  12. Add asafoetida and curry leaves and mix well.
  13. Pour the tempering over khandvis, garnish with coconut and coriander leaves and serve.

RECIPE 155: Pizza Roll Ups
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pizza-Roll-Ups.html

Pizza roll-ups are a delicious twist on traditional pizza, where pizza dough is rolled up with your favorite toppings and then baked until golden and crispy. They're perfect for a quick snack or appetizer! This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Fresh yeast, Sugar | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 51-60 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 20 grams fresh yeast
  - 1 teaspoon sugar
  - 1½ cups refined flour + for dusting
  - 1 pickled jalapeno, chopped Dried oregano for sprinkling Red chilli flakes for sprinkling

METHOD:
  1. Place the yeast in a big bowl.
  2. Add the sugar, 1 teaspoon salt and 2-3 tablespoons of warm water and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  3. Add flour, olive oil and remaining salt to the activated yeast and mix well.
  4. Add sufficient water and knead into soft dough.
  5. Cover with a wet muslin cloth and set aside for 15-20 minutes in a warm place.
  6. Preheat the oven to 200°C.
  7. Grease a baking tray with oil.
  8. Dust some flour on the work table, place the dough over it and roll it into a thin rectangular sheet.
  9. Apply pizza sauce and sprinkle mozzarella cheese.
  10. Add corn, mushrooms, mixed capsicums, jalapeno.
  11. Sprinkle dried oregano and chilli flakes.
  12. Roll tightly and cut into thick slices.
  13. Place the slices on a baking tray keeping some distance between each and bake for 10-15 minutes.
  14. Remove and let them cool.
  15. Wrap and pack it in the tiffin.

RECIPE 156: Pizza Samosa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pizza-Samosa-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Why choose between pizza and samosas when you can have the best of both worlds in one crispy bite? This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Readymade samosa dough, Refined sunflower oil | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 tablespoons oil + to deep fry
  - 1 medium onion, cut into ½ inch cubes
  - 1 medium green capsicum, cut into ½ inch cubes ½ cup boiled corn kernels ¼ cup tomato puree
  - 150 grams cottage cheese (paneer), cut into ½ inch cubes Salt to taste ¼ cup green peas, blanched ½ tablespoon dried mixed herbs + to sprinkle ½ teaspoon red chilli flakes + to sprinkle
  - 100 grams mozzarella cheese, cut into ½ inch cubes Parmesan cheese powder to sprinkle Tomato ketchup to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add onion and sauté for a minute.
  2. Add capsicum and corn kernels and cook for 1 minute.
  3. Add tomato puree and cook for 1 minute on medium heat.
  4. Add paneer, salt and green peas and mix.
  5. Sauté for 1a minute and switch off heat.
  6. Transfer into a bowl.
  7. Add dried mixed herbs, red chilli flakes and mozzarella cheese and mix well.
  8. Heat sufficient fortune oil a kadai.
  9. Lightly knead the dough, divide into equal medium portions and roll them into thin oval discs.
  10. Halve each disc.
  11. Take water in a bowl.
  12. Apply water on the edges of each halved disc, shape into a cone, fill in the prepared filling, apply water on edges and seal the edges to form a triangle.
  13. Slide in the samosas into hot oil and deep fry till golden and crisp.
  14. Keep rotating the samosas occasionally so that they are evenly cook all around.
  15. Drain on absorbent paper.
  16. Sprinkle parmesan cheese powder, crushed mixed herbs and red chilli flakes on them.
  17. Arrange on a platter and serve hot with tomato ketchup.

RECIPE 157: Pizza Sauce
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pizza-Sauce.html

Originated essentially from Italian cuisine, Pizza has garnered many fans from India. Better than the average store bought Pizza Sauce, this one is much more authentic and flavorful This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Fresh tomato puree, Olive oil | Cuisine: Italian | Course: Gravies, Sauces and Stocks | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup fresh tomato puree
  - 1 tablespoon olive oil
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 1 medium Onion , finely chopped Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1 teaspoon paprika
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli flakes
  - 2 pizza bases Toppings of your choice Mozzarella cheese as required

METHOD:
  1. Heat olive oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic and sauté for 2 minutes.
  2. Add onion, mix and sauté till golden brown.
  3. Add tomato puree, mix and saute for a minute.
  4. Add salt and peppercorn and mix well.
  5. Add 1 cup water and mix, and cook for a minute.
  6. Add paprika and red chilli flakes and mix well.
  7. Add tomato ketchup, mix and sauté on medium heat for 5-7 minutes.
  8. Tear and add basil leaves and mix well.
  9. Remove the pan from heat and let the sauce cool.
  10. Preheat the oven to 180º C.
  11. Keep the pizza base on a baking tray, spread a ladleful of pizza sauce on it.
  12. Top with topping of your choice and mozzarella cheese.
  13. Bake for 5 minutes.
  14. Make another pizza similarly.
  15. Serve the sauce as a dip with pizza.

RECIPE 158: Posto Halwa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Posto-Halwa-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

It will take a while to make this khus khus halwa but the end result is well worth the effort This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Poppy seeds (khuskhus / posto), Milk | Cuisine: Bengali | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup Poppy seeds (khuskhus / posto) , soaked
  - 2 cups Milk
  - 1/2 cup Ghee
  - 1/2 cups Mawa , grated
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder a few strands Saffron

METHOD:
  1. Spoon the soaked poppy seeds into a blender jar, add ½ cup milk and blend to a fine paste.
  2. Heat a non-stick pan, add ghee, poppy seed paste and semolina, mix and sauté, stirring continuously to avoid the formation of lumps, on medium heat for 15-20 minutes, or till the mixture thickens and becomes golden brown.
  3. Crush and add 15-20 walnuts and mix well.
  4. Add caster sugar, remaining milk and stir continuously to avoid formation of lumps and cook on medium heat till the mixture thickens and colour changes to brown.
  5. Add khoya / mawa and mix well.
  6. Sauté for a minute and add green cardamom powder, mix and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  7. Switch off heat and add saffron and mix well.
  8. Transfer into a serving bowl and garnish with California walnuts.
  9. Allow to cool down.
  10. Serve cold.

RECIPE 159: Pot Roast Vegetable Stew
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pot-Roast-Vegetable-Stew-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Medley of vegetables and mushrooms cooked together to make a wonderful stew. Vegetables cooked with whole spices and served with bread. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Carrots, Potatoes | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Main | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 small carrots , peeled
  - 2 medium potatoes , peeled
  - 1 medium onion
  - 1 medium sweet potato , peeled
  - 1 tablespoon olive oil
  - 1 tablespoon butter
  - 4-5 button mushrooms , halved A few sprigs of fresh thyme
  - 1/2 cups vegetable stock
  - 1 cup mixed capsicums triangles Toasted bread slices to serve

METHOD:
  1. Cut carrots into 2 inch pieces, quarter potatoes and onion.
  2. Cut sweet potato into 2 inch pieces.
  3. Heat olive oil in a non-stick heavy bottom pan, add butter and let it melt.
  4. Add onion, carrots, sweet potatoes, potatoes, garlic cloves, salt, crushed black peppercorns and baby corns, mix and cook on high heat for 2-3 minutes.
  5. Add shitake mushrooms, button mushrooms and thyme and sauté well.
  6. Add refined flour and mix well.
  7. Sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  8. Add stock and mix well.
  9. Add mixed capsicums and mix well.
  10. Cover and cook for 15-20 minutes.
  11. Take it off the heat.
  12. Transfer into a serving dish and serve hot with toasted bread slices.

RECIPE 160: Potato Bites
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Potato-Bites-----.html

Spicy potato mixture rolled into small bites, dipped in batter, coated with bread crumbs and deep fried. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Potatoes, Schezwan sauce | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3-4 medium potatoes, boiled, peeled and grated
  - 2 tablespoons schezwan sauce ¼ cup mayonnaise Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1-2 green chillies, chopped
  - 1 teaspoon chilli flakes
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander ¼ cup dried breadcrumbs + for coating Salt to taste
  - 2-3 tablespoons corn flour slurry Oil for deep-frying

METHOD:
  1. Mix together potatoes, schezwan sauce, mayonnaise, peppercorns, green chillies, chilli flakes, coriander, bread crumbs and salt in a bowl.
  2. Divide the prepared mixture into equal portions.
  3. Dip in slurry, coat in bread crumbs, roll lightly between your palms, repeat the process once again and place on a plate.
  4. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  5. Deep-fry the potato bites until golden-brown and crisp.
  6. Drain on absorbent paper.
  7. Serve hot with ketchup.

RECIPE 161: Power Idli
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Power-Idli-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

These idlis have neither rice nor rawa but only dals – healthy, tasty and an ideal breakfast snack. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Split skinless black gram (dhuli urad dal), Split skinless green gram (dhuli moong dal) | Cuisine: South Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 10-15 hour | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup split skinless black gram (dhuli urad dal), soaked
  - 1 cup split skinless green gram (dhuli moong dal), soaked
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ½ teaspoon asafoetida
  - 1 teaspoon ginger-green chilli paste ½ teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste Coconut chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Drain and put split black gram and split green gram into a blender jar.
  2. Add sufficient water and blend to a fine paste.
  3. Transfer into a large bowl and whisk well.
  4. Cover the bowl and set aside in a warm place to ferment for 6-8 hours.
  5. Add cumin seeds, asafoetida, ginger-green chilli paste, turmeric powder and salt and mix well.
  6. Heat sufficient water in a steamer, pour the batter into greased idli moulds and steam for 12-15 minutes.
  7. Take them off the heat.
  8. Dip spoon in water and scoop out the idlis from the mould and arrange them in a serving platter.
  9. Serve hot with coconut chutney.

RECIPE 162: Protein Bowl
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/protein-bowl-7373685

Discover our ultimate 'Protein Bowl' recipe that’s both nutritious and flavorful. This bowl features a hearty mix of brown rice, grilled tofu, and colorful veggies. Ideal for a quick, healthy lunch, it’s packed with protein and taste.

Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Main | Cook Time: 25-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 thick slices
  - 1 teaspoon garlic powder
  - 1 teaspoon onion powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli flakes
  - 1½ teaspoons lemon juice
  - 4 teaspoons olive oil Salt to taste
  - 2 tablespoons oil Herbed rice
  - 1 cup cooked brown rice
  - 1½ tablespoons finely chopped garlic ¾ teaspoon red chilli flakes
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh mint leaves
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 3 teaspoons chopped fresh mixed herbs Salt to taste Sautéed veggies
  - 4 teaspoons olive oil
  - 6-8 button mushrooms, thickly sliced
  - 12-15 medium broccoli florets, blanched and drained ½ cup mixed coloured capsicums triangles
  - 1 medium carrot, peeled, cut into triangles, boiled and drained
  - 1 medium onion, cut into quarters and layers separated Salt to taste ½ teaspoon chopped fresh mixed herbs Dressing
  - 2 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil
  - 2 tablespoons honey
  - 1 tablespoon mustard paste Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns
  - 8-10 cherry tomatoes, halved
  - 20-25 assorted lettuce leaves
  - 4 tablespoons assorted micro greens + for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Place cottage cheese slices on a plate.
  2. Sprinkle garlic powder, onion powder, red chilli flakes, dried mixed herbs, lemon juice, olive oil and salt and apply the mixture well on all the slices and set aside to marinate for 10-15 minutes.
  3. To make the herbed rice, heat olive oil in a non-stick pan.
  4. Add garlic, mix and saute for a few seconds.
  5. Add red chilli flakes, mint leaves, coriander leaves, mixed herbs and salt and mix well.
  6. Add brown rice and mix well.
  7. Add ½ cup water, cover and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  8. Take the pan off the heat.
  9. To make the sautéed veggies, heat olive oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic, mix and saute till golden brown.
  10. Add mushrooms, mix and cook for 3-4 minutes.
  11. Add broccoli, capsicums, carrots, and onion and mix well.
  12. Add salt and fresh herbs, mix well and saute for 1-2 minutes.
  13. Take the pan off the heat.
  14. To make the dressing, take extra virgin olive oil in a bowl, add honey, mustard paste, salt and crushed black peppercorns and whisk well.
  15. Add lemon juice and mix well.
  16. Add cherry tomatoes and English cucumber.
  17. Tear the assorted lettuce leaves and add to the bowl along with micro greens and gently toss till well combined.
  18. To grill the cottage cheese, heat oil in a non-stick grill pan.
  19. Place the cottage cheese slices on it and grill on high heat for 1-2 minutes.
  20. Flip and grill the other side for 1-2 minutes as well.
  21. To assemble, place a portion of the herbed rice in a serving bowl.
  22. Add a portion of the veggie mixture on one side, some of the salad on other side and place a cottage cheese slice on top.
  23. Garnish with micro greens and serve.

RECIPE 163: Protein Rich Poha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Protein-Rich-Poha-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Elevate your poha with the nutritious power of moth and moong sprouts, adding a protein-rich punch to this beloved breakfast dish. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Pressed rice (poha), Sprouted moth beans | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 0-5 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups pressed rice ½ cup sprouted moth beans ½ cup sprouted green gram (moong) Salt to taste ½ large onion, peeled
  - 1 inch ginger
  - 1 green chilli ½ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ lemon Red radish slices for garnish Fresh coriander sprig for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick pan, add moth, green gram, ¼ cup water and salt.
  2. Mix well and cook till the sprouts soften.
  3. Roughly chop onion.
  4. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add curry leaves and cumin seeds and sauté till the seeds change colour.
  5. Add onion, sauté well and cook till translucent.
  6. Finely chop ginger, green chilli and add to the pan.
  7. Mix well and cook for 1 minute.
  8. Add cooked sprouts mixture, cover and cook for 2 minutes.
  9. Add turmeric powder and salt and mix well.
  10. Take pressed rice in a large bowl, wash and strain well.
  11. Add pressed rice to the onion-sprout mixture and mix well.
  12. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  13. Squeeze the juice of lemon into the pan, mix well and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  14. Transfer the mixture into a serving bowl, garnish with red radish slices and coriander sprig and serve hot.

RECIPE 164: Pudla Sandwich
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pudla-Sandwich.html

A dish that fuses two of our favourites, pudla and sandwich into one is simply brilliant. The remarkable taste of the two dishes blending together beautifully makes it a must try This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Gram flour (besan), White bread | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8 white bread slices ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder Salt to taste
  - 1-2 green chillies, finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 medium tomato, finely chopped
  - 3 small mixed bell peppers, roughly chopped ½ teaspoon chaat masala
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped purple cabbage
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped cabbage Butter for greasing and basting
  - 2 tablespoons grated processed cheese (optional) + for garnishing Tomato ketchup for serving Green chutney for serving

METHOD:
  1. To make pudla batter, mix together gram flour, turmeric powder, chilli powder, salt, green chillies, 1½ teaspoons coriander leaves, and ¼ cup water in a bowl.
  2. Heat a non-stick pan.
  3. Take 2 bread slices, coat in batter and place on the pan.
  4. Add tomatoes, mixed bell peppers, ¼ teaspoon chaat masala, purple cabbage, cabbage, and dab lightly.
  5. Grease the edges with butter lightly.
  6. Turn it over to the other side once the underside turns golden brown.
  7. Apply some butter on the edges and flip once more.
  8. Top with remaining coriander leaves, processed cheese (optional) and remaining chaat masala.
  9. Cut the bread slices from the centre and place one bread slice over the other.
  10. Remove from heat and cut into four parts.
  11. Garnish with processed cheese and serve hot with tomato ketchup and green chutney.

RECIPE 165: Pumpkin Halwa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/pumpkin-halwa-4509975

Not many like pumpkin but have you ever tasted a halwa made with pumpkin? Don't judge it before you try it. It's supremely delicious and easy to make too! And since pumpkin is a super food, it would you good to include it in your menu.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithai Prep time 15-20 minutes | Cook Time: 30-35 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ tablespoons ghee
  - 2 cups full fat milk ½ teaspoon green cardamom powder A large pinch of saffron A pinch of nutmeg powder ¾ cup granular sugar ½ cup grated mawa
  - 5-6 cashewnuts, vertically halved and fried

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a deep and wide non-stick pan.
  2. Add pumpkin, mix and sauté for 4-5 minutes.
  3. Add milk, green cardamom powder and saffron and mix.
  4. Add nutmeg powder and mix till well combined.
  5. Continue to cook, stirring in between, for 12-15 minutes or till the pumpkin softens and the mixture thickens.
  6. Add sugar, mawa, cashewnuts, almonds and pistachios and mix.
  7. Cook, stirring, for 8-10 minutes or till the mixture thickens again.
  8. Take the pan off the heat and transfer into serving bowls.
  9. Garnish with silver warq, fried cashewnuts and slivered pistachios.

RECIPE 166: Pumpkin Poppers
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pumpkin-Poppers-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Experience the perfect bite-sized sweet pumpkin mixture cooked in a paniyaram mould, makes a great breakfast snack. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Red pumpkin (kaddu / bhopla) , Ghee | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ tablespoons ghee + for greasing
  - 1 cup grated jaggery ½ cup semolina½ cup fine rice flour Oil for deep-frying Tomato ketchup to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add pumpkin and sauté on high heat for 2-3 minutes till moisture evaporates.
  3. Switch off heat.
  4. Add jaggery and mix well.
  5. Transfer in a bowl.
  6. Mix well.
  7. Add semolina, rice flour and mix well.
  8. Divide the dough into equal portions, grease palms with ghee and make small balls of each portion.
  9. Drizzle ghee in a hot paniyaram mould.
  10. Place the balls in the mould.
  11. Cook on low heat till slightly brown.
  12. Flip and cook on the other side as well.
  13. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  14. Serve hot with tomato ketchup.

RECIPE 167: Punjabi Samosa
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/PUNJABI-SAMOSA.html

Samosa dough, shaped into a cone, stuffed with spicy potato pea mixture and deep fried. A popular snack from the Indian cuisine. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida), Potatoes | Cuisine: Indian,Punjabi | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 41-50 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Difficult | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups refined flour
  - 4 medium potatoes, boiled and peeled ¼ teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain) Salt to taste
  - 4 tablespoons ghee
  - 3 tablespoons coriander seeds
  - 2 tablespoons cumin seeds
  - 1 tablespoon chopped ginger
  - 2-3 green chillies, chopped ½ cup boiled green peas ½ teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 2 tsps dried and crushed pomegranate seeds
  - 2 tsps dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves Oil for drizzling + for deep frying Green chutney to serve Date and tamarind chutney to serve Fried green chillies to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take refined flour in a parat.
  2. Add carom seeds, salt and mix well.
  3. Add 2 tablespoons ghee and mix well.
  4. Add 1 cup water and knead to stiff dough.Cover with a moist muslin cloth and set aside for 10 minutes.
  5. Dry roast coriander seeds on medium heat for 2-3 minutes.
  6. Transfer to a mortar pestle.
  7. Dry roast the cumin seeds in the same pan for 2 minutes on medium heat.
  8. Transfer in the mortar pestle and crush coarsely.
  9. For the stuffing, heat remaining ghee in a kadai.
  10. Add 1½ tablespoons of ground spice mix and sauté for a few seconds.
  11. Add ginger, green chillies and sauté for 30 seconds.
  12. Crush the potatoes and add to the kadai.
  13. Add the green peas and mix well.
  14. Add salt, garam masala powder, dried pomegranate seeds, dried mango powder and mix well.
  15. Add coriander leaves and mix well.
  16. Take the pan off the heat.
  17. Drizzle a little oil on a worktop and spread it evenly.
  18. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape each into a ball.
  19. For making samosa, roll the prepared balls in an oblong and cut in half to make a semi-circle.
  20. Take a semi-circle and apply water on the edges, shape into a cone.
  21. Stuff with a portion of the prepared stuffing and press the edges to seal.
  22. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai, deep fry the prepared samosas on medium heat till golden brown and crisp.
  23. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  24. Serve hot with green chutney, date and tamarind chutney and fried green chillies.


========================================================================
RECIPE 168: Pyaaz ki Kachori
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Pyaaz-ki-Kachori.html

Pyaaz ki Kachori is a traditional Rajasthani snack which satisfies your taste buds to the core. Its raw, authentic flavour is bound to make this kachori your favourite snack This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida) dough, Onions (pyaaz) | Cuisine: Rajasthani | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium onions (pyaaz), finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon oil + for deep-frying
  - 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon chopped garlic
  - 1 teaspoon fennel seeds
  - 1 tablespoon coriander seeds
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon dried mango powder Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander leaves Date-tamarind chutney for serving

METHOD:
  1. Heat 1 tablespoon oil in a non-stick pan.
  2. Add cumin seeds and sauté till it changes colour.
  3. Add ginger, garlic, green chilli, fennel seeds and coriander seeds and sauté for 1 minute.
  4. Add onion and sauté till light golden brown.
  5. Add chilli powder, dried mango powder and salt and sauté for 1 minute.
  6. Add crushed peppercorns and sauté.
  7. Add coriander leaves and mix well.
  8. Transfer in a bowl and cool.
  9. Divide the dough into equal portions and shape into balls.
  10. Make cavity in the center of each ball, put a portion of sautéed onion mixture, bring the ends together, seal and shape into balls.
  11. Lightly flatten each stuffed portion using your fingers into small thick disc.
  12. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  13. Put the stuffed discs and deep-fry till golden brown and crisp.
  14. Drain on absorbent paper.
  15. Serve hot with date-tamarind chutney.


========================================================================
RECIPE 169: Quinoa Chole
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Quinoa-Chole-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Chole served over a bed of spiced quinoa – a complete meal in itself. Rice is replaced with quinoa in this recipe. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Quinoa, Chickpeas (kabuli chane) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 7-8 hours | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups quinoa , cooked
  - 1/2 teaspoons cumin seeds
  - 1/2 medium onion , peeled
  - 1/2 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 1/2 teaspoons red chilli powder
  - 3 large tomatoes , pureed Salt to taste
  - 1 medium onion , finely chopped
  - 2 green chillies Fresh coriander sprigs to garnish Salad to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat 1½ tbsps oil in a pressure cooker, add 1 tsp cumin seeds and saute till they change colour.
  2. Finely chop onion and add, mix and sauté well.
  3. Add ginger and garlic and mix well.
  4. Add chole masala and mix well.
  5. Add red chilli powder, mix well and cook for 1 minute.
  6. Add tomato puree and mix well.
  7. Drain and add chickpeas, salt and 2 cups water and mix well.
  8. Close the cooker with its lid and cook under pressure till 8-10 whistles are released.
  9. Take it off the heat and allow the pressure to settle completely.
  10. Meanwhile, heat remaining oil in a non-stick pan, add remaining cumin seeds and saute till they change colour.
  11. Add finely chopped onion and mix well.
  12. Roughly chop green chillies and add to the onion mixture, add cooked quinoa and salt and toss till well combined.
  13. Drizzle a little water over the quinoa, cover and cook on low heat for 2-3 minutes.
  14. For serving, place a portion of quinoa on each serving plate, pour a portion of chole over it, garnish with a coriander sprig and serve hot with salad.

RECIPE 170: Radish Cakes
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Radish-Cakes.html

Indulge in the savory delight of deep-fried radish cakes, a delicious Oriental starter paired perfectly with a flavorful dip. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: White radish, White radish | Cuisine: Oriental | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 8-10 hour | Cook Time: 1.30-2 hour | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 small white radish, peeled and grated
  - 1 medium white radish, peeled and cut into thin strips
  - 1 small carrot, peeled and cut into thin strips ¾ cup rice flour ½ cup refined flour (maida) ¼ cup wheat starch or cornflour Salt to taste
  - 2 teaspoons sugar
  - 1 teaspoon garlic powder
  - 3-4 dried shitake mushrooms, soaked and chopped
  - 2 tablespoons oil + for deep fryingTo serve Fried chopped garlic Spring onion greens, diagonally sliced Fresh red chillies, diagonally sliced Soy-ginger dip to serve

METHOD:
  1. Boil sufficient water in a deep non-stick pan, add white radish strips and boil for 4 minutes.
  2. Drain them and transfer into a bowl of ice cold water.
  3. Add carrot strips to the same pan and boil for 4 minutes.
  4. Drain them and transfer into another bowl of ice cold water.
  5. To make batter, take rice flour, refined flour, and wheat starch in a large bowl.
  6. Add grated radish, salt, sugar, garlic powder, onion powder, and white pepper powder and 3 cups water and mix till well combined.
  7. Heat 2 tablespoons oil in a non-stick pan.
  8. Add mushrooms and sauté on high heat for 2-3 minutes.
  9. Drain white radish strips and carrot strips and add to the pan and sauté well.
  10. Switch off the heat, add the batter and stir immediately to avoid any lump formation.
  11. Transfer the mixture into a 6” x 4” square silicon cake mould and level out the top.
  12. Heat sufficient water in a steamer.
  13. Place the cake mould in the steamer and steam for 1 hour 5 minutes.
  14. Switch the heat off and allow to rest for 5 minutes.
  15. Remove the cake mould from the steamer and allow to cool down to room temperature.
  16. Place it in the refrigerator for 6-8 hours or till completely chilled.
  17. De-mould the cake and cut into 1 inch thick squares.
  18. These are the radish cakes.
  19. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  20. Gently slide in the squares, a few at a time, and deep-fry till golden brown and crisp.
  21. Drain on absorbent paper.
  22. Arrange the radish cakes on a serving plate and garnish with fried garlic, spring onion greens and fresh red chillies.
  23. Serve hot with soy-ginger dip.

RECIPE 171: Ragi Jaggery Cookies
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Ragi-Jaggery-Cookies.html

A nutritious twist on the classic cookie, blending wholesome ragi flour with the natural sweetness of jaggery for a delicious treat. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Ragi flour, Jaggery powder | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2-3 tablespoons milk
  - 1-2 tablespoon chocolate chips

METHOD:
  1. Preheat the oven to 180º C.
  2. Line a baking tray with parchment paper.
  3. Mix together ragi flour, cocoa powder and baking soda in a bowl.
  4. Cream together butter and jaggery powder in another bowl till soft and creamy.
  5. Add the flour mixture and fold in.
  6. Add milk and mix well.
  7. Divide the mixture into small equal portions, shape them into balls and flatten them a little.
  8. Arrange them on the tray keeping them 1 inch apart.
  9. Place the chocolate chips on top.
  10. Put the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 10-15 minutes.
  11. Remove from oven and allow to cool.
  12. Arrange the cookies on a serving plate and serve.

RECIPE 172: Ragi Oats Cookies With Banana Milkshake
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Ragi-Oats-Cookies-With-Banana-Milkshake.html

If you are a health freak, then this combination of ragi cookies and banana milkshake is just right for you This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Ragi oats cookies, Finger millet (ragi) flour | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 ripe banana
  - 2 cups milk
  - 2 tablespoons peanut butter
  - 1 tablespoon honey

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 180º C.
  2. Sift together roasted millet flour, wheat flour and powdered sugar into a bowl.
  3. Add oats and mix well.
  4. Add baking powder and butter and rub it in with finger tips till you get a breadcrumb like texture.
  5. Add vanilla essence and milk and knead into soft dough.
  6. Grease your palms with a little oil, divide the dough into equal parts and shape them into cookies.
  7. Place the cookies on a baking tray and bake for 15-20 minutes.
  8. For milkshake, peel and chop banana and put it into a smoothie jar.
  9. Add milk, peanut butter and honey and blend till smooth.
  10. Remove the cookies from oven and set aside to cool.
  11. Once cooled, pack them in tiffin.
  12. Pour the milkshake into a mug flask.

RECIPE 173: Ragi Oats Dhokla
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Ragi-Oats-Dhokla.html

Savor the wholesome goodness of our Ragi Oats Dhokla, a nutritious twist on a traditional favorite, combining the richness of ragi and oats with the tangy flavors of dhokla. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Finger millet (ragi) flour, Oats | Cuisine: Gujarati | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup finger millet (ragi) flour ½ cup oats, powdered ½ cup split skinless black gram (dhuli urad dal) flour ⅓ cup yogurt (dahi) Salt to taste ½ teaspoon cumin powder ½ teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon ginger-green chilli paste ½ teaspoon baking soda
  - 1 tablespoon oil + for greasing Green chutney to serveTempering
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon mustard seeds
  - 2 teaspoons white sesame seeds
  - 6-8 curry leaves
  - 1 teaspoon sugar Chopped fresh coriander leaves for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Combine together finger millet flour, oats powder, split skinless black gram flour, yogurt and 1¼ cups water and whisk till a smooth batter is formed.
  2. Cover and set aside to ferment for 6-8 hours.
  3. Add salt, cumin powder, red chilli powder, ginger-green chilli paste and baking soda and mix well.
  4. Brush a dhokla thali with some oil.
  5. Add 1 tablespoon oil into the batter and mix well.
  6. Pour this into the greased thali.
  7. Heat sufficient water in a steamer.
  8. Place the thali into the steamer basket.
  9. Cover and steam for 12-15 minutes.
  10. Remove the thali and allow to cool slightly.
  11. Scrape the sides of the thali and cut into squares.
  12. To make the tempering, heat oil in a pan.
  13. Add mustard seeds and let them splutter.
  14. Add white sesame seeds, green chillies, curry leaves and sugar and mix well.
  15. Add ¼ cup water and mix well.
  16. Pour this onto the dhokla.
  17. Garnish with coriander leaves.
  18. Serve with green chutney.

RECIPE 174: Rainbow Idli with Beet Ketchup
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Rainbow-Idli-with-Beet-Ketchup.html

These rainbow idlis made with different coloured vegetables and nuts are served with ruby red ketchup made with beetroots This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Readymade idli batter, Beetroot | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 cups readymade idli batter Oil for greasing Salt to taste
  - 10-12 blueberries ½ cup chopped nuts ½ cup green peas, lightly crushed
  - 2 tablespoons boiled beetroot pureeBeet ketchup
  - 1 cup boiled beetroot puree ¾ cup apple cider vinegar ½ cup brown sugar
  - 5 spice powder ¼ teaspoon clove powder ½ teaspoon crushed black peppercorns
  - 2 tablespoons tomato puree Salt to taste

METHOD:

RECIPE 176: Rajasthani Kaddu ki Sabzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/rajasthani-kaddu-ki-sabzi-7080510

A simple and tasty Rajasthani preparation of red pumpkin or kaddu which is full of spices and flavours. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Rajasthani | Course: Main Course- Vegetarian Prep time 8-10 minutes | Cook Time: 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 inch cubes
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ½ teaspoon asafoetida (hing)
  - 2 small onions, sliced
  - 1 inch cubes ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ¾ teaspoon red chilli powder ¾ teaspoon coriander powder Salt to taste ½ teaspoon dry mango powder (amchur) ½ teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 2 tablespoons chopped fresh coriander leaves

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add cumin seeds and let them change colour.
  2. Add asafoetida and onion and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  3. Add potatoes, mix and sauté for 1 minute.
  4. Add turmeric powder, red chilli powder, and mix well.
  5. Add coriander powder and salt, mix and sauté for a few seconds.
  6. Add pumpkin, mix well.
  7. Sprinkle ¼ cup water, mix, cover and cook for 8-10 minutes or till the vegetables are ¾ cooked.
  8. Add dry mango powder and garam masala powder, mix and cook for a minute.
  9. Add coriander leaves and take the pan off the heat.
  10. Transfer the sabzi into a serving bowl and serve hot.

RECIPE 177: Rajasthani Raab
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/rajasthani-raab-7080628

A lightly-flavoured porridge or a kanji made with maize flour that is a healthy meal in itself. Ideal for winters so do try this. An important tip, it is best to simmer it in earthen cookware for that absolute rustic feel.

Cuisine: Rajasthani | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 8-10 minutes | Cook Time: 30-35 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup yogurt ¾ cup maize flour (makai ka atta) Salt to tasteTempering
  - 1½ teaspoons cumin seeds
  - 3-4 green chillies, slit
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander leaves Roasted cumin powder for garnish Red chilli powder for garnish

METHOD:
  1. To make buttermilk, take yogurt in a large jug.
  2. Add 3 cups water and mix with a help of a wooden churner.
  3. Take maize flour in a large bowl, add 1 cup of the buttermilk and mix till a lump free batter is formed.
  4. Add the remaining buttermilk and mix.
  5. Heat a non-stick deep pan.
  6. Add the mixture and mix well.
  7. Stir occasionally and cook for 20-25 minutes on medium heat.
  8. Add salt and mix well.
  9. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan.
  10. Add cumin seeds and let them change colour.
  11. Add green chillies and mix well.
  12. Pour this into the prepared mixture and mix well.
  13. Add coriander leaves and mix till well combined.
  14. Transfer the raab into serving bowls, garnish with roasted cumin powder and red chilli powder.

RECIPE 178: Rawa Vegetable Pancakes
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Rawa-Vegetable-Pancakes-.html

Enjoy a crispy and wholesome twist on pancakes with our Rawa Vegetable Pancakes, bursting with nutritious veggies and savory flavors in every bite. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3 tablespoons yogurt ¼ cup grated carrots ¼ cup frozen green peas
  - 1 small onion, chopped
  - 1 small capsicum, chopped
  - 2 green chillies, chopped A pinch of sugar Crushed black peppercorns to taste ¼ teaspoon red chilli powder Salt to taste Oil as required Green chutney to serve

  2. Add carrots, green peas, onion, capsicum, green chillies, sugar, crushed black peppercorns, red chilli powder, and salt.

RECIPE 179: Reshmi Paneer
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Reshmi-Paneer-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

Paneer pieces cooked in spicy creamy onion tomato masala with capsicum. Savoring the silkiness of Reshmi Paneer – where succulence meets sophistication. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Cottage cheese (paneer), Oil | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 1 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 250 gms cottage cheese (paneer)
  - 3 tbsps oil ½ tsp cumin seeds
  - 2 medium onions, thickly sliced
  - 2 tsps ginger paste
  - 2 tsps garlic paste ¼ tsp turmeric powder
  - 1 tsp coriander powder ½ tsp red chilli powder
  - 2 tbsps cashewnuts paste ¼ cup yogurt
  - 3 tbsps tomato puree
  - 1 large green capsicum, cut into thick strips
  - 1 large yellow capsicum, cut into thick strips
  - 1 large red capsicum, cut into thick strips
  - 2 medium tomatoes, cut into thick strips Salt to taste A pinch of garam masala powder A pinch of green cardamom powder
  - 2 tbsps crumbled mawa / khoya
  - 2 tbsps cream A few sprigs fresh coriander leaves

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick wok, add cumin seeds and onions and saute.
  2. Cut cottage cheese into thick fingers.
  3. When onions soften, add ginger paste and garlic paste and saute for 1 minute.
  4. Add turmeric powder, coriander powder and red chilli powder, mix and saute.
  5. Add cashewnuts paste and mix.
  6. Add yogurt and mix.
  7. Add tomato puree and mix.
  8. Add green, yellow and red capsicums, tomatoes and mix.
  9. Saute for1 minute.
  10. Add salt, cottage cheese fingers, garam masala powder, green cardamom powder, crumbled mawa and cream and mix.
  11. Simmer for 2 minutes.
  12. Chop coriander leaves and add.
  13. Transfer into a serving bowl and serve hot.

RECIPE 180: Rice Gnocchi Aglio Olio
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Rice-Gnocchi-Aglio-Olio.html

Rice flour gnocchi steamed to perfection and tossed in a herbed garlic-chili butter sauce, finished with parmesan and fresh parsley. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Gnocchi, Rice flour | Cuisine: Italian | Course: Noodles and Pastas | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup rice flour Salt to taste
  - 1/2 tablespoons olive oil
  - 1 tablespoon chopped garlic
  - 1/2 tablespoon red chilli flakes
  - 1 tablespoons chopped fresh mixed herbs (thyme, oregano, and rosemary)
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh parsley Salt to taste Crushed black peppercorns to taste
  - 1 teaspoon butter
  - 1 tablespoon parmesan cheese powder Fresh parsley sprig to garnish Parmesan cheese shavings to garnish

METHOD:
  1. To make the gnocchi, Heat 1 cup water, salt, oil and turmeric powder in a deep pan.
  2. Let the mixture come to boil.
  3. Gradually add the rice flour and mix with a wooden ladle till it starts forming a dough.
  4. Transfer the dough onto the worktop, and knead the dough with a small greased stainless steel bowl.
  5. Once the dough is warm, knead with your hand till a soft dough is formed.
  6. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and let it rest for 15-20 minutes.
  7. To make gnocchi, grease your hands with a mixture of oil and water and divide the dough into small portions, around 5 grams each.
  8. Press each portion on the back of a fork and roll it.
  9. This is a gnocchi.
  10. Heat sufficient water in a steamer, arrange the gnocchi on the steamer basket, cover and steam for 8-10 minutes.
  11. Transfer them into a bowl and drizzle some oil over them.
  12. To make the sauce, heat olive oil in a non-stick pan.
  13. Add garlic and red chilli flakes, mix and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  14. Add chopped herbs and parsley, mix sauté for a few seconds.
  15. Add the gnocchi and toss them well.
  16. Add salt and crushed black peppercorns and toss again.
  17. Continue to cook for 2-3 minutes.
  18. Add butter and parmesan cheese powder and mix gently till well combined.
  19. Transfer onto a serving plate, garnish with parsley sprig and parmesan cheese shavings.
  20. Serve hot.

RECIPE 181: Rice Kurkure
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/rice-kurkure-7368693

Leftover rice transforms into this light, spicy and chatpata snack that’s popular among kids. You can serve this for teatime too. This is Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters Prep time 5-6 minutes | Cook Time: 8-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2½ tablespoons corn flour
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder ¼ teaspoon baking soda Salt to taste Oil for deep frying Spice mix
  - 1 teaspoon chaat masala ¼ teaspoon citric acid ¼ teaspoon red chilli powder

METHOD:
  1. Put cooked rice in a mixer jar, add ½ cup water, and grind to a fine paste.
  2. Transfer into a large bowl.
  3. Add gram flour, corn flour, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, baking soda, and salt.
  4. Add ¼ cup water and whisk till a smooth batter is formed.
  5. Transfer the mixture into a squeezy bottle.
  6. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  7. Squeeze out small strips of the mixture into the hot oil and deep fry till golden brown and crisp.
  8. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  9. Take chaat masala in a wide shallow bowl.
  10. Add citric acid, red chilli powder and mix well.
  11. Add the fried rice sticks and gently toss.
  12. Serve.

RECIPE 182: Roasted Pumpkin Soup
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Roasted-Pumpkin-Soup.html

Red pumpkin is a very healthy vegetable being rich in vitamins, minerals and antioxidants. And all these nutrients are so good for growing children as also adults This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Red pumpkin, Olive oil | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Soups | Prep Time: 10-15 minutes | Cook Time: 1-1.30 hour | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 400 grams red pumpkin, seeded and cut into thick slices
  - 2 inches leek, chopped
  - 2 inches cinnamon
  - 2 teaspoons smoked paprika
  - 2 teaspoons brown sugar
  - 2-3 brown bread slices
  - 3 cups vegetable stock
  - 1 tablespoon fresh cream Pumpkin seeds to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Preheat oven to 160º C.
  2. Grease a baking tray with 2 tbsps of olive oil, spread the pumpkin slices on it, add sea salt, black peppercorns, star anise, leeks, onion and cinnamon.
  3. Sprinkle smoked paprika on top, add brown sugar, balsamic vinegar, thyme and rosemary.
  4. Place the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 1 hour.
  5. Trim the edges of the brown bread slices and cut into small cubes.
  6. Spread the bread cubes on another baking tray, drizzle remaining olive oil, toss well and place the tray in the preheated oven and toast for 10 minutes.
  7. Insert a toothpick through the pumpkin slices to check if they are done.
  8. Remove the tray from the oven, peel the pumpkin and chop roughly.
  9. Transfer the roasted pumpkin into a mixer jar, add 1 cup vegetable stock and blend into a smooth puree.
  10. Heat a deep non-stick pan, add the pumpkin puree, remaining stock and mix well.
  11. Bring the mixture to a boil.
  12. Add fresh cream and mix well and remove the pan from heat.
  13. Pour the soup into a jug and then gently into a thermos flask.
  14. Garnish with some pumpkin seeds and cover the flask.
  15. Pack the baked croutons in an airtight container to serve with soup.

RECIPE 183: Sabudana Papad
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sabudana-papad---SK-Khazana.html

A crispy and light Indian snack made from tapioca pearls (sabudana), seasoned with spices, and sun-dried to perfection. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup sago Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds Oil to deep fry

METHOD:

RECIPE 184: Sabudana Vada
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/-SABUDANA-VADA.html

Crispy, crunchy and 'oh so good' - Sabudana Vadas are an all-time favourite snack for everyone. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Sago (sabudana), Chutney | Cuisine: Indian,Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 6-7 hour | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ sago (sabudana), soaked Chutney ½ cup scrapped fresh coconut ½ cup fresh coriander leaves
  - 1 green chilli ½ teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1½ tablespoons powdered sugar A pinch of salt Vada
  - 3 medium potatoes, boiled, peeled and mashed
  - 2 teaspoons ginger-green chilli paste Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds ¾ cup roasted and crushed peanuts ½ lemon Oil for greasing + for deep frying

METHOD:
  1. To make the chutney, put coconut in a mixer jar, add coriander leaves, green chilli, cumin seeds, roasted peanuts, salt and ¼ cup water and grind to a fine paste.
  2. To make sweetened yogurt, take yogurt in a bowl.
  3. Add powdered sugar and salt and mix well.
  4. To make the vada mixture, take soaked sago in a large plate.
  5. Add potatoes, ginger-green chilli paste, salt, cumin seeds, peanuts and squeeze the juice of lemon and mix till well combined.
  6. Grease your palms with oil, take a portion of the vada mixture, shape it into a ball and slightly flatten it to shape like a vada.
  7. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  8. Gently slide in the vades into the hot oil and deep fry till golden brown and crisp.
  9. Drain on an absorbent paper.
  10. Serve hot with prepared chutney and sweetened yogurt.

RECIPE 185: Saeb Makhane ki Kheer
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Saeb-Makhane-ki-Kheer-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Makhana sautéed in ghee enhances the taste and falvour of this kheer This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Medium apples (saeb), Lotus seeds (makhana) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 6-10 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: Taste Sweet | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium Medium apples (saeb) , grated
  - 1 cup Lotus seeds (makhana)
  - 1/4 cup Ghee
  - 1/4 cup Jaggery , grated
  - 1/4 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 500 millilitres Milk
  - 1 cup Khotya (mawa) , grated to garnish Apple fans

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a non-stick pan, add makhana and sauté till crisp.
  2. Drain and transfer into a bowl and set aside to cool.
  3. Add apples to the ghee remaining in the pan and sauté for 7-8 minutes.
  4. Transfer makhana into a grinder jar and grind to a fine powder.
  5. Add jaggery to the apples and mix till it melts.
  6. Add green cardamom powder and mix well.
  7. Transfer the mixture into another bowl.
  8. Add nuts to the same pan and roast till lightly browned.
  9. Add milk and bring to a boil.
  10. Add makhana powder, mix well and cook till the mixture thickens.
  11. Add khoya and mix till it melts.
  12. Switch off heat, add prepared apple mixture and mix till well combined.
  13. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with apple fans and serve hot.

RECIPE 186: Sambousek
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sambousek-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A delightful Middle Eastern pastry filled with with spicy chenna and spinach mixture, inviting you to savor its crispy exterior and flavorful fillings in every bite. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Readymade whole wheat flour (atta) dough, Carom seeds (ajwain) | Cuisine: Middle Eastern | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 250 grams readymade whole wheat flour (atta) dough
  - 1 teaspoon carom seeds (ajwain)
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped ginger
  - 1 cup grated cottage cheese (chhena)
  - 1½ teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 medium bunch fresh spinach, shredded Salt to taste Oil for basting

METHOD:
  1. Take carom seeds, ginger, cottage cheese, onion, black salt, dried mango powder, garam masala powder, turmeric powder and spinach in a bowl and mix well.
  2. Add salt and mix well.
  3. Divide the dough into equal portions and roll each portion into a disc.
  4. Spread a spoonful of cottage cheese-spinach mixture on each disc and roll into a cylinder.
  5. Roll into a spiral, dust some flour and roll out into medium size discs.
  6. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  7. Place the discs on it, one at a time, and cook, basting with oil and turning sides, till evenly browned on both sides.
  8. Cut each disc into 4 pieces, arrange them on a serving platter and serve with your choice of pickle.


========================================================================
RECIPE 187: Samosa Patti
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Samosa-Patti.html

Samosa patti are broad strips made of wheat or refined flour which serve as an outer covering for the stuffing of samosas This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida), Oil | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup refined flour (maida) + for dusting
  - 3 teaspoons oil + for applying Salt to taste

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a small pan.
  2. Take refined flour in a large bowl.
  3. Add salt and the hot oil and mix till the mixture comes together.
  4. Add ¼ cup water little by little and knead till a soft dough is formed.
  5. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside to rest for 30 minutes.
  6. Divide the dough into 6 equal portions.
  7. Shape each portion into a ball.
  8. Place a dough ball on a worktop and dust with some refined flour.
  9. Roll into a small disc.
  10. Apply some oil and generously dust some refined flour over it.
  11. Place this on a plate.
  12. Dust the worktop with some refined flour again and place another dough ball on it.
  13. Roll it into a small disc.
  14. Repeat this process one more time with another dough ball.
  15. Place the first disc over the second one with the flour side facing each other.
  16. Similarly, place the third disc with the flour side facing down over the sandwiched discs.
  17. Dust some flour on top and roll it into a large thin disc.
  18. Heat a non-stick tawa.
  19. Place the rolled out discs and cook on low heat for a few minutes while rotating the tawa to ensure the discs are uniformly semi-cooked.
  20. Flip and cook the other side for a few minutes as well.
  21. Carefully separate the layers and place a worktop.
  22. Trim the sides and cut into 24cm x 8cm sized thick strips.
  23. Carefully place them in a zip lock bag and keep them in the freezer.
  24. Use as required.

RECIPE 188: Sangam Vada
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sangam-Vada.html

The popular vada pav made differently – potato mixture sandwiched in pavs, dipped in batter and deep-fried This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Potatoes, Pavs | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 pavs
  - 3 green chillies, stemmed and broken
  - 8 garlic cloves ½ inch ginger, roughly chopped
  - 8 curry leaves, shredded
  - 1 tsp turmeric powder Salt to taste
  - 1¼ cups gram flour ¼ cup rice flour
  - 1 tsp red chilli powder ¼ tsp baking soda Date and tamarind chutney to drizzle Green chutney to drizzle Chopped onions to sprinkle Nylon sev to sprinkle

METHOD:
  1. Transfer green chillies, garlic cloves and ginger in a mixer jar and grind coarsely without adding any water.
  2. Heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  3. Add curry leaves and sauté for a few seconds.
  4. Add the prepared paste and sauté for 2 minutes on medium heat.
  5. Add ½ tsp turmeric powder, salt and mix well.
  6. Cook for 30 seconds.
  7. Add the boiled potatoes and mix well.
  8. Sprinkle 2 tbsps water and cook for 2-3 minutes or till the mixture is heated thoroughly.
  9. Add coriander leaves and mix well.
  10. Transfer in a bowl and set aside to cool down.
  11. For the batter, take gram flour in a bowl.
  12. Add rice flour, red chilli powder, remaining turmeric powder, salt, baking soda and mix well.
  13. Add 1¼ cups water and mix well to form a smooth batter.
  14. Slit the pavs without cutting through.
  15. Apply a generous portion of the potato mixture on lower half and close it.
  16. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  17. Dip the pav pieces in the gram flour batter and slide into the hot oil.
  18. Deep fry till golden brown and crisp.
  19. Drain on absorbent paper.
  20. Cut the fried pav sandwich into 4 pieces and transfer on a serving plate.
  21. Drizzle date and tamarind chutney and green chutney on top.
  22. Sprinkle chopped onion, sev and coriander leaves.
  23. Serve immediately.

RECIPE 189: Sattu Baingan Masala
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sattu-Baingan-Masala--Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Brinjals stuffed with spicy sattu mixture, tossed with Indian spices and cooked to perfection. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel.

Main Ingredients: Sattu, Brinjals | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups sattu
  - 8 medium brinjals
  - 1 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 large onion , finely chopped
  - 2 green chillies , finely chopped
  - 1 tablespoon ginger , finely chopped
  - 3 teaspoons red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 2 teaspoons coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds Salt to taste
  - 13 teaspoons mustard oil Fresh coriander sprigs to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Take sufficient water in a bowl, add ½ tsp turmeric powder and mix well.
  2. Slit brinjals without cutting through and immerse in turmeric water.
  3. To prepare the stuffing, take sattu in another bowl, add onion, green chillies, ginger, 2 tsps red chilli powder, remaining turmeric powder, ¼ tsp asafoetida, fennel powder, 1½ tsps dried mango powder, coriander powder, cumin seeds, salt and 6 tsps mustard oil and mix well.
  4. Heat 5 tsps mustard oil in a stainless steel pan till it begins to smoke.
  5. Stuff the brinjals with the sattu mixture, place them in the hot pan, cover and shallow fry on low heat, stirring occasionally, till golden brown on all sides.
  6. Heat another non-stick pan, add remaining mixture of sattu and dry roast till colour darkens.
  7. Spread this on a serving plate.
  8. Heat remaining mustard oil in the same pan, add remaining asafoetida, brinjals, remaining red chilli powder, remaining dried mango powder and mix lightly.
  9. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  10. Place the brinjals over the sattu mixture spread on the serving plate.
  11. Garnish with coriander sprigs and serve hot.

RECIPE 190: Sattu Pancakes
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sattu-Pancakes.html

Enjoy a hearty breakfast with sattu pancakes, combining the wholesome goodness of sattu and whole wheat flour for a delightful morning treat. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Sattu, Yogurt | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup sattu ½ cup yogurt ½ teaspoon baking soda
  - 4 tablespoons butter + as required ½ cup jaggery powder ½ cup whole wheat flour
  - 1 teaspoon baking powder A pinch of salt ¼ teaspoon green cardamom powder ½ teaspoon vanilla essence
  - 1 cup milk Banana slices as required Chopped almonds as required Chopped pistachios as required Maple syrup to serve

METHOD:
  1. Take yogurt in a bowl.
  2. Add baking soda and mix well.
  3. Set aside.
  4. Heat butter in a deep nonstick pan.
  5. Add jaggery powder and cook till butter melts.
  6. Allow to cool slightly.
  7. Sift sattu, whole wheat flour, baking powder and salt in a bowl.
  8. Make a well in the centre, add yogurt mixture, butter -jaggery mixture, green cardamom powder, vanilla essence, milk and whisk well.
  9. Heat a nonstick tawa.
  10. Grease with some butter, spread a ladleful of batter.
  11. Cover and cook on medium heat for 2-3 minutes.
  12. Flip and cook on other side for 2 minutes.
  13. Pile up the pancakes on serving plate.
  14. Arrange banana slices on top.
  15. Sprinkle almonds, pistachios on top.
  16. Place some butter cubes in the centre.
  17. Serve with maple syrup.

RECIPE 191: Shakkarkand Tuk Tuk
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Shakkarkand-Tuk-Tuk-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Tuk is a popular Sindhi side dish that is generally served with Sindhi kadhi and chawal. Here sweet potatoes replace the usual potatoes This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Sweet potatoes (shakkerkand), Oil | Cuisine: Sindhi | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2-3 medium sweet potatoes (shakkarkand), parboiled with skin Oil for deep-frying Spice mix Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon red chili powder
  - 2 teaspoons coriander powder ½ teaspoon dried mango (amchur) powder
  - 1 tablespoon chopped fresh coriander leaves Tomato ketchup to serve Green chutney to serve

METHOD:
  1. Heat sufficient oil in a deep pan.
  2. Cut the sweet potato into thick slices.
  3. Flatten the slices between your palms by pressing a little and deep-fry in hot oil till golden brown and crisp.
  4. Drain on absorbent paper.
  5. To prepare the spice mix, mix together salt, red chilli powder, coriander powder, amchur powder and coriander leaves in a bowl.
  6. While tuk is still hot, sprinkle spice mix over them and toss well.
  7. Insert a toothpick in each tuk and arrange them on a serving plate.
  8. Serve hot with tomato ketchup and green chutney.

RECIPE 192: Shakkarkandi Matar Masala
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Shakkarkandi-Matar-Masala-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Super food sweet potatoes mixed with green peas and some masalas to make a tasty dish. Serve this with choice of your bread. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Sweet potatoes (shakkerkand), Green peas (matar) | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 6-10 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4 medium sweet potatoes (shakkerkand) , scrubbed clean and cut into cubes
  - 1/4 cup green peas (matar)
  - 4 tablespoons sunflower oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 tablespoon ginger , finely chopped
  - 1/2 tablespoons coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon cumin powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1/2 teaspoons dried mango powder (amchur)
  - 10-12 Fresh coriander sprigs + to garnish Fresh red chilli to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat sunflower oil in a non-stick pan, add cumin seeds, ginger and green chillies, stir and sauté till fragrant.
  2. Add sweet potatoes, toss and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  3. Add coriander powder, cumin powder, red chilli powder, turmeric powder, dried mango powder, garam masala powder and salt, mix well and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  4. Add green peas and mix.
  5. Add water as required, cover and cook for 6-8 minutes.
  6. Finely chop coriander leaves, add to the pan and mix.
  7. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with coriander sprigs and red chilli and serve hot.

RECIPE 193: Sheer Payara
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sheer-Payara.html

Simple fudge made with milk powder and some dried fruits This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Sugar, Milk powder | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 1-1.30 hour | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups Milk powder to grease Butter
  - 1 tablespoon Rose water
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 1/4 cup Walnuts and almonds , chopped to garnish Pistachios , chopped
  - 1 tablespoon Sultanas , chopped

METHOD:
  1. Grease a burfi tray with ghee, line with butter paper.
  2. Heat a deep-pan, add sugar and water and bring the mixture to a boil.
  3. Simmer, stirring continuously, till the syrup reaches one string consistency.
  4. Remove the pan from heat and add rose water, green cardamom powder, walnuts, almonds and milk powder and mix well.
  5. Pour the mixture into the greased tray and spread evenly.
  6. Sprinkle pistachios and sultanas and set aside to cool for about an hour.
  7. When the fudge cools, cut into pieces of your preferred shape, remove from tray and serve.

RECIPE 194: Shegaon Kachori
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Shegaon-Kachori.html

A popular street food, these kachoris were first made in Shegaon and therefore the name. Eat one and you will want more and more This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida), Salt | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 41-50 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups refined flour (maida) Salt to taste
  - 1½ tablespoons fennel seeds (saunf)
  - 1 tablespoon coriander seeds
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1 cup gram flour (besan)
  - 1½ ginger-green chilli paste
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon garam masala powder ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste

METHOD:
  1. Take refined flour in a large bowl.
  2. Add salt and oil and mix till the mixture resembles bread crumb consistency.
  3. Add ½ cup water and knead to a stiff dough.
  4. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  5. To make the masala stuffing, dry roast fennel seeds, coriander seeds and cumin seeds till fragrant.
  6. Transfer into a mortar and coarsely crush it with a pestle.
  7. Heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  8. Add ginger-green chilli paste and mix well.
  9. Sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  10. Add red chilli powder, garam masala powder, turmeric powder and salt and sauté for a few seconds.
  11. Add gram flour and roast on low heat for 4-5 minutes.
  12. Add the crushed mixture and mix well.
  13. Set aside to cool completely.
  14. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  15. To make the kachoris, grease the worktop with some oil.
  16. Take a medium sized portion of the dough and shape it into a ball.
  17. Place it on the greased worktop and roll it into a small disc.
  18. Add a portion of the masala stuffing and bring the edges to the centre and press to seal.
  19. Gently press and lightly roll into a small disc.
  20. Gently slide in the kachoris a few at a time and deep fry on medium heat till they turn golden, crisp and lightly puffed.
  21. Serve with fried green chillies.

RECIPE 195: Sitaphal Basundi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sitaphal-Basundi-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Sitaphal adds its unique flavour and texture to this basundi This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Custard apples (sitaphal), Milk | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 51-60 minutes | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 litres Milk
  - 3/4 cup Condensed milk
  - 2 tablespoons Cashewnuts , chopped
  - 2 tablespoons Almonds , chopped
  - 1/2 teaspoon Green cardamom powder a few strands Saffron water , soaked in water to brush Honey
  - 1/2 cup Pistachios , crushed

METHOD:
  1. Boil milk in a deep non-stick pan, stirring frequently, till it is reduced to half.
  2. Keep scraping the sides of the pan and mixing with milk.
  3. Meanwhile break open the custard apples and scoop the seeds and mash through a strainer, to separate the flesh from the seeds, into a bowl.
  4. Some pieces may not get separated from the seeds so collect these pieces in another bowl and remove their seeds.
  5. Add condensed milk, cashewnuts, almonds and green cardamom powder to the reduced milk and mix well.
  6. Cook on low heat for 5-6 minutes or till it thickens a little more.
  7. Scrape the sides occasionally.
  8. Put a ladle of the milk mixture into a bowl, add saffron along with water and mix well.
  9. Refrigerate for 40-50 minutes.
  10. Add the remaining milk mixture to the custard apple pulp.
  11. Add 2 tbsps of chunky pieces.
  12. Mix well.
  13. Refrigerate it for 40-50 minutes.
  14. Brush the rims of serving glasses with honey.
  15. Take crushed pistachios in a plate and roll the rims of the and roll over it.
  16. Fill each serving glass till ¾ with plain sitafal basundi and add 2 spoons of saffron basundi on top.
  17. Serve chilled.

RECIPE 196: Sofiyani Sherbat
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sofiyani-Sherbat--Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Sofiyani Sherbat is best enjoyed cold, making it a perfect beverage to serve during festive gatherings or as a refreshing drink on a warm day.

Main Ingredients: Fennel seeds (saunf), Cumin seeds | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Beverages | Prep Time: 5-10 minutes | Cook Time: 0-5 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet &amp; Sour | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 12 tbsps fennel seeds (saunf)
  - 4 tsps cumin seeds
  - 4 tbsps coriander seeds
  - 6 ½ lemons juice Mint sprigs for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat a non-stick deep pan, add saunf, cumin seeds and coriander seeds.
  2. Dry roast on low heat for 2-3 minutes till saunf is fragrant.
  3. Transfer roasted mixture in a blender.
  4. Add sugar and blend to a fine powder.
  5. Transfer the blended mixture in a bowl.
  6. Add 1 cup water, ice cubes as required, black salt and lemon juice.
  7. Mix well.
  8. Remove some ice cubes and add in a serving glass.
  9. Strain the sherbet in another bowl and add ice cubes.
  10. Transfer mixture in the serving glass and garnish with mint sprigs.
  11. Serve cold.

========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Soya-Aloo-Tahiri-Pulao-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

This is recipe is so simple yet so very tasty and nutritious too This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

RECIPE 198: Soya Keema Sheperd's Pie
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Soya-Keema-Sheperd&#x27;s-Pie.html

Soya granules contain immunity building nutrients, protein, iron and zinc besides being rich in dietary fiber. They are an excellent substitute for mutton keema This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Soya granules, Potatoes | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium onion, chopped
  - 1 medium tomato, chopped
  - 1 inch ginger, chopped ½ cup chopped fresh coriander leaves
  - 2 green chillies
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 3-4 black peppercorns
  - 3-4 cloves ½ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 2 teaspoons red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon garam masala powder ¼ cup frozen green peas Salt to taste
  - 2 large potatoes, boiled
  - 2 tablespoons butter
  - 2 tablespoons fresh cream ½ teaspoon chaat masala
  - 4 tablespoons fresh breadcrumbs

METHOD:
  1. Put onion, tomato, garlic, ginger, fresh coriander, green chillies and ¼ cup water and blend into a coarse paste.
  2. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add fennel seeds, cinnamon, bay leaf, black peppercorn and cloves and sauté until fragrant.
  3. Add half the prepared paste and sauté well.
  4. Add soya granules and mix well.
  5. Add ½ cup of water and combine to mix, add ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder, red chilli powder, garam masala powder and mix well.
  6. Add green peas, salt and mix well, cook for 2 minutes and remove the pan from heat.
  7. Preheat the oven to 200º C.
  8. Cut the potatoes into small pieces, transfer into a bowl and mash with a masher.
  9. Add butter, fresh cream and mix well, add remaining turmeric powder, chaat masala, salt and mix well.
  10. Transfer this mixture into a piping bag fitted with star nozzle.
  11. Take a bake proof glass tiffin, add the soya mixture, pipe out the mashed potatoes on top.
  12. Spread breadcrumbs on top, keep the tiffin in the oven and bake for 5 minutes.
  13. Remove it from the oven, let it cool and cover with the lid.

RECIPE 199: Soyabean Granules Sabzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/soyabean-granules-sabzi-7188956

Protein-rich soya granules cooked in a simple tomato-onion semi-dry version. Tastes great even with chapatis or stuff between bread slices for a variation of sandwich.

Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Cook Time: 15-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild Level of cooking Easy | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 200 grams soyabean granules
  - 2 cups warm milk
  - 3 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 3 medium onions, finely chopped
  - 1 tbsp ginger-green chilli paste
  - 3 medium tomatoes, chopped
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon turmeric powder Salt to taste ¼ cup chopped fresh coriander leaves + for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Wash soyabean granules with lukewarm water.
  2. Drain and then soak in warm milk for ½ hour.
  3. Heat oil in a non-stick pan.
  4. Add cumin seeds.
  5. When they start to change colour, add onions and sauté till golden brown.
  6. Add ginger-green chilli paste and cook for ½ minute.
  7. Add tomatoes and cook for 4-5 minutes.
  8. Add red chilli powder and turmeric powder.
  9. Cook till the oil separates.
  10. Add soyabean granules and mix well.
  11. Cover and cook till soya granules are cooked.
  12. These normally take about 10 minutes.
  13. Add a little water if required.
  14. Add salt and cook till it is almost dry.
  15. Add coriander leaves, mix and cook for a few seconds.
  16. Serve hot garnished with coriander leaves.

RECIPE 200: Spinach Fried Rice
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Spinach-Fried-Rice-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

The ever popular fried rice made more nutritious with the addition of spinach This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Fresh spinach leaves, Spinach puree | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Rice | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 6-8 Fresh spinach leaves
  - 4 tablespoons Spinach puree
  - 3 cups Basmati rice , cooked
  - 1 tablespoon Oil
  - 2 tablespoons Garlic , finely choppped
  - 2 Green chillies , finely chopped
  - 8-10 French beans , finely chopped
  - 1/4 cup Cabbage , shredded
  - 1 tablespoon Soy sauce
  - 1-2 Spring onions with geens

METHOD:
  1. Heat oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic and sauté till fragrant.
  2. Add sesame seeds and green chillies, mix and sauté till the seeds pop.
  3. Transfer the mixture into a bowl and set aside.

  5. Add salt and mix.
  6. Add basmati rice and toss.
  7. Roughly chop spinach leaves and spring onions.
  8. Reserve some spring onion greens for garnishing and add the rest to the pan along with spinach leaves and toss well.
