RECIPE 201: Strawberry Kalakand
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Strawberry-Kalakand-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Strawberry syrup takes the popular Kalakand to another level This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Strawberry syrup, Milk | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 4-5 tbsps for drizzling Strawberry syrup
  - 1/2 cup Milk
  - 1/2 cup Cottage cheese (paneer) , grated for greasi tablespoons Ghee
  - 1/4 cup + to sprinkle Almonds , chopped
  - 1/4 cup + to sprinkle Walnuts , chopped
  - 1/4 cup +G to sprinkle Pistachios , chopped
  - 1/4 cup + to sprinkle Cashewnuts , chopped
  - 1 teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 1/2 cup Khoya , grated

METHOD:

  5. Add khoya and mix well.
  6. Grease a barfi tray with some ghee.
  7. Sprinkle some mixed nuts and drizzle some strawberry syrup in it.
  8. Spread the cooked mixture evenly in it and set aside for 3-4 hours or till cooled.

  10. Cut into pieces and serve.

RECIPE 202: Strawberry Shahi Tukda
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Strawberry-Shahi-Tukda---Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

This royal traditional sweet dish is further enhanced with strawberry syrup This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Strawberry syrup, White bread slices | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 6-10 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 8 White bread slices to deep fry Ghee
  - 2 teaspoons Green cardamom powder
  - 1/4 cup Khoya , grated as required Fresh strawberries to garnish Rabdi to garnish Pistachios , blanched and slivered

METHOD:
  1. Cut bread slices into roundels with a medium sized cookie cutter.
  2. Heat sufficient ghee in a kadai and deep-fry the bread roundels till golden brown and crisp.
  3. Drain on absorbent paper.
  4. Heat Hersheys Strawberry Syrup in a non-stick pan.
  5. Add green cardamom powder and mix well.
  6. Add fried bread roundels, stir and cook till the bread slightly softens.
  7. Transfer the bread roundels onto a serving plate.
  8. Add khoya to the pan and mix till it melts.
  9. Pour the mixture on top of the bread roundels.
  10. Make fans of fresh strawberries.
  11. Top the bread roundels with some rabdi and strawberry fans, sprinkle pistachios, drizzle some strawberry syrup and serve warm.

RECIPE 204: Superpowder laddoos
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Superpowder-laddoos-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

These laddoos are not only delicious they are a power house of essential nutrients This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Whole green gram (sabut moong), Walnuts | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: Preparation Time | Cook Time: Cooking Time | Serve: Taste Sweet | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 10-12 Walnuts
  - 1/2 cup Short grain rice (kolam)
  - 1/2 cup Wheat grain
  - 1 tablespo for greasing Ghee
  - 1/4 teaspoon Green cardamom powder

METHOD:
  1. Dry roast green gram in a non-stick pan, on low heat, till golden brown.
  2. Transfer into a bowl.
  3. Dry roast walnuts in the same pan, on low heat, till golden.
  4. Transfer into same bowl.
  5. Dry roast rice in the same pan, on low heat, till light brown.
  6. Transfer into the same bowl.
  7. Dry roast wheat grains in the same pan, on low heat, till light golden.
  8. Transfer into the same bowl.
  9. Dry roast dried coconut, on low heat, till light brown.
  10. Transfer into same bowl.
  11. Mix everything and set aside to cool.
  12. Put the roasted mixture into a grinder jar and grind to a fine powder.
  13. Heat a non-stick pan, add jaggery and ¼ cup water and cook, on low heat, till jaggery melts completely.
  14. Add ghee and mix well.
  15. Add the powdered mixture and green cardamom powder and mix well.
  16. Cook on low heat for 8-10 minutes or till the mixture leaves the sides of the pan.
  17. Transfer into a plate and spread it.
  18. When mixture is slightly warm, grease your palms with ghee, take small portions of the mixture and shape into small sized laddoos and keep on a plate and let them cool down to room temperature.
  19. Keep the laddoos in mini paper cups, arrange on a serving plate and serve.

RECIPE 205: Sweet Khichdi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sweet-Khichdi.html

A typical saraswat sweet made usually during the month of Shravan. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Broken wheat (dalia/lapsi), Split Bengal gram (chana dal) | Cuisine: Karnataka | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups Split Bengal gram (chana dal) , soaked
  - 2 cups Sugar
  - 1/4 cup + for garnishing Cashewnuts
  - 1/4 cup + for garnishing Raisins
  - 1/2 cup + for garnishing Fresh coconut , scraped ½ teaspoon Green cardamom powder
  - 2 tablespoons Ghee

METHOD:
  1. Put wheat and Bengal gram in a pressure cooker, add 7 cups water and cook under pressure till 1 whistle.
  2. Reduce heat and cook for 7-8 minutes.
  3. To prepare sugar syrup, heat sugar in a deep non-stick pan.
  4. Add 1 cup water, mix and cook till the syrup reaches one string consistency.
  5. Add broken wheat-Bengal gram mixture and mix well.
  6. Add cashewnuts and raisins, mix, cover and cook on low heat for 5-6 minutes.
  7. Add coconut, cardamom powder and ghee and mix well.
  8. Serve hot garnished with coconut, cashewnuts and raisins.

RECIPE 206: Sweet Momo Curry
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sweet-Momo-Curry-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Momos stuffed with sweet coconut mixture and cooked in This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Refined flour (maida), Ghee | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups for dusting Refined flour (maida) for applyi tablespoons Ghee a pinch Salt
  - 4 tablespoons Sugar
  - 1 tablespo to garnish Mixed nuts (almonds and pistachios) , chopped
  - 1 cup Fresh coconut , scraped
  - 1 cup Jaggery , chopped

METHOD:
  1. Take refined flour in a bowl.
  2. Add 1 tbsp ghee, salt, 1 tbsp sugar, 3 tbsps coconut milk and a pinch of green cardamom powder and mix well.
  3. Add sufficient water and knead to medium stiff dough.
  4. Apply ghee on the dough, cover with muslin cloth and set aside to rest.
  5. To make filling, heat remaining ghee in a stainless steel pan, add mixed nuts and coconut and sauté lightly.
  6. Add jaggery and switch off heat.
  7. Stir till the jaggery melts, add a pinch of green cardamom powder.
  8. Switch on heat and cook on low heat till pan is hot and switch off heat again.
  9. Transfer into a bowl and set aside to cool.
  10. Divide the dough into equal portions.
  11. Take water in a bowl.
  12. Dust flour on the worktop, roll each portion into a thin disc.
  13. Apply water on the edges.
  14. Place some filling in the centre, fold in the sides and seal the edges to make momos.
  15. Heat ¾ cup water in a copper based stainless steel pan, add remaining coconut milk and stir well.
  16. Add the momos, remaining green cardamom powder and remaining sugar and mix well.
  17. Keep stirring continuously gently.
  18. Cook for 10-12 minutes on low heat.
  19. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with mixed nuts and serve immediately.

RECIPE 207: Sweet Potato Chips
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Sweet-Potato-Chips---SK-Khazana.html

Slice sweet potatoes thinly, season with salt and your favourite spices, then bake or fry until crispy for a delicious and healthy snack of Sweet Potato Chips. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Sweet potatoes, Sendha namak | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium sweet potatoes washed Sendha namak to taste Oil for deep-frying

METHOD:
  1. Take sufficient water in a large bowl, add sendha namak and mix well.
  2. Thinly slice sweet potatoes on a slicer and soak them in the slated water .
  3. Drain and place sweet potato slices on a muslin cloth and pat them dry.
  4. Set aside for 15-20 minutes.
  5. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai, deep fry the slices till golden brown and crisp.

RECIPE 208: Taazi Haldi aur Gajar ki Sabzi
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Taazi-Haldi-aur-Gajar-ki-Sabzi.html

A unique dish made with fresh turmeric and carrot which is luscious and easy to make. Fresh turmeric and carrots cooked with Indian spices and served. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Fresh turmeric (taazi haldi), Carrot | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cups fresh turmeric (taazi haldi) , chopped
  - 1 medium carrot , chopped
  - 2-3 tablespoons ghee
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1/4 teaspoon asafoetida
  - 2 tablespoons crushed ginger-garlic-green chillies
  - 1 large onion , chopped Salt to taste
  - 1/4 cup yogurt
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder
  - 1/2 tablespoon cumin powder
  - 1 tablespoon coriander powder
  - 5-6 tablespoons fresh coriander leaves , chopped

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a non-stick kadai, add cumin seeds and saute till they change colour.
  2. Add asafoetida and crushed ginger-garlic-green chillies, mix and saute for 1-2 minutes.
  3. Add onion, mix and saute till translucent.
  4. Add fresh turmeric and carrot, mix well and saute for 2-3 minutes.
  5. Add salt, mix, cover and cook on medium heat for 6-8 minutes.
  6. Add yogurt, red chilli powder, cumin powder, coriander powder, a little salt and 3 tbsps coriander leaves and mix well.
  7. Cover and cook for 2-3 minutes or till ghee surfaces.
  8. Add remaining coriander leaves and mix well.
  9. Transfer the sabzi into a serving bowl, garnish with coriander leaves and serve hot.

RECIPE 209: Tandoori Phalo ka Guldasta
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Tandoori-Phalo-ka-Guldasta-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

A vibrant bouquet of tandoor-roasted fruits, bursting with flavors and colors, promising a unique culinary experience. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Pear, Pineapple | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 16-20 minutes | Cook Time: 6-10 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 medium pear
  - 1 inch cubes
  - 1 medium red apple
  - 2 medium ripe bananas
  - 3 tablespoons malt vinegar
  - 2 tablespoons mustard oil
  - 1 tablespoon tamarind paste
  - 1 tablespoon red chilli powder
  - 1 teaspoon coriander powder ½ teaspoon black pepper powder ¼ teaspoon green cardamom powder
  - 1½ tablespoons honey + to drizzle Salt to taste Chaat masala to sprinkle Roasted white sesame seeds to sprinkle Green chutney to serve Lemon wedge to serve Onion rings to serve Micro greens to serve

METHOD:
  1. Cut pear into 1 inch cubes and put into a bowl.
  2. Add pineapple cubes.
  3. Cut apple into 1 inch cubes, peel and cut the bananas into thick slices and transfer into the same bowl.
  4. Take malt vinegar, mustard oil, tamarind paste, red chilli powder, coriander powder, black pepper powder, green cardamom powder, brown sugar and honey in another bowl.
  5. Add salt and mix well.
  6. Pour ¾ of this marinade over fruits and mix well.
  7. String the cut fruits onto skewers in the following sequence: pear, apple, pineapple, banana and apple.
  8. Heat a non-stick grill pan, place the skewers and grill the fruits on medium heat, rotating the skewers and drizzling remaining marinade over the fruits till they turn golden brown on all sides and grill marks appear.
  9. Remove onto a serving plate.
  10. Sprinkle chaat masala and roasted white sesame seeds, and drizzle honey.
  11. Serve hot with green chutney, lemon wedge, onion rings and micro greens.

RECIPE 210: Teen Dal ke Dahi Bhalle
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/teen-dal-ke-dahi-bhalle-family-food-tales-4754243

Make the ultra popular Delhi ka chaat even more interesting by combining the magic of three Dals into Dahi Bhalle. Try this delicious recipe to satiate your next chatpate cravings!

Main Ingredients: Split Skinless Green Gram, Split Skinless Black Gram, Split Bengal Gram | Cuisine: Punjabi | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 40-50 minutes Cook Time 10-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Vegetarian

INGREDIENTS:
  - 40 minutes and drained
  - 40 minutes and drained Salt to taste
  - 2 teaspoons ginger-green chilli paste Oil for deep frying
  - 4 teaspoons castor sugar ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing)
  - 2 cups chilled yogurt ½ teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon roasted cumin powder + to sprinkle A pinch of yellow chilli powder Date and tamarind chutney to drizzle Chopped fresh coriander leaves to sprinkle Green chutney to drizzle

METHOD:
  1. Grind all the dals with little water and transfer in a bowl.
  2. Beat well to incorporate air.
  3. Add salt, ginger-green chilli paste and mix well.
  4. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  5. Apply some water on palm, take a portion of batter and make a hole in the centre.
  6. Deep fry till golden brown and crisp.

  8. Add 1 tsp castor sugar, salt and asafoetida and mix well.

RECIPE 211: Tofu Bhurji Wrap with Pickled Veggies
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Tofu-Bhurji-Wrap-with-Pickled-Veggies.html

Tofu as is well known is a rich source of proteins and vegetables are full of vitamins so when you combine them to make a tasty wrap it is bound to be high in nutrition This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: split green gram with skin (chilkewali moong dal), Turmeric powder | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 7-8 hour | Cook Time: 31-40 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 6-8 hours and drained ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 2 green chillies Salt to taste Oil for greasing and drizzling Tofu Bhurji
  - 200 grams silken tofu
  - 1 tablespoon oil
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped
  - 1 small tomato, finely chopped
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1-2 green chillies, finely chopped ¼ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon asafoetida
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped fresh coriander leaves Salt to tastePickled Vegetables
  - 1 cup vinegar
  - 1 tablespoon sea salt
  - 1 tablespoon sugar
  - 1 medium carrot, cut into sticks
  - 1 medium beetroot, cut into sticks
  - 1 medium cucumber, peeled and cut into sticks

METHOD:
  1. For pickled vegetables, heat a non-stick sauce pan, add vinegar, 1 cup water, salt and sugar and bring the mixture to a boil Grind drained green gram with turmeric powder, broken green chillies, salt and some water to a smooth and semi-thick batter.
  2. Transfer into a bowl.
  3. Add carrot, beetroot and cucumber to the vinegar mixture, remove the pan from heat and set aside.
  4. To make the bhurji, heat oil in another non-stick pan, add onion, tomato, cumin seeds and green chillies and sauté well.
  5. Heat a little oil in a non-stick tawa, pour some green gram batter and swirl to make cheela.
  6. Cook turning sides till evenly done on both sides.
  7. Make more cheelas similarly.
  8. Add tofu to the onion tomato mixture and scramble it well, add turmeric powder, red chilli powder and asafoetida and mix well Add coriander leaves and salt, mix well and remove it from heat.
  9. Place each cheela on the work table, keep a spoonful of tofu bhurji in the center and fold the edges from all the sides and secure it with a toothpick.
  10. Pack them in the tiffin box with pickled vegetables.

RECIPE 212: Tofu Chilli Garlic
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Tofu-Chilli-Garlic-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

A delectable and spicy vegetable dish made with tofu and bird’s eye chillies and garlic. Tofu tossed with some garlic and vegetables. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Silken tofu, Bird&#x27;s eye chillies | Cuisine: Indo- Chinese | Course: Main | Prep Time: 11-15 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

  - 2-3 bird's eye chillies
  - 1 tablespoon finely chopped garlic
  - 3-4 tablespoons olive oil
  - 1/2 cup diced mixed capsicums

  - 1/2 small green zucchini , cut into triangles
  - 4-5 small spring onions
  - 1 tablespoon red chilli sauce
  - 1/2 teaspoon soy sauce
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli flakes
  - 3 teaspoons cornflour slurry

METHOD:

  2. Drain them on a plate.
  3. Add yellow and green zucchini to the oil remaining in the same pan and sauté for 2-3 minutes.

Paneer cubes cooked in basil flavoued tomato sauce. Serve this delicious recipe with crispy garlic bread.

  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 2 tablespoons chopped garlic

RECIPE 214: Turai Baskets
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Turai-Baskets-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Deep fried hollowed ridge gourds stuffed with paneer and vegetable mixture, sprinkled with mozzarella cheese and baked This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Ridge gourds (turai), Salt | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Tangy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 2 medium ridge gourds (turai) Salt to taste Chaat masala to sprinkle
  - 1 teaspoon to sprinkle red chilli flakes
  - 1 cup cornflour
  - 2 tablespoons butter
  - 1 tablespoon garlic, chopped
  - 1 teaspoon ginger, chopped
  - 2 teaspoon oil + to deep fry
  - 1 small carrot, finely chopped
  - 2 medium tomatoes, pureed ¼ cup corn kernels, boiled ¼ cup green peas, blanched
  - 1/2 inch pieces
  - 1 teaspoon to sprinkle dried mixed herbs
  - 1 lemon
  - 2 tablespoons grated mozzarella cheese + to sprinkle Red cherry tomatoes to serve Micro greens to serve Edible flowers to serve Red radish, cut into thin strips to serve

METHOD:
  1. Peel the ridge gourds completely.
  2. Trim the ends.
  3. Cut it into half horizontally and scoop out the centre portion to make hollowed cylinders.
  4. Place these cylinders in a bowl, add salt, sprinkle chaat masala and red chilli flakes and mix well.
  5. Take cornflour in another bowl.
  6. Add enough water and make thick slurry.
  7. Heat butter in a non-stick pan, add garlic, ginger and sauté for a minute.
  8. Add 2 tsps oil, carrot and sauté for 1-2 minutes.
  9. Add tomato puree and sauté till oil separates.
  10. Add corn kernels, green peas, capsicum, salt, 1 tsp red chilli flakes and 1 tsp mixed herbs and mix well.
  11. Add cottage cheese and sauté for 2-3 minutes.
  12. Transfer into a bowl.
  13. Halve the lemon, squeeze its juice and add to the cooked mixture.
  14. Mix well and set aside to cool down.
  15. Preheat the oven to 180˚C.
  16. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  17. Squeeze out extra moisture from ridge gourds.
  18. To make ridge gourd baskets, dip them in cornflour slurry, slide into hot oil and deep-fry till golden brown and crisp.
  19. Drain on absorbent paper.
  20. Arrange these baskets on a baking tray.
  21. Add 2 tbsps mozzarella cheese to the cottage cheese mixture and stuff it into the baskets.
  22. Sprinkle mozzarella cheese on top.
  23. Keep the tray in the preheated oven and bake for 3-4 minutes or till cheese melts.
  24. Arrange the baked ridge gourd baskets on a serving platter and sprinkle mixed herbs and red chilli flakes on top.
  25. Serve hot with red cherry tomatoes, micro greens, edible flowers and red radish.

RECIPE 215: Turai Shami Sliders
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Turai-Shami-Sliders-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Turai and chana dal kebabs served on multigrain bread roundels – they are as delicious as they look This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Ridge gourd (turi), Split Bengal gram (chana dal) | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 1.30-2 hour | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 500 grams ridge gourd (turai), peeled and cut ½ inch cubes
  - 1 tablespoon +
  - 1 teaspoon ghee
  - 1 teaspoon chopped garlic
  - 1 teaspoon chopped ginger ¼ teaspoon asafoetida (hing) Salt to taste
  - 4 cheese slices, cut into small roundels Red cherry tomatoes, halved for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat 1 tablespoon ghee in a deep non-stick pan, add garlic, ginger and asafetida sauté for a minute.
  2. Add ridge gourd and sauté for a minute.
  3. Add salt and mix well.
  4. Add red chilli powder, turmeric powder and green chilli and mix well.
  5. Add chana dal and mix well.
  6. Cook for 8-10 minutes.
  7. Switch off heat.
  8. Add breadcrumbs and mix well.

  16. Drizzle ketchup mayo mixture and place a kebab on each.
  17. Cover with cheese slice roundels.
  18. Insert toothpicks with halved red cherry tomatoes and serve immediately.

RECIPE 216: Turmeric Ice Cream - SK Khazana
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Turmeric-Ice-Cream---SK-Khazana.html

It’s fun to make ice cream at home and when made this way you will enjoy it all the more This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Turmeric powder, Milk | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Desserts | Prep Time: 6-7 hour | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 teaspoon Turmeric powder
  - 1/2 cups Fresh cream
  - 1/2 cup Condensed milk
  - 1 cup Milk powder
  - 2 teaspoons Milk masala mix
  - 12-15 Cashewnuts blanched for garnish Icing sugar for garnish Dried cranberries for garnish Pistachio powder

METHOD:
  1. Put milk, fresh cream, condensed milk and milk powder in a deep non-stick pan and mix till you get a smooth and lump free mixture.
  2. Place the pan on heat.
  3. Add milk masala and mix well.
  4. Allow the mixture to come to a boil, lower the heat and let the mixture reduce slightly.
  5. Add turmeric powder and mix well.
  6. Cook on low heat for 4-5 minutes, mixing constantly.
  7. Add sugar and mix well.
  8. Cook till the sugar dissolves completely.
  9. In a blender jar, add almonds, pistachios, cashewnuts and a little milk mixture.
  10. Switch off the heat.
  11. Blend the nuts to a fine paste, add it to the milk mixture and mix well.
  12. Strain the mixture into a bowl and refrigerate for 1 hour.
  13. Add the ice cream mixture into the cold ice cream churner bucket.
  14. Place it on the churner and start the machine.
  15. Let it churn for 20 minutes.
  16. Transfer the mixture into an air tight container and freeze it for 4-5 hours.
  17. To serve, keep a waffle cup on a serving plate, dust icing sugar all around it.Scoop out the ice cream into the waffle cup and sprinkle some dried cranberries, pistachio powder and garnish with mint sprig.
  18. Serve immediately.

RECIPE 217: Valacha Birda
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Valacha-Birda-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

A traditional Maharashtrian dish, it is often cooked on special occasion. Field beans cooked with Indian spices and served. This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Sprouted val, Cumin seeds | Cuisine: Maharashtrian | Course: Main | Prep Time: 4-5 hour | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1 cup sprouted val , soaked and peeled
  - 2 teaspoons cumin seeds
  - 2 medium onions , peeled
  - 3/4 cup scraped fresh coconut
  - 5-6 garlic cloves
  - 1/2 teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 2 teaspoons red chilli powder Salt to taste
  - 2 tablespoons oil
  - 1 teaspoon mustard seeds
  - 1 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 3 kokum petals
  - 1 tablespoon chopped jaggery Fresh coriander sprig to garnish

METHOD:
  1. Put cumin seeds, 1 quartered onion, coconut and sufficient water in a blender jar and blend well.
  2. Add garlic cloves and blend to a fine paste.
  3. Finely chop remaining onion and put it in a large bowl.
  4. Add val, turmeric powder, red chilli powder and salt and mix well.
  5. Add the ground paste and mix well.
  6. Heat oil in a deep non-stick pan, add mustard seeds, cumin seeds and asafoetida and let the seeds splutter and change colour.
  7. Add the val mixture and mix well.
  8. Add 2 cups water and mix well.
  9. Cover and cook for 6-8 minutes.
  10. Remove the lid and mix well.
  11. Add kokum petals and jaggery and mix well.
  12. Cook on medium heat for 12-15 minutes.
  13. Take it off the heat and rest for a few minutes.
  14. Transfer into a serving bowl, garnish with coriander sprig and serve hot.

RECIPE 218: Veg Chowmein
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Veg-Chowmein.html

This is the popular Indo-Chinese noodles stir fry dish made with mixed veggies and some sauces. Go ahead if you are looking for something savoury yet delicious This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Noodles, Button mushrooms | Cuisine: Indo- Chinese | Course: Noodles and Pastas | Prep Time: 21-25 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 3-4 babycorn , diagonally sliced and blanched
  - 1/4 cup mixed capsicum (red, green and yellow) diamonds
  - 1 medium onion , thickly sliced
  - 1 tablespoon sesame oil (til oil)
  - 2-3 spring onion bulbs , sliced Salt to taste
  - 1 teaspoon soy sauce
  - 1 tablespoon red chilli sauce
  - 1 teaspoon vinegar
  - 1 teaspoon toasted sesame seeds (til) , to garnish Diagonally sliced spring onion greens , for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat sesame oil in a non-stick pan, add garlic, ginger and spring onion bulbs, mix and sauté for 1 minute.
  2. Add mushrooms and babycorn, mix and sauté for 1 minute.
  3. Add salt and mix.
  4. Add mixed capsicums diamonds and onion, mix and sauté for 1 minute.
  5. Add noodles, soy sauce, red chilli sauce and salt, mix and cook for 2 minutes.
  6. Add vinegar and 1 teaspoon sesame seeds and mix well.
  7. Transfer onto a serving platter, garnish with spring onion greens and sesame seeds and serve hot.

RECIPE 219: Veg Club Sandwich
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Veg-Club-Sandwich-.html

Delight in layers of freshness and flavor with our Veg Club Sandwich, packed with crisp veggies and zesty spreads, perfect for a satisfying bite on-the-go. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Triangular bread slices, Cabbage | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 12 white bread slices
  - 2 cups shredded cabbage
  - 2 medium carrots, peeled and cut into strips
  - 2 medium green capsicums, cut into strips
  - 3 tablespoons mayonnaise Crushed black peppercorns to taste Salt to taste
  - 1 tablespoon mixed herbs
  - 6 tablespoons oil
  - 600 grams cottage cheese (paneer), cut into squares Butter as required Ice berg lettuce leaves as required Mustard sauce as required Tomato slices as required Tomato ketchup to serve Potato chips to serve

METHOD:
  1. Place the bread slices in a toaster and toast till done.
  2. Remove and set aside.
  3. In a bowl, add cabbage, carrots, capsicum, and mayonnaise.
  4. Mix well and set aside.
  5. In another bowl, add crushed black peppercorns, salt and 4 tablespoons oil, mix well.
  6. Add the paneer pieces in it and apply the prepared mix on them.
  7. Heat remaining oil in a non-stick grill, place the paneer pieces and grill till done on both side.
  8. Keep aside.
  9. Apply butter on one side of the bread slices, place a few lettuce leaves, add prepared vegetable mixture and sprinkle some crushed black peppercorns and salt.
  10. Place another slice of bread and apply mustard sauce, arrange the paneer pieces, add tomato slices, sprinkle crushed black peppercorns, salt and top it with a few lettuce leaves.
  11. Place the third slice of bread and secure the sandwich with the help of toothpicks and cut into half.
  12. Serve immediately along with tomato ketchup and potato chips.

RECIPE 220: Veg Mughlai Parantha
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Veg-Mughlai-Parantha---skk.html

Experience the royal flavors of Mughlai cuisine in every bite of our Veg Mughlai Parantha, filled with rich, aromatic spices and delectable vegetarian fillings. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Refined flour, Salt | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 21-25 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1½ cups refined flour + dusting Salt to taste
  - 3 tablespoons oil
  - 1 tablespoon chopped garlic
  - 1 tablespoon chopped ginger ½ tablespoon chopped green chillies
  - 1 medium onion, finely chopped
  - 1 small capsicum, finely chopped
  - 1 small carrot, peeled and grated
  - 1 teaspoon red chilli powder ½ teaspoon turmeric powder
  - 1 teaspoon coriander powder
  - 1 teaspoon ghee + for applying
  - 250 grams cottage cheese (paneer), grated Tomato ketchup to serve

METHOD:
  1. In a bowl, add flour, salt and sufficient water, knead to soft dough.
  2. Drizzle 1 tablespoon oil and knead again.
  3. Cover with a damp muslin cloth and set aside for 10-15 minutes.
  4. Meanwhile, heat remaining oil in a non-stick pan; add garlic, ginger, and mix well.
  5. Add green chillies and onion, cook till translucent.
  6. Add capsicum, carrots and mix well.
  7. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  8. Add red chilli powder, turmeric powder, coriander powder and mix well.
  9. Cook for 1 minute.
  10. Add 1 teaspoon ghee and cottage cheese, mix well.
  11. Add salt and mix well.
  12. Divide the prepared dough into equal portions and shape them into balls.
  13. Dust flour on the worktop, and roll out a portion of the dough into a disc of medium thickness.
  14. Place a portion of the prepared stuffing and bring the sides to the centre and flip it.
  15. Roll out into a square parantha.
  16. Heat a non-stick pan; place the prepared parantha on it.
  17. Cook till both sides are done.
  18. Apply ghee on both sides and cut into pieces.
  19. Serve hot along with tomato ketchup.


========================================================================
RECIPE 221: Vegetable Makhani
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Vegetable-Makhani-Sanjeev-Kapoor-Kitchen-FoodFood.html

An extremely popular dish, Vegetable Makhani is made with the classic rich and creamy gravy. Served with any Indian bread, this dish is finger-licking good This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Baby potatoes, Cottage cheese (paneer) | Cuisine: Punjabi | Course: Main | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 26-30 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Spicy | Level of Cooking: Moderate | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 250 grams baby potatoes , boiled and peeled
  - 10 fresh button mushrooms , halved
  - 15-20 small Broccoli florets , blanced
  - 2 inches ginger , roughly chopped
  - 10-15 garlic cloves
  - 5 green cardamoms A few maceblades
  - 2 teaspoons red chilli powder (deghi mirch powder)
  - 1/2 teaspoon crushed red chillies A few fresh coriander stems
  - 4 tablespoons oil
  - 1/2 teaspoon cumin seeds
  - 1/2 teaspoon garam masala powder
  - 1 teaspoon dried fenugreek leaves (kasuri methi) , roasted and powdered
  - 2 tablespoons honey
  - 1 tablespoon butter
  - 2 tablespoons fresh cream Ginger , cut into thin strips for garnish

METHOD:
  1. Heat a deep non-stick pan, add tomatoes, salt, ginger, garlic, green cardamoms, mace blades, red chilli powder, crushed red chillies and 3 cups water and mix.
  2. Add fresh coriander stems, cover and cook.
  3. Heat 2 tbsps oil in a non-stick wok, add baby potatoes and salt and let them cook till light golden.
  4. Cut cottage cheese into medium cubes and put them in a bowl.
  5. Add the baby potatoes.
  6. Add button mushrooms to the same wok and toss till they soften.
  7. Transfer them into same bowl.
  8. The tomatoes are fully done.
  9. Strain the liquid into a bowl.
  10. Transfer the tomatoes into a mixer jar, cool and grind into a smooth puree.
  11. Heat 2 tbsps oil in the same wok, add cumin seeds and let them change colour.
  12. Add the strained liquid and cook till it is reduced.
  13. Strained the tomato puree into the wok, pressing the residue in the strainer to extract all the flavours.
  14. Mix well.
  15. Add the vegetables and cottage cheese and mix.
  16. Add garam masala powder and dried fenugreek leaf powder and mix well.
  17. Cook till the gravy thickens.
  18. Add honey and mix well.
  19. Take the broccoli florets in a serving and heat in the microwave.
  20. Add butter and fresh cream to the wok and mix well.
  21. Pour this over the broccoli.
  22. Garnish with a few more broccoli florets and ginger strips and serve hot.

RECIPE 222: Veggie Burger
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Veggie-Burger-.html

Sink your teeth into a symphony of flavors with our Veggie Burger, featuring a hearty patty made from wholesome vegetables, nestled in a soft bun, and topped with fresh, crunchy veggies. This is a Sanjeev Kapoor exclusive recipe.

Main Ingredients: Green peas, French beans | Cuisine: Fusion | Course: Snacks and Starters | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 11-15 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Mild | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1-2 French beans, roughly chopped and blanched
  - 1 small carrot, roughly chopped and blanched ⅓ cup blanched corn kernels ½ small cauliflower, roughly chopped and blanched
  - 1 burger bun
  - 1 green chilli
  - 2 white bread slices Breadcrumbs for coating Oil for deep-frying Butter for applying
  - 1-2 tablespoons mayonnaise
  - 2 tomato slices + for serving

METHOD:
  1. Mix together green peas, French beans, carrots, corn kernels and cauliflower in a chopper and finely chop the vegetables.
  2. Add green chilli, garlic cloves and ginger and finely chop.
  3. Transfer to a bowl.
  4. Grate in potatoes, add salt and pepper powder and mix well.
  5. Crumble bread slices, add to the bowl and mix well.
  6. Shape the mixture into a patty and coat with breadcrumbs.
  7. Heat sufficient oil in a kadai.
  8. Deep-fry the patty till golden brown and crisp.
  9. Drain on absorbent paper.
  10. Slice burger bun horizontally.
  11. Heat a non-stick tawa, place the slices on it and toast till crisp.
  12. Apply some butter to the slices and toast for a few more seconds.
  13. Remove from heat and set aside.
  14. To make chutney mayonnaise, mix together mayonnaise and green chutney in a bowl.
  15. Place a cheese slice on the base half of the bun and top with some lettuce.
  16. Slice an onion and sprinkle salt over the slices.
  17. Place them on the lettuce, top with chutney mayonnaise, patty, tomato slices, some more chutney mayonnaise and cover with the top half of the bun.
  18. Serve immediately with crisps, tomato slices and lettuce leaves.


========================================================================
RECIPE 223: Walnut Phirni in Chocolate Cups
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Walnut-Phirni-in-Chocolate-Cups-Mummy-Ka-Magic-FoodFood.html

Chocolate and walnuts make a great combination, and when walnut phirni is served in chocolate cups it is divine This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: Walnuts, Dark chocolate | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Mithais | Prep Time: 31-40 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 cup Walnuts
  - 1 litres Full fat milk
  - 30 minutes and drained
  - 3/4 cup Sugar
  - 1/4 teaspoon Green cardamom powder a few strands Saffron to garnish Chocolate cigars to garnish Fresh mint sprigs

METHOD:
  1. To prepare chocolate cups, fill silicon moulds till ¾ full with melted dark chocolate.
  2. Swirl to coat all sides and drain extra chocolate.
  3. Keep them in the refrigerator for 5-10 minutes or till set.
  4. Put walnuts in a grinder jar and grind coarsely.
  5. Boil milk in a deep non-stick pan.
  6. Transfer walnuts into a bowl.
  7. Put drained rice in the same grind jar and grind coarsely.
  8. Add both rice and walnuts to the boiling milk and cook, stirring continuously till the rice gets cooked and the mixture thickens.
  9. Scrape the sides occasionally and mix well.
  10. Stir continuously so that no lumps are formed.
  11. Add sugar, green cardamom powder and saffron strands, mix and cook for 2-3 minutes on low heat.
  12. Remove from heat and let it cool down to room temperature.
  13. Demould chocolate cups from the silicon moulds and place on a serving platter.
  14. Fill up each chocolate cups with phirni.
  15. Garnish with chocolate cigars and mint sprig.
  16. Serve immediately.


========================================================================
RECIPE 224: Zarda Boondi Biryani
========================================================================
URL: https://www.sanjeevkapoor.com/Recipe/Zarda-Boondi-Biryani-Turban-Tadka-FoodFood.html

Sweet biryani made with sweet boondi, basmati rice and plenty of nuts This recipe is from FoodFood TV channel

Main Ingredients: saffron strands, Sweet boondi | Cuisine: Indian | Course: Rice | Prep Time: 26-30 minutes | Cook Time: 16-20 minutes | Serve: 4 | Taste: Sweet | Level of Cooking: Easy | Diet: Veg

INGREDIENTS:
  - 1/2 grams saffron strands
  - 1 cup Sweet boondi
  - 3 cups Basmati rice , cooked
  - 2 tablespoons Ghee
  - 2 tablespoons Chironjee / charoli
  - 2-3 tablespoons Cashewnuts , chopped
  - 1/2 cup Milk
  - 1/4 cup Castor sugar
  - 15-20 Walnuts
  - 1/2 Lemon to garnish Orange to garnish Rabdi

METHOD:
  1. Heat ghee in a deep stainless steel handi, add chironji, cashewnuts, raisins and dried coconut and sauté on medium heat for 1-2 minutes.
  2. Add milk, boondi, castor sugar, saffron and ½ tsp cinnamon powder, mix well and cook for 2-3 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  3. After the mixture comes to a boil, add walnuts and mix well.
  4. Cook for 1-2 minutes, add ¼ cup khoya, cooked basmati rice, mint leaves and remaining khoya.
  5. Squeeze lemon juice into the handi and add remaining cinnamon powder, mix, cover and cook for 4-5 minutes on low heat.
  6. Cut orange into round slices and halve them.
  7. Transfer the biryani onto a serving platter, garnish with rabdi, orange slices and a mint sprig and serve.
